 skandhā dhātava āyatanāni ca kati skandhāḥ pañca rūpa skandhaḥ  vedanā skandhaḥ saṃjñā skandhaḥ saṃskāra skandhaḥ  vijñāna skandhaḥ ca dhātavaḥ  aṣṭādaśa cakṣuḥ dhātū rūpa dhātuḥ cakṣuḥ vijñāna dhātuḥ śrotra dhātuḥ śabda dhātuḥ śrotra vijñāna dhātuḥ ghrāṇa dhātuḥ gandha dhātuḥ ghrāṇa vijñāna dhātuḥ jivhādhātū rasa dhātuḥ jivhā vijñāna dhātuḥ kāyadhātuḥ spraṣṭavya dhātuḥ kāya vijñāna dhātuḥ manaḥ dhātuḥ dharmadhātuḥ manaḥ vijñāna dhātuḥ ca āyatanāni dvadaśa cakṣuḥ āyatanam rūpa āyatanam śrotra āyatanam śabda āyatanam ghrāṇa āyatanam gandha āyatanam jivhā āyatanam rasa āyatanam kāya āyatanam spraṣṭavya āyatanam manaā āyatanam dharma āyatanam ca kim upādāya skandhāḥ pañca eva paṃcākāra ātma vastu udbhāvana tām upādāya sa parigraha deha ātma vastu upabhoga ātma vastu abhilāpa ātma vastu sarva dharma adharma abhisaṃskāra ātma vastu tad āśraya ātma svastu ca upādāya kim upādāya dhātovaḥ  aṣṭādaśa eva dvābhyām deha parigrahābhyām atīta varttamāna ṣaḍa ākāra upabhoga dhāraṇa tām upādāya kim upādāya āyatanāni dvādaśā eva dvābhyām deha parigrahābhyām anāgata ṣaḍa ākāra upabhogāya dvāra tām upādāya kasmāt  skandhā upādānam iti ucyante upādānena sahita tvāt  skandhā upādānam i tyucyante upādānam katamat  skandheṣu cchandaḥ rāgaḥ ca kasmāt  ḥcchandaḥ  rāgaḥ ca upādānam iti ucyate anāgata varttamāna skandhānām abhinirvarttanataḥ  aparihārataḥ ca anāgate abhilāṣāt  varttamāne adhāvasānāt ca cchandaḥ rāgaḥ ca upādānam iti ucyate kasmāt  dhātava āyatanāni ca sa upādāna dharmā iti ucyante tatra skandhavat nirddeśaḥ kiṃlakṣaṇam rūpam rūpaṇa lakṣaṇam rūpam tad  dvividham sparśena rūpaṇam pradeśena rūpaṇam ca sparśena rūpaṇam katamat  kara caraṇa pāṣāṇa śasra daṇḍa śīta uṣṇa kṣudh pipāsā maśaka daṃśa sarpa vṛścika ādīnām sparśena vyābādhanam pradeśena rūpaṇam katamat  deśena rūpaṇa midam ca idam ca rūpam evam ca evam ca rūpam iti praṇihita apraṇihita cetaḥ vitarkeṇa pratibimba citrīkāra tā kiṃlakṣaṇā vedanā anubhava lakṣaṇā vedanā nānāvidhānām śubha śubhānām karmaṇām phala vipākam pratyanubhavanti anena iti anubhavaḥ kiṃlakṣaṇā saṃjñā saṃjānanā lakṣaṇā saṃjñā saṃjñā nānā dharma pratibimba udgrahaṇa svabhāvā yayā draṣṭa śruta mata vijñātān arthān vyavaharati kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ saṃskāraḥ abhisaṃskāra lakṣaṇaḥ saṃskāraḥ saṃskāra bhisaṃskāra svabhāvaḥ  yena kuśala akuśalāvya kṛteṣu pakṣeṣu cittam prerayati kiṃlakṣaṇam vijñānam vijānanā lakṣaṇam vijñānam vijñānam yena rūpa śabda gandha rasa sparśa dharmān nānā viṣayān vijānāti cakṣuḥ dhātuḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ yena cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi dṛṣṭavān paśyati yad ca tasya bījam upacitam ālaya vijñānam tad cakṣuḥ yathā cakṣuḥ dhātu lakṣaṇam tathā śrotra ghrāṇa jihya kāya manaḥ dhātūnām api lakṣaṇāni rūpa dhātuḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ rūpam yad cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭam dṛśyate ca yad ca tatra cakṣuḥ dhātoḥ ādhipatyam tad rūpa dhātu lakṣaṇam yathā rūpa dhātu lakṣaṇam tathā śabda gandha rasa sparśa dharma dhātūnām api lakṣaṇāni cakṣūḥ vijñāna dhātuḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ cakṣuḥ āśrayā rūpa ālambanā rūpa prativijñaptiḥ yad ca tasya bījam upacitam vipāka ālaya vijñānam tad cakṣuḥ vijñāna dhātu lakṣaṇam yathā cakṣuḥ vijñāna dhātu lakṣaṇam tathā śrotra ghrāṇa jivhā kāya manaḥ vijñāna dhātūnām api lakṣaṇāni āyatanam kiṃlakṣaṇam dhātuvat  yathāyogam veditavyam rūpa skandha vyavasthānam katamat  yad kiṃcid rūpam sarvam tad catvāri mahābhūtāni catvāri ca mahābhūtāni upādāya katamāni catvāri mahābhūtāni pṛthivī dhātuḥ abdhātuḥ tejaḥ dhātuḥ vāyudhātuḥ ca pṛthivī dhātuḥ katamaḥ kaṭhina tā abdhātuḥ katamaḥ niṣyandatā tejaḥ dhātuḥ katamaḥ uṣṇa tā vāyudhātuḥ katamaḥ kampanatā upādāya rūpam katamat  cakṣuḥ indriyam śrotra indriyam ghrāṇa indriyam jivha indriyam kāya indriyam rūpa śabda gandha rasa spraṣṭavyānām eka deśaḥ  dharma āyatana saṃgṛhītam ca rūpam cakṣuḥ indriyam katamat  catvāri mahābhūtāni upādāya cakṣu vijñānā śrayaḥ rūpa prasādaḥ śrotra indriyam katamat  catvāri mahābhūtāni upādāya śrotra vijñāna āśrayaḥ  rūpa prasādaḥ ghrāṇa indriyam katamat  catvāri mahābhūtāni upādāya ghrāṇa vijñāna āśrayaḥ  rūpa prasādaḥ jivha indriyam katamat  catvāri maha bhūtāni upādāya jivhā vijñāna śrayaḥ  rūpa prasādaḥ kāya indriyam katamat  catvāri mahābhūtāni upādāya kāya vijñāna āśrayaḥ  rūpa prasādaḥ rūpam katamat  catvāri mahābhūtāni upādāya cakṣuḥ indriya gocaraḥ  arthaḥ yathā nīlam pītam lohitam avadātam dīrgham hrasvam vṛttam parimaṇḍalam sthūlam sūkṣmam unnatam avanatam sātam visātam ātapaḥ chāyā ālokaḥ  adhakāram abhram dhūmaḥ  rajaḥ  mahikā ca abhyavakāśa rūpam vijñapti rūpam nabha eka varṇam rūpam tad  punar tridhā śobhanam aśobhanam ubhaya viparītam ca śabdaḥ katamaḥ catvāri mahābhūtāni upādāya śrotra indriya brāhyaḥ  arthaḥ manojñaḥ  vā amanojñaḥ  vā ubhaya viparītaḥ  vā upātta mahābhūta hetu kaḥ vā anupātta mahābhūta hetu kaḥ vā tad ubhayaḥ  bāloka prasiddhaḥ  vā siddha upanītaḥ  vā parikalpitaḥ  vā āryaiḥ deśitaḥ  vā tīrtha et aśitaḥ  vā gandhaḥ katamaḥ catvāri mahābhūtāni upādāya ghrāṇa indriya grāhyaḥ  arthaḥ yathā surabhiḥ asurabhiḥ sama gandhaḥ sahaja gandhaḥ sāṃyogika gandhaḥ pāriṇāmika gandhaḥ ca rasaḥ katama catvāri mahābhūtāmi upādāya jivha indriya brāhyaḥ  arthaḥ tiktaḥ  amlaḥ  madhuraḥ kaṭukaḥ  lavaṇaḥ kaṣāyaḥ ca manojñaḥ  vā amanojñaḥ  vā ubhaya viparītaḥ  vā sahajaḥ  vā sāṃyogikaḥ  vā pāriṇāmikaḥ  vā spraṣṭavya eka deśaḥ katamaḥ catvāri mahābhūtāni upādāya kāya indriya grāhyaḥ  arthaḥ ślakṣṇa tvam karkaśa tvam laghu tvam gurū tvam picchila tvam manda tvam amanda tvam śīta tvam uṣṇa tvam jighatsā pipāsā tṛptiḥ balam daurbalayam mūrcchā kaṇḍūtiḥ pūtiḥ vyādhiḥ jarā maraṇam klāntiḥ viśrāma ūrjā ca dharma āyatana saṃgṛhītam rūpam katamat  pañcavidham ābhisaṃkṣepi kam ābhyavakā śiṃkam sāma ādānikam parikalpitam vaibhu tvikam ca vedanā skandha vyavasthānam katamat  ṣaṣ vedanā kāyāḥ cakṣuḥ saṃsparśa jā vedanā śrotra ghrāṇa jivhākā yamanaḥ saṃsparśa jā vedanā evam ṣaṣ vedanā kāyāḥ sukhā vā duḥkhā aduḥkha asukhā vā punar  sukhā kāyikī vedanā duḥkhā kāyikī vedanā aduḥkha asukhā kāyikī vedanā sukhā caitasikī vedanā duḥkhā caitasikī vedanā aduḥkha asukhā caitasikī vedanā sukhā sa āmiṣa vedanā duḥkhā sa āmiṣa vedanā aduḥkha asukhā sa āmiṣa vedanā sukhā nirāmiṣa vedanā duḥkhā nirāmiṣa vedanā aduḥkha asukhā nirāmiṣa vedanā punar  sukhā gredha āśrita vedanā duḥkhā gredha āśrita vedanā aduḥkha asukhā gredha āśrita vedanā sukhā naiṣkramya āśrita vedanā duḥkhā naiṣkramya āśrita vedanā aduḥkha asukhā naiṣkramya annita vedanā ca kāyikī vedanā katamā paṃca vijñāna saṃprayuktā vedanā caitasikī vedanā katamā manaḥ vijñāna saṃprayuktā vedanā sa āmiṣa vedanā katamā ātma bhāva tṛṣṇā saṃprayuktā vedanā nirāmiṣa vedanā katamā tad tṛṣṇā viprayuktā vedanā gredha āśrita vedanā katamā paṃca kāma guṇa tṛṣṇā saṃprayuktā vedanā naiṣkramya āśrita vedanā katamā tad tṛṣṇā viprayuktā vedanā saṃjñā skandha vyavasthānam katamat  ṣaḍ  saṃjñā kāyāḥ cakṣuḥ saṃsparśa jā saṃjñā śrotra ghrāṇa jivhā kāya manaḥ saṃsparśa jā saṃjñā yathā sa nimittam pi saṃjānāti animittam api parīttam api mahat gata mapi apramāṇam api na asti kiṃcid iti ākiṃcanya āyatanam api saṃjānāti sa nimitta saṃjñā katamā avyavahāra kuśalasya animitta dhātu samā pannasya bhava agra samāpannasya ca saṃjñām sthāpayitvā yāvat anyā saṃjñā animitta saṃjñā katamā yā sthāpitā saṃjñā parīttā saṃjñā katamā yayā kāmadhātum saṃjānāti mahagdatā saṃjñā katamā yayā rūpa dhātum saṃjānāti apramāṇa saṃjñā katamā yayā ākāśāna nti āyatanam vijñāna ānanti āyatanam saṃjānāti akiñcana saṃjñā katamā yayā ākiñcani āyatanam saṃjānāti saṃskāra skandha vyavasthānam katamat  ṣaḍ  cetanā kāyāḥ cakṣuḥ saṃsparśa jā cetanā śrotra ghrāṇa jvihā kāya manaḥ saṃsparśa jā cetanā yayā kuśala tvāya cetayate saṃkleśāya cetayate avasthā bhedāya cetayate iti iyam cetanā vedanām saṃjñāt ca sthāpayitvā tad anye caitasikā dharmāḥ citta viprayuktāḥ ca saṃskārāḥ saṃskāra skandha iti ucyate te punar  katame manaskāraḥ sparśaḥ cchandaḥ adhimokṣaḥ smṛtiḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śraddhā hīra patrāpyam ālobhaḥ  adveṣaḥ  amohoḥ vīryam praśrabdhiḥ apramāda upekṣā apristhitā rāgaḥ pratighaḥ  mānaḥ  avidyā vicikitsā sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ antara grāha dṛṣṭiḥ dṛṣṭi parāmarśaḥ śīla vṛta parāmarśaḥ mithyā dṛṣṭi krodha upanāhaḥ mrakṣaḥ pradāśaḥ īrṣyāḥ mātsaryam śāṭhyam madaḥ  vihinsā āhrikyam anapatrāpyam styānam auddhatyam āśraddhyam kausīdyam pramādaḥ  muṣita smṛtitā saṃprajanyam vikṣepaḥ  middham kaukṛtyam vitarkaḥ  vicāraḥ ca cetanā katamā citta abhisaṃskāraḥ  manaskarma kuśala akuśala avyākṛteṣu citta preraṇa karmikā manaskāraḥ katamaḥ cetasa ābhogaḥ ālambana citta dhāraṇa karmakaḥ sparśaḥ katamaḥ trika sakṣipāte indriya vipāra paricchedaḥ vedanā sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ cchandaḥ katamaḥ īpsite vastuni tad tad upasaṃhatā karttṛ kāma tā vīrya ādāna sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ adhimokṣaḥ katamaḥ niścite vastuni yathā niścayam dhāraṇā asaṃhāryatā karmakaḥ smṛti katamā saṃsṛte vastuni cetasaḥ asaṃpramoṣaḥ  avikṣepa karmikā samādhiḥ katamaḥ upaparīkṣye vastuni vittasya ekāgra tā jñāna sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ prajñā katamā upaparīkṣya eva vastuni dharmāṇām pravicayaḥ saṃśaya vyāvarttana karmikā śraddhā katamā astitva guṇavattva śakta tveṣu abhisaṃpratyayaḥ prasādaḥ  abhilāpaḥ cchanda sakṣi śraya dāna karmikā hrīḥ katamā svayam avadyena lajjanā duścarita saṃyama sanniśraya dāna karmikā apatrāpyam katamat  paratas  avadyena lajjanā tad karmakam eva alobhaḥ katamaḥ bhave bhava upakaraṇeṣu vā anāsaktiḥ duścarita apravṛtti sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ adveṣaḥ katamaḥ sattveṣu duḥkhe duḥkha sthānīyeṣu ca dharme ṣu anāghātaḥ duścarita apravṛtti sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ amohaḥ katamaḥ vipākataḥ  vā āgamataḥ  vā adhigamataḥ  vā jñānam pratisaṃkhyā duścarita apravṛtti sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ vīryam katamat  kuśale cetasaḥ  abhyutsāhaḥ sannāhe vā prayoge vā alīna tve vā avyāvṛttau vā asantuṣṭau vā kuśala pakṣa paripūraṇa pariniṣpādana karmakam aśrabdhiḥ katamā kāya citta dauṣṭhulyānām pratipraśrabdheḥ kāya citta karmaṇya tā sarva āvaraṇa niṣkarṣaṇa karmikā amra mādaḥ katamaḥ sa vīrya kāna lobhāt veṣā mohat niśritya yā kuśalānām dharmāṇām bhāvanā sa āsravebhyaḥ ca dharmebhyaḥ cittā rakṣā sa ca laukika lokottara sampatti paripūraṇa pariniṣpādana karmakaḥ upekṣā katamā sa vīrya kāna lobhāt veṣā mohāt niśritya yā saṃkliṣṭa vihāra vairodhikī citta sama tā citta praśaṭha tā cittasya anābhoga avasthita tā saṃkleśa anavakāśa sanniśraya dāna karmikā avihin sā katamā adveṣām śikā karūṇa tā aviheṭhana karmikā rāgaḥ katamaḥ traidhātukaḥ  anunayaḥ duḥkha saṃjanana karmakaḥ pratighaḥ katamaḥ sattveṣu duḥkhe duḥkha sthānīyeṣu ca dharmeṣu āghātaḥ asparśa vihāra duścarita sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ mānaḥ katamaḥ sat kāya dṛṣṭi sanniśrayeṇa cittasya unnatiḥ agaurava duḥkha utpatti sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ avidyā katamā traidhātukam ajñānam dharmeṣu mithyā niścaya vicikitsāt saṃkleśa utpatti sanniśraya dāna karmikā bicikitsā katamā satyeṣu vimatiḥ kuśala pakṣā pravṛtti sanniśraya dāna karmikā sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ katamā pañca upādāna skandhān ātmataḥ ātmīyataḥ  vā samanupaśyataḥ  yā kṣāntī rūciḥ matiḥ prekṣā dṛṣṭiḥ sarva dṛṣṭi gata sanniśraya dāna karmikā anta grāha dṛṣṭiḥ katamā pañca upādāna skandhān śāśva ta taḥ vā ucchedataḥ  vā samanupaśyataḥ yā kṣāntī ruciḥ matiḥ prekṣā dṛṣṭiḥ madhyamā pratipad niryāṇa paripantha karmikā dṛṣṭi parāmarśaḥ katamaḥ dṛṣṭim dṛṣṭayā āśrayān  ca pañca upādāna skandhān agrataḥ śreṣṭhataḥ viśiṣṭataḥ paramatas ca samanupaśyataḥ  yā kṣānti ruciḥ matiḥ prekṣā dṛṣṭi asa dṛṣṭi ami niveśa sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ śīlavata parām arthaḥ katamaḥ śīlam vratam śīla vratā śrayām śca pañca upādāna skandhān śuddhitaḥ  mukti taḥ  nairyāṇikataḥ ca samanupaśyataḥ  yā kṣāntī rūciḥ matiḥ prekṣā dṛṣṭiḥ śrama vaiphalya sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ mithyādṛṣṭiḥ katamā hetum vā apavadataḥ phalam vā kriyām vā sadvā vastu nāśayataḥ mithyā ca vikalpayataḥ  yā kṣānti ruciḥ matiḥ prekṣā dṛṣṭiḥ kuśala mūla samuccheda karmikā akuśala mūla dṛḍha tā sanniśraya dāna karmikā akuśale pravṛtti karmikā kuśa leca apravṛtti karmikā vā yā etāḥ pañca dṛṣṭayaḥ āsām kati samāropa dṛṣṭayaḥ kati apavāddṛṣṭayaḥ catasraḥ samāropa dṛṣṭayaḥ jñeye svabhāva viśeṣa samāropa tām upādāya dṛṣṭau ca agra śuddhi samāropa tām upādāya ekā yad bhūyasā apavāda dṛṣṭiḥ yāḥ ca purvānta kalpikā dṛṣṭayaḥ yāḥ ca parānta kalpikā dṛṣṭayaḥ tāḥ katibhyaḥ  dṛṣṭibhyaḥ  veditavyāḥ dvābhyām sarvābhyaḥ  vā yā avyākṛta castuṣu dṛṣṭayaḥ tāḥ katibhyaḥ  dṛṣṭibhyaḥ  veditavyāḥ dvābhyām sarvābhyaḥ  vā kam doṣam paśyatā bhagavatā skandha dhātu āyatanegu pañcamiḥ kāraṇaiḥ ātmā pratikṣiptaḥ sat kāya dṛṣṭi parigṛhītān pañca doṣān paśyatā vilakṣaṇa tā doṣam anitya tā doṣam asvāsthya doṣam nirdeha tā doṣam ayatnataḥ mokṣa doṣam ca yā pañca su upādāna skadheṣu viṃśati koṭikā sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ rūpa[mā]tma iti samanupaśyati rūpavantam ātmānam ātmīyam rūpam rūpe ātmānam vedanām saṃjñām saṃskārān vijñānam ātmā iti samanupaśyati vijñānavantam ātmānam ātmīyam vijñānam vijñāne ātmānam tatra kati ātma dṛṣṭayaḥ kati ātmīya dṛṣṭayaḥ pañca ātma dṛṣṭayaḥ pañcadaśa ātmīya dṛṣṭayaḥ kena kāraṇena pañca [da śā]tmīya dṛṣṭayaḥ sambandha ātmīyatām upādāya vaśa varttana ātmīya tām upādāya avinirbhoga vṛtti ātmīyatām ca upādāya sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ nirūpita vastukā vaktavyā anirupita vastukā vaktavyā anirūpita vastu kā vaktavyā rajjvām sarpa buddhivat  krodhaḥ katamaḥ pratyupasthite apakāra nimitte prati[ghāṃ] śikaḥ cetasa āghātaḥ śastra ādānam daṇḍa ādāna ādi saṃrambha sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ upanohaḥ katamaḥ tatas  ūrdhvam pratighāṃśika eva vaira āśayasya anutsargaḥ akṣānti sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ makṣaḥ katamaḥ samyak  coditasya moha aṃśikā avadya pracchādanā kaukṛtya asparśa vihāra sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ mad āśaḥ katamaḥ pratighāṃśikaḥ krodha upanāha pūrvaṅgamaḥ cetasa āghātaḥ ucca pragāḍha pāruṣya vacana sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ apuṇya prasava karmakaḥ asparśa vihāra karmakaḥ ca īrṣyā katamā lābha satkārā dhyavasitasya para saṃpatti viśeṣe dveṣa aṃśikaḥ a[marṣa] kṛtaḥ cetasaḥ  vyāropaḥ daurmanasya asparśa vihāra karmakaḥ mātsaryam katamat  lābha satkāra adhyavasitasya pariṣkāreṣu rāga aṃśiḥ cetasa āgrahaḥ asaṃlekha sanniśraya dāna karmakam māyā katamā lābha satkāra adhyavasitasya rāgamoha aṃśikā abhūta guṇa saṃdarśanā mithyājīva sanniśraya dāna karmikā śāṭhyam ka[tamat] lābha satkāra adhyavasitasya rāgamoha aṃśikā bhūta doṣa vimālanā samyak avavāda lābha paripantha karam madaḥ katamaḥ ārogyam vā āgamya yauvanam vā dīrgha āyuṣka lakṣaṇam vā upalabhyanyatama anyatamām vā sa āsravān saṃpattim rāga aṃśi kannandī saumanasyam sarvva kleśa upakleśa sanniśraya dāna karmakaḥ vihinsā katamā prati[ghā aṃśi]kā nirvṛṇa tā niṣkaraṇa tā nirdayatā viheṭhana karmikā āhrīkyam katamat  rāga dveṣa moha aṃśikā svayam avadyena alat janā sarvva kleśa upakleśa sāhāyya karmakam auddhatya katamat  śubha nimittam anusarataḥ  rāga aṃśikaḥ cetasaḥ  avyupaśamaḥ śamatha paripantha karmakam āśradudhvaṃ katamat  moha aṃśikaḥ kuśaleṣu dharmeṣu cetasaḥ  anabhisaṃpratyayaḥ  aprasādaḥ  anabhilāṣaḥ kausīdya sanniśraya dāna karmakam kausīdyam katamat  nidrā pārśva śayana sukhallikām āgamya moha aṃśikaḥ cetasaḥ  anabhyutsāhaḥ kuśala pakṣa prayoga paripantha karmakam pramodaḥ katamaḥ sa kausīdyān rāga dveṣa mohāt niśritya kuśalānām dharmāṇām abhāvanā sa āsravebhyaḥ ca dharmebhyaḥ cetasaḥ  anārakṣā akuśala vṛddhi kuśala parihāṇi sanniśraya dāna sanniśraya dāna karmakam vikṣepaḥ katamaḥ rāga dveṣa moha aṃśikaḥ cetasaḥ  visāraḥ sa punar  svabhāva vikṣepaḥ bahirdhāvikṣepaḥ adhyātma vikṣepaḥ nimi tta vikṣepaḥ dauṣṭhulya vikṣepaḥ manasikāra auddhatyāsvādanā nimitta vikṣepa katamaḥ para saṃbhāvanām puraskṛtya kuśala prayogaḥ hauṣṭhulya vikṣepaḥ katamaḥ ahaṃkāra mamakāra asmi mānapakṣyam dauṣṭhulyam āganya kuśala prayuktasya utpanna utpanneṣu vediteṣu aham iti vā mama iti vā asmi iti vā udgrahaḥ  vyavakiraṇā nimittīkāraḥ manasikāra vikṣepaḥ katamaḥ sama patti antaram vā yāna antaram vā samāpadyamānasya saṃśrayataḥ  vā yaḥ  visāraḥ vairāgya pari pantha karmakaḥ middham katamat  middha nimittam āgamya moha aṃśikaḥ cetasaḥ  abhisaṃkṣepaḥ kuśalaḥ akuśalaḥ avyākṛtaḥ kāle vā akāle vā yuktaḥ  vā ayuktaḥ  vā kṛtyā vipatti ca cittasya sūkṣma tā sparśa asparśa vihāra saṃniśraya dāna karmakau api khalu kuśalānām dharmāṇām sva vipakṣa prahāṇam karma kleśa upakleśānām sva pratipakṣa paripanthanam karma 0 citta viprayuktāḥ saṃskārāḥ katame prāptiḥ asaṃjñi samāpatti nirodha samāpattiḥ āsaṃjñikam jīvita indriyam nikāya sabhā gatā jātiḥ jarā sthitiḥ anitya tā nāmakāyāḥ padakāyāḥ vyañjana kāyāḥ pṛthagjana tvam pravṛttiḥ pratiniyamaḥ  yogaḥ javaḥ anukramaḥ kālaḥ  deśaḥ saṃkhyā sāmagrī ca prāptiḥ katamā kuśala kuśalāṃnām dharmāṇām ācaya apacaye prāptiḥ pratilagbhaḥ samanvāgama iti prajñaptiḥ asaṃjñi samāpattiḥ katamā śubha kṛtsna vīta rāgasya upari avīta rāgasya niḥsaraṇa saṃjñā pūrvakeṇa manasikāreṇa āsthāvarāṇām citta caitasikānām dharmāṇām nirodhe asaṃjñi samāpattiḥ iti prajñaptiḥ nirodha samāpattiḥ katamā ākiṃcanya āyatana vīta rāgasya bhava agrāt uccalitasya śānta vihāra saṃjñā pūrvakeṇa manasikāreṇa āsthāvarāṇām citta caitasikānām dharmāṇām nirodhe nirodha samāpattiḥ iti prajñaptiḥ āsaṃjñikam katamat  asaṃjñisattva iṣu deveṣu upapannasya āsthāvarāṇām citta caitasikānām dharmāṇām nirodhe āsaṃjñika priti prajñaptiḥ jīvita indriyam katamat  nikāya sa bhāge pūrva karma āviddhe sthiti kāla niyame āyuḥ iti prajñaptiḥ nikāya sa bhāgaḥ katamaḥ teṣām teṣām sattvānām tasmin stasmin sattva nikāye ātma bhāva sadṛśa tāyām nikāya sa bhāga iti prajñaptiḥ jātiḥ katamā nikāya sa bhāge saṃskārāṇām abhūtvā abhāve jātiḥ iti prajñaptiḥ jarā katamā nikāyasa bhāme saṃskārāṇām prabandhān i athātve jarā iti prajñaptiḥ sthitiḥ katamā nikāya sa bhāge prabandha avipraṇāśe sthitiḥ iti prajñaptiḥ anitya tā katamā nikāya sa bhāge saṃskārāṇām prabandha vināśe anitya tā iti prajñaptiḥ nāmakāyāḥ katame dharmāṇām svabhāva adhivacane nāmakāyā iti prajñaptiḥ padakāyāḥ katame dharmāṇām viśeṣa adhivacane padakāyā iti prajñaptiḥ vyañjana kāyāḥ katameḥ tad ubhaya āśrayeṣu akṣareṣu vyañjanakāyā iti prajñaptiḥ tad ubhaya abhivyañjana tām upādāya varṇaḥ  api saḥ artha saṃvarṇana tām upādāya akṣare punar  paryāya akṣaraṇa tām upādāya pṛthagjana tvam katamat  ārya dharmāṇām apratilābhe pṛthagjana tvam iti prajñaptiḥ pravṛttiḥ katamā hetu phala prabandhān upacchede pravṛttiḥ iti prajñaptiḥ pratiniyamaḥ katamaḥ hetu phala nānā tve pratiniyama iti prajñaptiḥ yogaḥ katamaḥ hetu phala ānurūpye yoga iti prajñaptiḥ javaḥ katamaḥ hetu phala aśupravṛttau java iti prajñaptiḥ anukramaḥ katamaḥ hetu phala aikatye pravṛttau anukrama iti prajñaptiḥ kālaḥ katamaḥ hetu phala prabandha pravṛttau kāla iti prajñaptiḥ deśaḥ katamaḥ pūrva dakṣiṇa paścima uttarā dharā ūrdhvāsu sarvatas  daśasu dikṣu hetu phala eva deśa iti prajñaptiḥ saṃkhyā katamā saṃskārāṇām pratyekaśaḥ  bhede saṃkhyā iti prajñaptiḥ sāmagrī katamā hetu phala pratyaya samavadhāne sāmagri iti prajñaptiḥ 0 vijñāna skandha vyavasthānam katamat  yad cittam manaḥ vijñānam api tatra cittam katamat  skandha dhātu āyatana vāsanā paribhāvitam sarva vījakam ālaya vijñānam vipāka vijñānam ādāna vijñānam api tad  tad vāsanā cita tām upādāya manaḥ katamat  yad nitya kālam manyana ātmā kam ālayavijñānam caturbhiḥ kleśaiḥ saṃprayuktam ātma dṛṣṭi ātma snehena asmi mānena avidyayā ca tad ca sarvatragam kuśale api akuśale api avyākṛte api sthāpayitvā mārga sabhmukhībhāvam nirodha samāpattim aśaikṣa bhūmim ca yad ca ṣaṇṇām vijñānānām samanantara niruddham vijñānam vijñānam katamat  ṣaṣ  vijñāna kāyāḥ cakṣuḥ vijñānam śrotra ghrāṇa jivhā kāya manaḥ vijñānam cakṣuḥ vijñānam katamat  cakṣuḥ āśrayā rūpa ālambanā prati vijñaptiḥ śrotra vijñānam katamat  śrotra āśrayā śabda ālambanā prativijñaptiḥ ghrāṇa vijñānam katamat  ghrāṇa āśrayā gandha ālambanā pratibijñaptiḥ jilhā vijñānam katamat  jivhā āśrayā rasa ālambanā prativijñaptiḥ kāya vijñānam katamat  kāya āśrayā spraṣṭavya ālambanā prativijñaptiḥ manaḥ vijñānam katamat  manaā āśrayā dharma ālambanā prativijñaptiḥ dhātu vyavasthānam katamat  rūpa skandhā eva daśa dhātavaḥ cakṣuḥ dhātuḥ rūpa dhātuḥ śrotra dhātuḥ śabda dhātuḥ ghrāṇa dhātuḥ gandhadhātuḥ jivhādhātuḥ rasa dhātuḥ kāyadhātuḥ spraṣṭavya dhātuḥ manaḥ  dhātu eka deśaḥ ca vedanā skandhaḥ saṃjñā skandhaḥ saṃskāra skandhaḥ ca dharmadhātu eka deśaḥ vijñāna skandha eca sapta vijñāna ghātavaḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ ṣaṣ  vijñāna dhātavaḥ  manodhātuḥ ca dharmadhātau skandhaiḥ asaṃgṛhītam katamat  dharmadhātau  asaṃskṛtā dharmāḥ te asaṃskṛta adharmāḥ punar aṣṭadhā kuśala dharma tathatā akuśala dharma tathatā avyākṛta dharma tathatā ākāśam apratisaṃkhyā nirodhaḥ pratisaṃkhyā nirodhaḥ āniṃjyam saṃjñā vedayita nirodhaḥ ca kuśala dharma tathatā katamā nairātmyam sā punar ucyate śūnyatā animittam bhūtakoṭiḥ parama arthaḥ  dharma ādhātuḥ ca kim upādāya tathatā tathatā ucyate ananyaya abhāva tām upādāya kim upādāya tathatā nairātmyam ucyate dvividha ātma viprayukta tām upādāya kim upādāya tathatā śūnyatā ucyate sarva saṃkleśa apracāra tām upādāya kim upādāya tathatā animittam ucyate sarva nimitta upaśama tām upādāya kim upādāya tathatā bhūtakāṭiḥ ucyate aviparyāsa ālambana tām upādāya kim upādāya tathatā parama artha ucyate parama artha jñāna gocara sthāna tām upādāya kim upādāya tathatā dharmadhātuḥ ucyate sarveṣām śrāvakāṇām pratyekabuddhānām ca buddha dharma nimitta āśraya tām upādāya yathā kuśa lala dharma tathatā tathā akuśala dharma tathatā avyākṛta dharma tathatā ca jñeyā ākāśam katamat  rūpa abhāvaḥ sarva kṛtya avakāśa tām upādāya apratisaṃkhyā nirodhaḥ katamaḥ yaḥ  nirodhaḥ  na visaṃyogaḥ pratisaṃkhyā nirodhaḥ katamaḥ yaḥ  nirodhaḥ  visaṃyogaḥ ānijyam katamat  śubha kṛtsna vīta rāgasya upari avīta rāgasya sukha nirodhaḥ saṃjñā vedayita nirodhaḥ katamaḥ ākiṃcanya āyatana vīta rāgasya bhāva agrāt uccalitasya śānta vihāra saṃjñā manasikāra pūrvakeṇa asthāvarāṇām citta caitasikānām dharmāṇām tad ekatyānām ca sthāvarāṇām nirodhaḥ paṃca rūpāṇi vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra skandhāḥ te aṣṭau asaṃskṛtā dharmāḥ ca evam te ṣoḍaśa dharmadhātava ucyante āyatana vyavasthānam katamat  daśa rūpa dhātava eva daśa rūpa āyatanāni sapta vijñāna dhātava eva manaā yatunam dharmadhātuḥ dharma āyatanam anene nayena skandha dhātu āyatanāni triṣu dharmeṣu saṃgṛhītāni bhavanti rūpa skandhaḥ  dharmadhātuḥ manaā āyatanam ca yad uktam cakṣuḥ ca cakṣuḥ dhātuḥ ca iti kim syāt cakṣuḥ ca cakṣuḥ dhātuḥ ca āhosvit  syāt cakṣuḥ dhātuḥ ca cakṣuḥ ca syāt cakṣuḥ na cakṣuḥ dhātuḥ yathā arhataḥ caramam cakṣuḥ syāt cakṣardhātu rna cakṣuḥ yathā aṇḍe vā kalale vā arvude vā peśyām vā mātuḥ kukṣau vālabdham cakṣuḥ labdham vā naṣṭam ārūpyeṣu upapannasya pṛthagjanasya vā yaḥ cakṣuḥ hetuḥ syāt cakṣuḥ cakṣuḥ dhātuḥ ca śiṣṭāsu avasthāṣu na syāt cakṣuḥ na cakṣuḥ dhātuḥ ca nirupādhi śeṣa nirvāṇa dhātu samāpannasya ārūpyeṣu upapannasya āryasya vā yathā cakṣuḥ ya cakṣuḥ dhātuḥ ca tathā śrotra ghrāṇa jivhākāya dhātavaḥ  yathāyogyam veditavyāḥ kim syāt manaḥ  api manaḥ dhātuḥ api ahosvit syāt manaḥ dhātuḥ api manaḥ  api syāt manaḥ  na manaḥ dhātuḥ yathā arhataḥ caramam manaḥ syāt manaḥ dhātuḥ na manaḥ yathā nirodha samāpannasya yaḥ  manohetuḥ syāt manaḥ  api manaḥ dhātuḥ api śiṣṭāsu avasthāsu na syāt manaḥ  api bhūmikena api kāmadhātā avapapannaḥ māvacareṇa cakṣuṣā kāmāvacarāṇi rūpāṇi paśyati rūpāvacareṇa ūrdhva bhūmikeana cakṣuṣā adhara bhūmikāni api rūpāṇi paśyati yathā cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi pratigṛṇhāti tatha dhātau  utpannaḥ rūpāvacareṇa kāyena sva bhūmikān sparśān budhyati tasmin dhātau svabhāvataḥ  na gandharasau vijñapti āhāra rāga virahāt anena nayena na ghrāṇa jivhayaḥ  rvijñānam kāmadhātau  utpannaḥ kāma avacareṇa manasā traidhātuka ānanāsravān  ca dharmāna vijānāti yadhā kāmadhātau  utpannaḥ tathā rūpa dhātau  utpannaḥ ārūpya dhātau  utpanna ārūpya avacareṇa manasā ārūpya avacarān sva bhūmikā nanāsravān  ca dharmān vijānāti anāsraveṇa manasā traidhātuka ānanāsravān  ca dharmān vijānāti kim upādāya skandhānām tathā anukramaḥ vijñāna adhiṣṭhāna tām upādāya catvāri vijñāna adhiṣṭhānāni vijñānāni ca pūrva apara āśritāni yathā rūpam tathā bhavaḥ yathā vedayate tathā saṃjānīte yathā saṃjānīte tathā cetayate yathā cetayate tathā vijñānam tatra tatra upagaṃ bhavati saṃkleśa vyavadānataḥ yatra saṃkliśyate vyavadāyate ca vedanā nimitta grahaṇa abhisaṃskāreṇa saṃkleśa vyavadānābhyām ca saṃkliśyate vyavadāyate ca anena nayena skandhānām ukramaḥ  nirdiśyate katham dhātūnām tathā anukramaḥ laukika vastu vikalpa pravṛtti tā mupādāya katamā laukikī vastu vikalpa pravṛttiḥ loke prathamam paśyati dṛṣṭvā vyatisārayati vyatisārya snāpitam gandham mālyam ca paricarati tatas  nānāvidham praṇītam bhojanam paricarati tatas  aneka śayyā āsana dāsī parikān paricarati aparataḥ manaḥ dhātoḥ api teṣu teṣu vikalpaḥ evam ca adhyātma dhātoḥ anukrameṇa bahirdhā dhātoḥ vyavasthānam tad anukrameṇa vijñāna dhātoḥ vyavasthānam yathā dhātūnām anukrama āyatanānām api tadvat  skandha arthaḥ katamaḥ yad  kiṃcid rūpam atītam anāgatam pratyutpannam adhyātmam vā bahirdhā vā audārikam vā sūkṣmam vā hīnam vā praṇītam vā yad vā dūre yad vā antike tad sarvam abhisaṃkṣipya ucyate rūpa skandhaḥ rāśi artham upādaya yathā vitta rāśiḥ evam yāvat  vijñāna skandham āpica duḥkha vaipulya lakṣaṇa tām upādāya skandha ucyate yathā mahā vṛkṣa skandhaḥ yad uktam sūtre yathā aikāntika mahā duḥkha samudayataḥ api ca saṃkleśataḥ  bhāra vahana tām upādāya skandha ucyate yathā skandhena bhāram udvahati dhātvarthaḥ katamaḥ sarva dharma vīja arthaḥ sva lakṣaṇa dhāraṇa arthaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva dhāraṇa arthaḥ sarva prakāra dharma saṃgra hadhāraṇa arthañca āyatana arthaḥ katamaḥ vijñānāya dvāra artha  āyatana arthaḥ yathā buddhena bhāṣitam rūpam budbuda upamam vedanā phena upamā saṃjñā marīcikā upamā saṃskārāḥ parṇaḥ  pamā vijñānam māyā upamam iti kimartham rūpam budbuda upamam yāvat  vijñānam māyā upamam iti anātmataḥ  aśucitaḥ  hīna rasa taḥ  adṛḍhataḥ  asārataḥ ca atha mūla vastuni tridharma paricchede prathame dvitīyaḥ  bhāgaḥ punar  skandha dhātu āyatanānām vikalpāḥ katame tathā ca udānam dravyam antaḥ  jñeya rūpāṇi āsrava utpannaka ādi ca atītāḥ pratyayāḥ ca eva katham kati kimarthibhiḥ skandha dhātu āyataneṣu katham dravyamat  kati dvayamanti kimartham dravya mad parīkṣā abhilāpa nirapekṣaḥ tad anya nirapekṣaḥ ca indriya gocaraḥ  dravyamat  sarvam dravyamat  ātma dravyā bhiniveśa tyājana artham katham prajñaptimat  kati prajñaptimanti kimartham prajñaptimat parīkṣā abhilāpa sāpekṣaḥ tad anya sāpekṣaḥ ca indriya gocaraḥ prajñaptimat  sarvam prajñaptimat  prajñaptimada ātmā bhiniveśa tyājana artham katham saṃvṛtimat  kati saṃvṛtimanti kimartham saṃvṛtimat parīkṣā saṃkleśa ālambanam saṃvṛtimat  sarvam saṃvṛtimat  saṃkleśa nimitta ātma abhiniveśa tyajana artham katham paramārtha sat  kati paramārtha santi kimartham parama artha sat parīkṣā vyavadāna ālambanam paramārtha sat  sarvam paramārtha sat  vyavadāna nimitta ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham jñeyam kati jñeyāni kimartham jñeya parīkṣā jñeyāni paṃca rūpam cittam caitasikā dharmāḥ citta viprayuktāḥ saṃskārā asaṃskṛtam ca yatra saṃkleśaḥ  vyavadānam vayat  saṃkliśyate vyavadāyate vā yaḥ ca saṃkleśayati vyavadāyayati vā yā ca tatra avasthā yā ca vyavadāna tā tad āśrayeṇa sarvam jñeyam tatra rūpam rūpa skandhaḥ  daśa rūpa dhātavaḥ  daśa rūpa āyatanāni dharmadhātu āyatana saṃgṛhītāni ca rūpāṇi cittam vijñāna skandhaḥ sapta vijñāna dhātavaḥ  manaā āyatanam ca caitasikā dharmā vedanā skandhaḥ saṃjñā skandhaḥ saṃskāra skandhaḥ  dharmadhātu āyatana eka deśaḥ ca citta viprayuktāḥ saṃskārāḥ citta viprayuktaḥ saṃskāra skandhaḥ  dharmadhātu āyatana eka deśaḥ ca asaṃskṛtam dharmadhātu āyatana eka deśaḥ api khalu jñeyā dharmāḥ adhimukti jñāna gocarataḥ  api yukti jñāna gocarataḥ  api avisāra jñāna gocarataḥ  api pratyātma jñāna gocarataḥ  api para ātma jñāna gocarataḥ  api adhara jñāna gocarataḥ  api ūrdhva jñāna gocarataḥ  api vidūṣaṇa jñāna gocarataḥ  api samutthāna jñāna gocarataḥ  api anutpāda jñāna gocarataḥ  api jñāna jñāna gocarataḥ  api niṣṭhā jñāna gocarataḥ  api mahā artha jñāna gocarataḥ  api jānaka paśyaka ātma abhiniveśa tmā jana artham katham vijñeyam kati vijñeyāni kimartham vijñeya parīkṣā avikalpanataḥ  api vikalpanataḥ  api hetutaḥ api pravṛttitaḥ  api nimittatas  api naimittakataḥ api vipakṣa pratipakṣataḥ  api sūkṣma prabhedataḥ  api vijñeyam draṣṭavyam sarvāṇi vijñeyāni draṣṭā dyātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham abhijñeyam kati abhijñeyāni kimartham abhijñeya parīkṣā saṃkrāntitaḥ  api anuśravataḥ  api carita praveśataḥ  api āgatitaḥ  api gatitaḥ  api niḥsaraṇataḥ  api sarvāṇi abhijñeyāni sa anubhāva ātma abhiniveśa tyājanartham katham rūpi kati rūpīṇi kimartham rūpi parīkṣā rūpi tad ātmataḥ  api bhūta āśrayataḥ  api nandī samudayataḥ  api pradeśataḥ  api deśa vyāptitaḥ  api deśa upade śa taḥ api deśa gocarataḥ  api dvaya samaya gocarataḥ  api sambandhataḥ  api nuvandhataḥ  api prarūpaṇataḥ  api vyābādhanataḥ  api saṃprāpaṇataḥ  api saṃcaya vyavasthānataḥ  api vahiḥ mukhataḥ api antarmukhataḥ api āyatatas  api parichinnataḥ  api tad kālataḥ  api nidarśanataḥ api rūpi draṣṭavyam sarvāṇi rūpīṇi yathāyogam vā rūpyā tmā bhiniveśa tyājana artham katham arūpi kati arūpīṇi kimartham arūpi parīkṣā rūpi viparyayeṇa āpi am rūpi sarvāṇi arūpīṇi yathāyogam vā arūpya ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham sa nidarśanam kati sa nidarśanāni kimartham sa nidarśana parīkṣā cakṣuḥ gocaraḥ sa nidarśanam śiṣṭasya rūpivat  prabhedaḥ sarvāṇi sa nidarśanāni yathāyogam vā cākṣuṣa ātma abhiniveśa tyājanā rtham katham anirdarśanam kati anidarśanāni kimartham anidarśana parīkṣā sa nidarśana viparyayeṇa anidarśanam draṣṭavyam sarvāṇi anidarśanāni yathāyogam vā cākṣuṣā tmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham sa pratigham kati sa pratighāni kimartham sa pratigha parīkṣā yad  sa nidarśanam sa prati gham api tad  api khalu tribhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ sa pratigham draṣṭavyam jātitaḥ  api upacayataḥ  api aparikarma kṛtatas  api tatra jātitaḥ yadya da nyaḥ anyam āvṛṇoti avriyate ca tatra upacaya taḥ paramaṇaḥ rūrddham tatra aparikarma kṛtatas yad na samādhi vaśa vartti rūpam api khalu prakopa pada sthānataḥ   sa pratigham sarvāṇi sa pratighāni yathāyogam vā asarva gata ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham apratigham kati apratighāni kimartham apratigha parīkṣā sa pratigha viparyeṇa apratigham sarvāṇi apratighāni yathāyogam vā sarva gata ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham sa āsravam kati sa āsravāṇi kimartham sa āsrava parīkṣā āsrava tadātmataḥ  api āsrava saṃbandha taḥ  api āsrava anuvandhataḥ  api āsrava ānukūlyataḥ api āsrava anvayataḥ  api sa āsravam draṣṭavyam pañca upādāna skandhāḥ sa āsravāḥ pañcadaśa dhātavaḥ  daśa āyatanāni trayāṇām dhātūnām dvayoḥ ca āyatanayoḥ pradeśaḥ āsrava yukta ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham anāsravam kati anāsravāṇi kimartham anāsrava parīkṣā sa āsrava viparyayeṇa anāsravam pañca anupādana skandhāḥ trayāṇām dhātūnām dvayoḥ ca āyata tanayoḥ pradeśaḥ āsrava viyukta ātma ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham saraṇam kati saraṇāni kimartham saraṇa parīkṣā yad rūpān rāga dveṣa mohān āgamya śastra ādāna daṇḍa ādāna kalaha bhaṇḍana vigraha vivādāḥ saṃbhavanti tad ātmataḥ  api tad sambandha taḥ api tad bandhataḥ api tad anubandhataḥ  api tad ānukūlyataḥ  api tad anvayataḥ  api saraṇam draṣṭavyam yāvanti sa āsravāṇi tāvanti saraṇāni raṇa yukta ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham kathamaraṇam kati araṇāni kimartha maraṇa parīkṣā saraṇa viparyayeṇa āraṇam yāvanti anāsravāṇi tāvanti araṇāni raṇa viprayukta ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham sa āmiṣam kati sa āmiṣāṇi kimartham sa āmiṣa parīkṣā yad rūpān rāga dveṣa mohān āgamya paunarbha vikam ātma bhāvam adhyavasyati tad ātmataḥ  api tad sambandha taḥ api tad bandhataḥ api tad anubandhataḥ  api tad ānukūlyataḥ  api tad anvayataḥ  api sa āmiṣam draṣṭavyam yāvanti saraṇāni tāvanti sa āmiṣāṇi āmiṣa yukta ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham nirāmiṣam kati nirāmiṣāṇi kimartham nirāmiṣa parīkṣā sa āmiṣa viparyayeṇa nirāmiṣam yāvanti araṇāni tāvanti nirāmiṣāṇi āmiṣa viyukta ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham gredha āśritam kati gredhā śritāni kimartham gredha āśrita parīkṣā yad rūpān rāga dveṣa mohān āgamya pañca kāma guṇān adhyavasyati tad ātmataḥ  api tad sambandha taḥ api tabdandhataḥ  api tad anubandhataḥ  api tadā anukulyataḥ  api tad anvayataḥ  api gredha āśritam draṣṭavyam yāvanti sa āmiṣāṇi tāvanti gredha āśritāni gredha yukta ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham naiṣkramya āśritam kati naiṣkramya āśritāni kimartham naiṣkramya āśrita parīkṣā gredha āśrita viparyayeṇa naiṣkramya āśritam yāvanti nirāmiṣāṇi tāvanti naiṣkramya āśritāni gredha viyukta ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham saṃskṛtam kati saṃskṛtāni kimartham saṃskṛta parīkṣā yasya utpā daḥ api prajñāyate vyayaḥ  api sthiti anyathātvam api tad sarvam saṃskṛtam draṣṭavyam sarvāṇi saṃskṛtāni sthāpayitvā dharmadhātu āyatana eka deśam anitya ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham asaṃskṛtam kati asaṃskṛtāni kimartham asaṃskṛta parīkṣā saṃskṛta viparyayeṇa āsaṃskṛtam dharmadhātu āyatana eka deśaḥ nitya ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham anupādāna skandhāḥ saṃskṛtam vaktavyam asaṃskṛtam vaktavyam ḷ na saṃskṛtam na asaṃskṛtam vaktavyam tad kasya hetoḥ karma kleśān abhisaṃskṛta tām upādāya na saṃskṛtam kāmakāra saṃmukhī vimukhībhāva tām upādāya na asaṃskṛtam yad uktam bhagavatā dvayam idam saṃskṛtam ca asaṃskṛtam ca iti [ḷ] tad katham yena arthena saṃskṛtam na tena arthena āsaṃskṛtam yena asaṃskṛtam na tena arthena saṃskṛtam iti atra nayaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ katham laukikam kati laukikāni kimartham laukika parīkṣā traidhātuka paryāpannam laukikam lokottara pṛṣṭha labdham ca tad pratibhāsam skandhānām eka deśaḥ pañcadaśa dhātavaḥ daśa āyatanāni trayāṇām dhātūnām dvayoḥ ca āyatanayoḥ pradeśaḥ ātmani loka abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham loka uttaram kati loka uttarāṇi kimartham loka uttara parīkṣā traidhātuka pratipakṣaḥ  viparyāsa niṣprapañca nirvikalpa tayā ca nirvikalpam lokottaram api khalu paryāyeṇa lokaḥ  ttara pṛṣṭa labdham lokottaram laukikā śrita tām upādāya skandhānām eka deśaḥ trayāṇām dhātūnām dvayoḥ ca āyatanayoḥ kevala ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham utpannam kati utpannāni kimartham utpanna parīkṣā atīta pratyutpannam utpakṣam sarvepām eka deśaḥ aśāśvata ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham api khalu catur viśatividham utpannam ādi utpannam prabandha utpannam upacaya utpannam āśraya utpannam vikāra utpannam paripāka utpannam hāni utpannam viśeṣa utpannam prabhāsvarā utpannam aprabhāsvara utpannam saṃkrānti utpannam savīja utpannam avīja utpannam pratibimba vibhutva nidarśana utpannam paraṃpara utpannam kṣaṇa bhaṅga utpannam saṃyoga viyoga utpannam avasthā antara utpannam cyuta upapāda utpannam saṃvartta vivartta utpannam pūrva kāla utpannam maraṇa kālaḥ  tpannam antara utpannam pratisandhi kāla utpannam ca katham anutpannam kati anutpannāni kimartham anutpanna parīkṣā anāgatamasaṃskṛtam ca anutpannam sarvepām eka deśaḥ śāśvata ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham api khalu utpanna viparyayeṇa anutpannam katham grāhakam kati grāhakāṇi kimartham grāhaka parīkṣā rūpi indriyam citta caitasikāḥ ca dharmā grāhakam draṣṭavyam trayaḥ skandhā rūpa saṃskāra skandha eka deśaḥ dvādaśa dhātavaḥ ṣaṣ āyatanāni dharmadhātu āyatana eka deśaḥ ca bhoktā ātmā bhiniveśalājana artham api khalu aprāpta grāhakam prāpta grāhakam sva lakṣaṇa varttamāna pratyeka grāhakam sva sāmānya lakṣaṇa sarva kālam sarva viṣaya grāhakam ca grāhakam draṣṭavyam sāmagrī vijñāna samutpatti tām upādāya prajñaptikaḥ ca grāhaka vādaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ katham grāhyam kati grāhyāni kimartham grāhya parīkṣā yad tāvat  grāhakam grāhyam api tad  syāt grāhyam na grāhakam grāhaka gocara eva arthaḥ sarvāṇi grāhyāṇi viṣaya ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham vahirmukham kati bahirmukhāni kimartham bahirmukha parīkṣā kāma pratisaṃyuktam bahirmukham sthāpayitvā buddha śāsane śruta maya cintā āmaya tad anu dharma parigṛhītām ścitta caitasikān dharmān ca tu āraḥ  dhātavaḥ dve ca āyatane tad anyeṣām ca eka deśaḥ avīta rāga ātma abhiniveśa tyājanartham katham antarmukham kati antarmukhāni kimartham anta mukha parīkṣā bahirmukha viparyayeṇa antarmukham catutaḥ  dhātūn sthāpayitvā dve ca āyatane tad anyeṣām eka deśaḥ vīta rāga ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham kliṣṭam kati kliṣṭāni kimartham kliṣṭa parīkṣā akuśalam nivṛta avyākṛtam ca kliṣṭam nivṛta avyākṛtam punar  sarvatra gamanaḥ saṃprayuktaḥ kleśaḥ  rūpārūpya pratisaṃyu kta śca skandhānām daśānām dhātunām caturṇṇām āyatanānām eka deśaḥ kleśa yukta ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham akliṣṭam kati akliṣṭāni kimartham akliṣṭa pa rīkṣā kuśalam anivṛta avyākṛtam vā akliṣṭam aṣṭau dhātavaḥ aṣṭa āyatanāni skandhānām śeṣāṇām ca dhātu āyatanānām eka deśaḥ kleśa viyukta ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham atītam kati atītāni kimartham atīta parikṣā utpanna niruddha lakṣaṇataḥ  api hetu phala upayaḥ gataḥ  api saṃkleśa vyavadāna kāritra samatikrāntitaḥ  api hetu parigraha vināśa taḥ api phala sva lakṣaṇa bhāva abhāva tā api smara saṃkalpa nimittatā uhapi apekṣā saṃkleśa nimittatas  api upekṣā vyavadāna nimittatas  api atitam draṣṭavyam sarveṣām ekedaśaḥ pravarttaka ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham anāgatam kati anāgatāni kimartham anāgata parīkṣā hetau satya nutpannataḥ  api alabdha sva lakṣaṇataḥ  api hetu phala anupayogataḥ  api saṃkleśa vyavadāna bhāvā pratyupasthānataḥ  api hetu svabhā vā abhāvataḥ api abhinandana asaṃkleśa nimittatas  api abhinandana avyavadāna nimittatas  api anāgatam draṣṭavyam sarveṣām eka deśaḥ pravarttaka ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham pratyutpannam kati pratyutpannāni kimartham pratyutpanna parīkṣā utpanna aniruddha lakṣaṇataḥ  api hetu phala upayoga anupayogataḥ  api saṃkleśa vyavadāna pratyupasthānataḥ  api atīta anāgata bhāva nimittatas  api kāritra pratyupasthānataḥ  api pratyutpannam draṣṭavyam sarveṣām eka deśaḥ pravarttaka ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham eva atīta anāgata pratyutpannam punar  kathā vastu na nirvāṇam pratyātma vedanīya tayā nirabhilapya tām upādāya bhuta bhavya varttamāna parihā rādhiṣṭhā ānatām ca upādaya katham kuśalam kati kuśalāni kimartham kuśala parīkṣā svabhāvataḥ  api sambandhataḥ  api anubandhataḥ  api utthānataḥ api paramārtha taḥ  api upapatti lābhataḥ  api prayogataḥ  api puraskāra taḥ  api anugrahataḥ  api parigrahataḥ  api pratipakṣataḥ  api upaśamataḥ api niṣyandataḥ  api kuśalam draṣṭavyam skandhānām daśānām dhātunām caturṇām ca āyatānānām pradeśaḥ dharma yukta ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham svabhāvataḥ kuśalam katamat  śraddhādaya ekādaśa caitasikā dharmāḥ sambandhataḥ kuśalam katamat  tad saṃprayuktā dharmāḥ anubandhataḥ kuśalam katamat  teṣām eva yā vāsanā utthanataḥ kuśalam katamat  tad samutthāpitam kāya karmma vākkarmma paramārthataḥ kuśalam katamat  tathatā upapatti lābhataḥ kuśalam katamat  eṣām eva kuśalānām dharmāṇām pūrva abhyāsam āgamyam tad rūpā vipāka abhinirvṛtiḥ yathā teṣu eva prakṛtyā apratisaṃkhyāya rūciḥ saṃtiṣṭhate prayogataḥ kuśalam katamat  sat puruṣa saṃsevām āgamya saddharma śravaṇam yoni śas  manaskāram dharma anudharma pratipattim kuśalasya bhāvanā puskārataḥ kuśalam katamat  yad tathāgatam vā puraskṛtya caitye vā pusta gate vā citra gate dharmam vā puraskṛtya dharma adhiṣṭhāni pustake pūjā karma anugrahataḥ kuśalam katamat  yad caturbhi saṃgraha vastubhiḥ sattvān anugṛṇhataḥ parigrahataḥ kuśalam katamat  yad dāna mayena puṇya kriyā vastunā vā śīla mayena vā svarga upapatti parigrahaḥ  vā āḍhyaḥ  kula upapatti parigrahaḥ  vā vyavadāna ānukūlya parigrahaḥ  vā pratipakṣataḥ kuśalam katamat  yaḥ  vidūṣaṇa apratipakṣaḥ ādhāra pratipakṣa dūrobhāva pratipakṣaḥ viṣkambhaṇa apratipakṣaḥ visaṃyoga pratipakṣaḥ kleśa āvaraṇa pratipakṣaḥ jñeya āvaraṇa pratipakṣaḥ upaśamataḥ kuśalam katamat  yad tad paryādāya rāga prahāṇam paryādāya dveṣa prahāṇam paryādāya moha prahāṇam paryādāya sarva kleśa prahāṇam saṃjñā vedayita nirodhaḥ sa upadhi śeṣaḥ  nirupadhi śeṣaḥ  nirvāṇa dhā ātura pratiṣṭhita nirvāṇam ca niṣyandataḥ kuśalam katamat  upaśama prāptasya tad ādhipatyena vaiśeṣikā guṇā abhijñādayaḥ  laukika lokottarāḥ sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇāḥ katham akuśalam kati akuśalāni kimartham akuśala parīkṣā svabhāvataḥ  api saṃbandhataḥ  api anubandhataḥ  api utthānataḥ api paramārtha taḥ  api upapatti lābhataḥ  api prayogataḥ  api puraskāra taḥ  api upaghātatas  api parigrahataḥ  api vipakṣataḥ  api paripanthataḥ  api akuśalam draṣṭavyam skandhānām daśānām dhātunām caturṇṇām āyatanānām pradeśaḥ adharma yukta ātmābhini veśa tyājana artham svabhāvataḥ  akuśalam katamat  manaḥ saṃprayuktam rūpārūpya avacaram ca kleśam sthāpayitvā tad anyaḥ klaśa upakleśaḥ  duścarita samutthāpakaḥ sambandhataḥ  akuśalam katamat  taiḥ eva kleśa upakleśaiḥ saṃprayuktā dharmāḥ anubandhataḥ  akuśalam katamat  teṣām eva vāsanā utthānataḥ akuśalam katamat  samutthāpitam kāya vāc karma paramārtha taḥ  akuśalam katamat  sarva saṃsāraḥ upapatti lābhataḥ  akuśalam katamat  yathā api tad akuśalā bhyāsa stu udapaḥ  vipākaḥ  abhinivarttate yena akuśala eva rūciḥ santiṣṭhate prayogataḥ  akuśalam katamat  yathā api tad asat puruṣa saṃsevāmā gamya sat dharma śravaṇam ayoni śomanaskāram kāyena duścaritam carati vācā manasā duścarītam carati puraskāra taḥ  akuśalam katamat  yathā api tad anyatama anyatamam deva nikāya sanniśrayam puraskṛtya hiṃsā pūrvakam vā kudṛṣṭi pūrvakam vā caityam pratiṣṭhāpayati tatra vā pūjā karma prayojayati yatra mahān janakāyaḥ  apuṇyena yujyate upaghātatas  akuśalam katamat  yathā api tad sattveṣu kāyena vācā manasā mithyā pratipadyate parigrahataḥ  akuśalam katamat  yathā tad kāyena duścaritam caritvā vācā manasā duścaritam caritvā durgatau vā sugatau vā aniṣṭam phalam gṛṇhātyakṣepakam vā paripūrakam vā vipakṣataḥ  akuśalam katamat  ye pratipakṣa vipakṣā dharmāḥ pari panthataḥ akuśalam katamat  ye kuśala antarāyikā dharmāḥ katham avyākṛtam kati avyākṛtāni kimartham avyākṛta parīkṣā svābhāvataḥ  api sambandhataḥ  api anubandhataḥ  api utthānataḥ api paramārtha taḥ  api upapatti lābhataḥ  api prayogataḥ  api puraskāra taḥ  api anugrahataḥ  api upabhogataḥ  api parigrahataḥ  api pratipakṣataḥ  api upaśamataḥ  api niṣyandataḥ  api avyākṛtam praṣṭhavyam aṣṭau dhātavaḥ aṣṭau  āyatanāni śeṣāṇām skandha dhātu āyatanā nā meka deśaḥ dharma adharma viyukta ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham svabhāvataḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  aṣṭau rūpīṇi dhātu āyatanāni sa saṃprayogam manaḥ jīvita indriyam nikāya sabhāgaḥ  nāma kāya pada kāya vyañjana kāyāḥ ca sambandhataḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  aduṣṭa aprasanna cittasya taiḥ eva nāma pada vyañjana kāyaiḥ parigṛhītāḥ citta caitasikā dharmāḥ anubandhataḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  teṣām eva abhilāpa vāsanā utthānataḥ avyākṛtam katamat  tad parigṛhītaiḥ citta caitasikaiḥ dharmaiḥ ya tsamutthāpitam kāya vāc karma paramārtha taḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  ākāśam apratisaṃkhyā nirodhaḥ ca upapatti lābhataḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  akuśalānām kuśala sa āsravāṇām ca dharmāṇām vipākaḥ prayogataḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  akliṣṭa akuśala cetasa airyāpathikam śailpa sthānikam ca puraskāra taḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  yathā api tad anyatama anyatamam deva nikāya sanniśrayam puraskṛtya hiṃsā kudṛṣṭi vivarjitam caityam vā pratiṣṭhāpayati pūjā karma vā prayojayati yatra mahā janakāyaḥ  na puṇyam prasavati na apuṇyam anugrahataḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  yathā api tad dāsa bhṛtaka karma kareṣu putra dāreṣu vā aduṣṭa aprasanna cittaḥ  dānam dadāti upabhogataḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  yathā api tad apratisaṃkhyā kliṣṭa cittaḥ  bhogān bhuṃkte parigrahataḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  yathā api tad śilpa sthānasya abhyasta tvāt āyatyām tad rūpam mā ātma bhāva parigraham karoti yena laghu ladhvā iva teṣu śilpa sthāneṣu śikṣā niṣṭhām gacchati pratipakṣataḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  yathā api tad  pratisaṃkhyāya bhaiṣajyam niṣevate upaśamataḥ  avyākṛtam katamat  rūpārūpya vacaraḥ kleśaḥ śamatha upagūḍha tām upādāya niṣyandataḥ  avyākṛmatam katamat  nirvāṇa citta sahajam api khalu nidarśanataḥ kuśalam api akuśalam api avyākṛtam api draṣṭavyam tad punar  katamat  yad buddhāḥ parama pārami prāptāḥ ca bodhisattvā nidarśayanti sattvānām anugraha artham na tu teṣām tatra tathā kācid  pariniṣpattiḥ katham kāma pratisaṃyuktam kati kā ma pratisaṃyuktāni kimartham kāma pratisaṃyukta parīkṣā avīta rāgasya sa āsrava kuśala akuśala avya akṛtam kāma prati saṃyuktam draṣṭavyam catvāraḥ  dhātavaḥ  dve ca āyatane tad anyeṣām ca skandha dhātu āyatanānām eka deśaḥ kāma avīta rāga ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham rūpa pratisaṃyuktāni kimartham rūpa pratisaṃyukta parīkṣā kāma vīta rāgasya rūpāvīta rāgasya kuśala āvya kṛtam rūpa pratisaṃyuktam draṣṭavyam caturaḥ  dhātūna dve ca āyatane sthāpayitā tad anyeṣām skandha dhātu āyatanānām eka deśaḥ kāma vīta rāga ātmabhiniveśa tyājana artham katham ārūpapya pratisaṃyuktam kati ārūpya pratisaṃyuktāni kimartham ārūpya pratisaṃyuktā parīkṣā rūpa vīta rāgasya ārūpya avīta rāgasya kuśala avya akṛtam vārūpya pratisaṃyuktam draṣṭavyam caturṇānskandhānām dvayaḥ ścāyatanayoḥ pradeśaḥ rūpa vīta rāga ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham vairāgyam punar eka deśa vairāgyam skala vairāgyam prativedha vairāgyam upaghāta vairāgyam samudghāta vairāgyam ca draṣṭavyam api khalu daśa vairāgyāṇi prakṛti vairāgyam upaghāta vairāgyam upastambha vairāgyam samutkarṣa vairāgyam sammoha vairāgyam pratipakṣa vairāgyam parijñā vairāgyam prahāṇi vairāgyam sa uttara vairāgyam niruttara vairāgyam prakṛti vairāgyam katamat  duḥkhāyām vedanāyām duḥkha sthānīyeṣu ca dhamaṣu yā pratikula tā upaghāta vairāgyam katamat  maithuna prayuktasya dāha vigame yā pratikūla tā upastambha vairāgyam katamat  su bhuktavataḥ  mṛṣṭe api bhojane yā pratikūla tā samutkarṣa vairāgyam katamat  uccataram sthānam prāptava taḥ nirhīne sthāne yā pratikūla tā sammoha vairāgyam katamat  bālānām nirvāṇe yā pratikūla tā pratipakṣa vairāgyam katamat  laukikena vā loka uttareṇa vā mārgeṇa yad kleśa prahāṇam parijñā vairāgyam katamat  pratilabdha darśana mārgasya traidhātuke yā pratikūla tā prahāṇi vairāgyam katamat  bhūmau bhūmau kleśān prajahataḥ  yā pratikūla tā sa uttara vairāgyam katamat  laukikānām śrāvaka pratyekabuddhānām ca yad vairāgyam niruttaram vairāgyam katamat  yad  buddha bodhisattvānām vairāgyam sarva sattva hita sukha adhiṣṭhāna tā mupādāya katham śaikṣam kati śaikṣāṇi kimartham śaikṣa parīkṣā mokṣa prayuktasya kuśalam śaikṣam draṣṭavyam skandhānā daśānām dhātūnām caturṇām ca āyatanām eka deśaḥ mokṣa prayukta ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham aśaikṣam kati aśaikṣāṇi kimartham aśaikṣa parīkṣā śikṣāyām niṣṭhā gatasya kuśalam aśaikṣam draṣṭavyam skandhānām daśānām dhātūnām caturṇām ca āyatanānām pradeśaḥ bhukta ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham na eva śaikṣān āśaikṣam kati na eva śaikṣāna aśaikṣāni kimartham na eva śaikṣān āśa ekṣa parīkṣā pṛthagjanasya kuśala akuśala avya kṛtam śaikṣasya kliṣṭa avyākṛtam aśaikṣasya ca avyākṛtam asaṃskṛtam ca na eva śaikṣān āśaikṣam draṣṭavyam aṣṭau dhātavaḥ  aṣṭā vāyatanāni tad anyeṣām skandha dhātu āyatanānām pradeśaḥ amukta ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham darśana prahātavyam kati darśana prahātavyāni kimartham darśana prahāta vya parīkṣā parikalpitā kliṣṭā dṛṣṭiḥ vicikitsā dṛṣṭi sthānam ye ca dṛṣṭau vipratipannāḥ kleśa upakleśāḥ yad ca dṛṣṭyā samutthāpitam kāyavā kkarma sarvam cāpāyikam skandha dhātu āyatanam darśana prahātavyam draṣṭavyam sarveṣām eka deśaḥ darśana saṃpanna ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham bhāvanā prahātavyam kati bhāvanā prahātavyāni kimartham bhāvanā prahāta vyaparīkṣā labdha darśana mārgasya tad ūrdhvam darśana prahātavya viparyayeṇa sa āsravā dharmāḥ sarveṣām eka deśaḥ bhāvanā saṃpanna ātmā abhiniveśa tyajana artham katham aprahātavyam kati aprahātavyāni kimamartham aprahāta vya parīkṣā anāsravam aprahātavyam draṣṭavyam sthāpayitvā nirvedha bhāgīyam skaṃdhānām daśānām dhātūnām caturṇām ca āyatanānām pradeśaḥ siddha ātmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham pratītyasamutpannam kati pratītyasamutpannāni kimartham pratītyasamutpanna parīkṣā lakṣaṇataḥ  api aṅga vibhāgataḥ  api aṅga samāsataḥ  api aṅga pratyayatva vyavasthānataḥ api aṅga karma vyavasthānataḥ  api aṅga saṃkleśa saṃgrahataḥ  api arthataḥ  api gāmbhīryataḥ  api prabhedataḥ  api anuloma pratiloma taḥ api pratītyasamutpannam draṣṭavyam sarvāṇi dharmadhātu āyatana eka deśam sthāpayitvā ahetu viṣama hetuka ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham lakṣaṇataḥ nirī ha pratyaya utpatti tām upādāya anitya pratyaya utpatti tām upādāya samartha pratyaya utpatti tām upādāya katham aṅga vibhāgataḥ dvādaśa aṅgāni dvādaśa aṅgaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ avidyā saṃskārā vijñānam nāma rūpam ṣaṣ āyatanam sparśaḥ  vedanā tṛṣṇā upadānam bhavaḥ  jāti rjarā maraṇam ca katham aṅga samāsataḥ api ākṣepaka aṅgam ākṣipta aṅgam abhinirvarttaka aṅgam abhinirvṛtti aṅgam ca ākṣepaka aṅgam katamat  avidyā saṃskārā vijñānam ca ākṣiptaka aṅgam katamat  nāma rūpam ṣaṣ āyatanam sparśaḥ  vedanā ca abhinrivarttaka aṅgam katamat  tṛṣṇā upādānam bhavaḥ ca abhinirvṛtti aṅgam katamat  jāti rjarā maraṇam ca katham aṅga pratyayatva vyavasthānataḥ vāsanātaḥ  api āvedhataḥ  api manasikārataḥ  api sahabhāvataḥ  api āṅgānām pratyayatva vyavasthānam veditavyam tad ca yathāyogam katham aṅga karma vyavasthānataḥ avidyā kiṃkarmikā bhave ca sattvān saṃmohayati pratyayaḥ ca bhavati saṃskārāṇām saṃskārāḥ kiṃkarmakāḥ gatiṣu ca sattvān vibhajanti pratyayāḥ ca bhavanti vijñāna vāsanāyāḥ vijñānam kim karmakam sattvānām karma bandham ca dhārayati pratyayaḥ ca bhavati nāma rūpasya nāma rūpam ca kiṃkarmakam ātma bhāvam ca sattvān grāhayati pratyayaḥ ca bhavati ṣaṣ āyatanasya ṣaṣ āyatanam kiṃkarmakam ātma bhāva paripūrim ca sattvān grāhayati pratya yaḥ ca bhavati sparśasya sparśaḥ kiṃkarmakaḥ viṣaya upabhoge ca sattvān pravarttayati pratyayaḥ ca bhavati vedanāyāḥ vedanā kiṃkarmikā janma upabhoge ca sattvān pravarttayati pratyayaḥ ca bhavati tṛṣṇāyāḥ tṛṣṇā kiṃkarmikā janmani ca sattvān ākarṣayati pratyayaḥ ca bhavati upādānasya upādānam kiṃkarmakam punarbhava ādāna artham sa upādānam ca sattvānām vijñānam karoti pratyayaḥ ca bhavati bhavasya bhavaḥ kiṃkarmakaḥ punarbhave ca sattva anabhimukhīkaroti pratyayaḥ ca bhavati jāteḥ jātiḥ kiṃkarmikā nāma rūpa ṣaṣ āyatana sparśa vedanā ānupūrvyā ca sattvān abhinirvarttayati pratyayaḥ ca bhavati jarā maraṇasya jarā maraṇam kiṃkarmakam punar  punar vayaḥ pariṇāmena jīvita pariṇāmena ca sattvāni ojayati katham aṅga saṃkle śasaṃgrahataḥ yā ca avidyā yā ca tṛṣṇā yad ca upādānam iti ayam saṃkleśa saṃgrahaḥ ye ca saṃskārā yad ca vijñānam yaḥ ca bhava iti ayam karma saṃkleśa saṃgrahaḥ śeṣāṇi janma saṃkleśa saṃgrahaḥ katham arthataḥ niḥkartṛka arthaḥ pratītyasamutpāda arthaḥ sa hetuka arthaḥ niḥsattva arthaḥ para taṃtra arthaḥ nirohaka arthaḥ anitya arthaḥ kṣaṇikā arthaḥ hetu phala prabandha an upaccheda arthaḥ anurūpa hetu phala arthaḥ vicitra hetu phala arthaḥ pratiniyata hetu phala arthaḥ ca pratītyasamutpāda arthaḥ katham gāmbhīryataḥ hetu gāmbhīryataḥ  api lakṣaṇa gāmbhīryataḥ  api utpatti bhāgāmbhīryataḥ  api sthiti gāmbhīryataḥ  api vṛtti gāmbhīryataḥ  api gāmbhīryam draṣṭavyam api khalu kṣaṇikaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ sthititaḥ ca upalabhyate nirīhaka pratyayaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ samartha pratyayaḥ ca upalabhyate niḥsattvaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ attvataḥ ca upalabhyate na svatas  na paratas  na dvābhyām na svayaṃkāra apa ra kāra ahetu samutpannaḥ atas  api gambhīraḥ katham prabhedataḥ vijñāna utpatti prabhedataḥ cyuti upapatti prabhedataḥ vāhya śasya utpatti prabhedataḥ saṃvartta vivartta prabhe dattaḥ āhāra upastambha prabhedataḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa gati vibhāga prabhedataḥ viśuddhi prabhedataḥ prabhāva prabhedataḥ ca prabhedaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ katham anuloma pratilomataḥ saṃkleśā nulomapratiloma taḥ  api vyavadāna anuloma pratiloma taḥ  api pratītyasamutpādasya anuloma pratiloma nirddeśaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ atha mūla vastuni tridhama paricchede prathame tṛtīyaḥ  bhāgaḥ katham pratyayaḥ kati pratyayāḥ kimartham pratyaya parīkṣā hetutaḥ api samanantarataḥ  api ālambanataḥ  api adhipatitaḥ  api pratyayaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ sarvāṇi pratyayaḥ ātma hetuka dharma abhiniveśa tyājana artham hetu pratyayaḥ katamaḥ ālaya vijñānam kuśala vāsanā ca api khalu svabhāvataḥ  api prabhedataḥ  api sahāyataḥ  api saṃpratipattitaḥ  api paripanthataḥ  api parigrahataḥ  api hetu pratyayaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ katham svabhāvataḥ kāraṇam hetu svabhāvataḥ katham prabhedataḥ utpatti kāraṇam tad yathā cakṣuḥ sāmagrī vijñānasya sthiti kāraṇam tad yathā āhāraḥ  bhūtānām sattvānām saṃbhava eṣiṇām ca dhṛti kāraṇam tad yathā pṛthivī sattvānām prakāśa kāraṇam tad yathā pradīpaḥ  rūpāṇām vikāra kāraṇam tad yathā agniḥ indhanasya viyoga kāraṇam tad yathā dātram chedyasya pariṇati kāraṇam tad yathā śilpa sthānā dikam hiraṇya ādīnām saṃpratyaya kāraṇam tad yathā dhūmaḥ  agneḥ saṃpratyāyana kāraṇam tad yathā pratijñā hetu dṛṣṭāntāḥ sādhyasya prāpaṇa kāraṇam tad yathā mārgaḥ  nirvāṇasya vyavahāra kāraṇam tad yathā nāma saṃjñā dṛṣṭiḥ ca apekṣā kāraṇam yad apekṣya yatra arthi tvam utpadyate tad yathā jighatsām apekṣya bhojane ākṣepa kāraṇam vidūraḥ pratyayaḥ tad yathā avidyā jarā maraṇasya abhinirvṛtti kāraṇam āsannaḥ pratyayaḥ tad yathā avidyā saṃskārāṇām parigraha kāraṇam tad anyaḥ pratyayaḥ tad yathā kṣetra udaka pāsyā ḷ vāpyā dikam sasya udayasya āvāhaka kāraṇam anukūlataḥ pratyayaḥ tad yathā samyak rājā sevā rājā ārādhanāyāḥ prati niyama kāraṇam pratyaya vaicitryam tad yathā pañca gati pratyayāḥ pañcānām gatīnām sahakāri kāraṇam pratyaya sāmagrī tad yathā vijñānasya indriyam aparibhinnam viṣaya ābhāsa gataḥ tad jaḥ ca manaskāraḥ pratyupasthitaḥ virodhi kāraṇam antarāyaḥ tad yathā sasyasya aśaniḥ avirodha kāraṇam na ntarāyaḥ tad yathā tasya eva antarāyasya abhāvaḥ katham sahāyataḥ ye dharmāḥ sahabhāvena utpadyante na anyatama vaikalyena tad yathā bhūtāni bhauti kañca katham saṃpratipattitaḥ ye dharmāḥ sa ha bhāvena ālambanam saṃpratipadyante na anyatama vaikalyena tad yathā cittam caitasikāḥ ca katham puṣṭitaḥ pūrva bhāvitānām kuśala akuśala avya akṛtānām dharmāṇām yā apara ante uttarottarā puṣṭatarā puṣṭatamā pravṛttiḥ katham paripanthataḥ yā kleśānām anyatama bhāvanayā anyatama prabandha puṣṭi dṛḍhīkāraḥ nirvāṇa santāna dūrīkaraṇāya katham parigrahataḥ akuśalāḥ kuśala sa āsravāḥ ca dharmāḥ ātma bhāva parigrahāya katham samanantarataḥ nairantarya samanantarataḥ  api sa bhāga visa bhāga citta caitta utpatti samanantarataḥ  api samanantara pratyayaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ katham ālambanataḥ paricchinna viṣaya ālambanataḥ  api aparicchinna viṣaya ālambanataḥ  api acitrīkāra viṣaya ālambanaḥ api sa citrīkāra viṣaya ālambanataḥ  api sa vastu śikṣā ālambanataḥ  api avastuka viṣaya ālambanataḥ  api vastu ālambanataḥ  api parikalpa ālambanatā api viparyasta ālambanataḥ  api aviparyasta ālambatopi sa vyāghāta ālambanataḥ  api avyāghāta ālambanataḥ  api ālambana pratyayaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ katham adhipatitaḥ pratiṣṭhā adhipatītaḥ  api āvedha adhipatitaḥ  api sahabhāva adhipa titaḥ api viṣaya adhipatitaḥ  api prasava adhipatitaḥ  api sthāna adhipatitaḥ  api phala upabhoga adhipatitaḥ  api laukika viśuddhi dhipatitaḥ  api loka uttara viśuddhi dhipatitaḥ  api adhipati pratyayaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ katham sabhāga tad sa bhāgam kati sabhāga tad sa bhāgāni kimartham sabhāga tad sa bhāga parīkṣā vijñāna avirahita tad sādṛśya indriya viṣaya prabandha utpattitaḥ  api vijñāna virahita sva sādṛśya prabandha utpattitaḥ  api sabhāga tad sa bhāgam draṣṭavyam rūpa skandha eka deśaḥ pañca rūpīṇi dhātu āyatanāni vijñāna yukta ayukta ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham upāttam kati upāttāni kimartham upātta parīkṣā vedanā utpatyāśraya rūpa ta upāttam draṣṭavyam rūpa skandha eka deśaḥ pañca rūpīṇi dhātu āyatanāni   caturṇām ca eka deśaḥ deha vaśa varttyā tmā abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham indriyam kati indriyāṇi kimartha bhindriya parīkṣā viṣaya grahaṇa adhipatitaḥ  api kuśala prabandha adhipatitaḥ  api nikāya sa bhāga sthān adhipatitaḥ  api śubha aśubha karma phala bhoga adhipatitaḥ  api laukika vairāgya adhiā upatitaḥ  api loka uttara vairāgya adhipatitaḥ  api indriyam draṣṭavyam vedanā skandhaḥ  vijñāna skandha rūpa saṃskāra skandha eka deśaḥ dvādaśa dhātavaḥ ṣaṣ āyatanāni dharmadhātu āyatana eka deśaḥ ca ātma adhipati abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham duḥkha duḥkha tā kati duḥkha duḥkhatāni kimartham duḥkha duḥkha tā parīkṣā duḥkha vedanā svalakṣaṇataḥ api duḥkha vedanīya dharma sva lakṣaṇataḥ api duḥkha duḥkha tā draṣṭavyā sarvepām eka deśaḥ duḥkhita ātmā abhiniveśa tyāja na artham katham viparīṇa āma duḥkha tā kati viparīṇa āma duḥkhatāni kimartham vipariṇāma duḥkha tā parīkṣā sukha vedanā vipariṇati sva lakṣaṇataḥ api sukha vedanīya dharma vipariṇati sva lakṣaṇataḥ api tatra ca anunaya citta vipariṇatitaḥ  api vipariṇāma duḥkha tā draṣṭavyā sarvepām eka deśaḥ sukhita ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham saṃskāra duḥkha tā kati saṃskāra duḥkhatāni kimartham saṃskāra duḥkha tā parīkṣā aduḥkha asukha vedanā sva lakṣaṇataḥ  api aduḥkha asukha vedanīya svadharma lakṣaṇataḥ api tad ubhaya dauṣṭhulya parigrahataḥ  api dvaya avinirmokṣa anitya anubandha ayogakṣemataḥ  api saṃskāra duḥkha tā draṣṭavyā skandhānām trayāṇām dhātūnām dvayoḥ ca āyatanayoḥ eka deśam sthāpayitvā sarvāṇi aduḥkha asukha ātmabhiniveśa tyājana artham katham sa vipākam kati sa vipākāni kimartham sa vipāka parīkṣā akuśalam kuśala sa āsravam ca sa vipākam draṣṭavyam skandhānām daśānām dhātunām caturṇām ca āyatanānām eka deśaḥ skandha upanikṣepaka pratisaṃghāyaka ātma abhiniveśa tyājana artham vipākaḥ punar ālaya vijñānam sa saṃprayogam draṣṭavyam tad anyat tu vipāka jam katham āhāraḥ kati āhārāḥ kimartham māhāra parīkṣā pariṇatitaḥ  api pāriṇāmikaḥ viṣayataḥ  api vaiṣayikaḥ āśayataḥ  api āśi ḷ śayi kaḥ upādānataḥ  api upādānikaḥ āhāraḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ trayāṇām skandhānām ekādaśānām dhātūnām pañca anāñca āyatanānām eka deśaḥ āhāra sthitika ātmabhiniveśa tyajana artham api khalu āhāraḥ  aśuddhā śraya sthitikaḥ śuddha aśuddha āśraya sthitikaḥ śuddha āśraya sthitikaḥ sthiti sāṃdarśinakaḥ ca draṣṭavyaḥ katham sa uttaram kati sa uttarāṇi kimartham sa uttara parīkṣā saṃskṛtatas  asaṃskṛta eka deśataḥ ca sa uttaram draṣṭavyam dharmadhātu āyatana eka deśam sthāpayitva sarvāṇi ātma dravya hīna abhiniveśa tyājana artham katham anuttaram kati anuttarāṇi kimartham anuttara parīkṣā asaṃskṛta eka deśataḥ anuttaram draṣṭavyam dharmadhātu āyatana eka deśaḥ ātma dravya agra abhiniveśa tyājana artham iti anena nayena apramāṇaḥ prabheda nayaḥ api khalu samāsatas  skandha dhātu āyatanānām prabhedaḥ trividhaḥ parikalpita lakṣaṇa prabhedaḥ vikalpita lakṣaṇa prabhedaḥ dharmatā lakṣaṇa prabhedaḥ ca tatra parikalpita lakṣaṇa prabhedaḥ katamaḥ skandha dhātu āyataneṣu ātma iti vā sattvaḥ  jīvaḥ  jantuḥ poṣaḥ  pugdalaḥ  manujaḥ  mānava iti vā yad parikalpyate vikalpita lakṣaṇa prabhedaḥ katamaḥ tāni eva skandha dhātu āyatanāni dharmatā lakṣaṇa prabhedaḥ katamaḥ teṣu eva skandha dhātu āyataneṣu ātma abhāvaḥ sattva jīva jantu poṣa pugdala manuja mānavānām abhāvaḥ nairātmya astitā api khalu caturvidhaḥ prabhedaḥ lakṣaṇa prabhedaḥ prakāra prabhā ivā ākṣaya prabhedaḥ santati prabhedaḥ ca lakṣaṇa prabhedaḥ katamaḥ pratyekam skandha dhātu āyatanānām sva lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ prakāra prabhedaḥ teṣām eva skandha dhātu āyatanānām dravyam antar  prajñaptimantaḥ saṃvṛtimantaḥ parama artham antar  rūpiṇaḥ  arūpiṇaḥ sa nidarśanā anidarśanā iti evamādi yathā nirddiṣṭaḥ āśraya prabhedaḥ katamaḥ yāvantaḥ sattva āśrayā stāvanti skandha dhātu āyatanāni santati prabhedaḥ katamaḥ pratikṣaṇam skandha dhātu āyatānānām pravṛttiḥ lakṣaṇa prabhede kuśalaḥ kim parijānāti ātma abhiniveśam parijānāti prakāra prabhede kuśalaḥ kim parijānāti piṇḍa saṃjñām parijānāti āśraya prabhede kuśalaḥ kim parijānāti akṛta abhyāgama kṛta vipraṇāśa saṃjñām parijānāti santati prabhede kuśalaḥ kim parijāti sthira saṃjñām parijānāti api khalu ṣaḍvidhaḥ prabhedaḥ eṣām eva skandha dhātu āyatananām bahirmukha prabhedaḥ antarmukha prabhedaḥ āyata kāla bhedaḥ paricchinna kāla prabhedaḥ tad kāla prabhedaḥ saṃdarśana prabhedaḥ ca bahirmukha prabhedaḥ katamaḥ yad bhūyasā kāmāvacara prabhedaḥ antarmukha prabhedaḥ katamaḥ sarvāḥ sāma adhi bhūmayaḥ āyata kāla prabhedaḥ katamaḥ pṛthagjanānām paricchinna kāla prabhedaḥ katamaḥ śaikṣāṇām sthāpayitvā cara makṣaṇe skandha dhātu āyatanāni tad anyāni aśaikṣāṇām tad kāla prabhedaḥ katamaḥ aśaikṣāṇām cara makṣaṇe skandha dhātu āyatanāni saṃdarśana prabhedaḥ katamaḥ buddhānām pārami prāptānām bodhisattvānām mahāsattvānām ca sa nidarśanāni skandha dhātu āyatanāni 0 atha mahāyāna abhidharma samuccaya śāstre mūla vastuni saṃgraha paricchedaḥ  dvitīyaḥ saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ saṃgraha ekādaśavidhaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ lakṣaṇa saṃgrahaḥ dhātu saṃgrahaḥ jāti saṃgrahaḥ avasthā saṃgrahaḥ sahāya saṃgrahaḥ deśa saṃgrahaḥ kāla saṃgrahaḥ eka deśa saṃgrahaḥ sakala saṃgrahaḥ itaretara saṃgrahaḥ parama artha saṃgrahaḥ ca lakṣaṇa saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ skandha dhātu āyatanānām pratyekam sva lakṣaṇena eva tad tad saṃgrahaḥ dhātu saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ skandha dhātu āyatanānām vīja bhūtena ālaya vijñānena tad tad dhātu saṃgrahaḥ jati saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ skandha dhātu āyatanānām vilakṣaṇānām api skandha dhātu āyatanaiḥ anyaḥ anya saṃgrahaḥ avasthā saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ sukha avasthānām skandha dhātu āyatānānām sva lakṣaṇena saṃgrahaḥ duḥkha avasthānām aduḥkha asukha avasthānām api avasthām upādāya sahāya saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ rūpa skandhaḥ tad anyaiḥ skandhaiḥ anyaḥ  ayam sahāyataḥ sahāyaiḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ evam tad anye skandhā dhātava āyatanāni ca deśa saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ pūrva diś āśritānām skandha dhātu āyatanānām sva lakṣaṇena saṃgrahaḥ evam tad anya diśām api skandha dhātu āyatanānām veditavyam kāla saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ atītānām skandha dhātu āyatanānām sva lakṣaṇena saṃgrahaḥ anāgatānām pratyutpannānām api skandha dhātu āyatanānām eka deśa saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ yāvantaḥ  dharmāḥ skandha dhātu āyatanaiḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ teṣām anyatama saṃgraha eka deśa saṃgrahaḥ  veditavyaḥ sakala saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ yāvantaḥ  dharmāḥ skandha dhātu āyatanaiḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ teṣām aśeṣatas  saṃgrahaḥ sakala saṃgrahaḥ  veditavyaḥ itaretara saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ rūpa skandha saṃgrahe kati dhātavaḥ kati āyatanāni daśānām eka deśaḥ vedanā skandha saṃgrahe kati dhātavaḥ kati āyatanāni eka deśaḥ yathā vedanā skandhaḥ tathā saṃjñā saṃskāra skandhau vijñāna skandha saṃgrahe kati dhātavaḥ kati āyatanāni sapta dhātava ekam āyatanam cakṣuḥ dhātu saṃgrahe kati skandhaḥ kati āyatanāni rūpa skandha ekadeśa ekam āyatam cakṣuḥ dhātuvat  śrotra dhrāṇa jivhākāya rūpa śabda gandha rasa spraṣṭavya bhrātavaḥ manaḥ dhātu saṃgrahe kati skandhāḥ kati āyatanāni ekaḥ skandha ekam āyatanam dharmadhātu saṃgrahe kati skandhāḥ kati āyatanāni trayaḥ skandhā rūpa skandha ekadeśa ekam āyatanam cakṣuḥ vijñāna dhātu saṃgrahe kati skandhāḥ kati āyatanāni vijñāna skandhām anaāyatanayoḥ eka deśaḥ cakṣuḥ vijñānavat  śrotra ghrāṃṇa jivhā kāya manaḥ vijñāna dhātavaḥ cakṣuḥ āyatana saṃgrahe kati skandhāḥ kati dhātavaḥ rūpa skandha ekadeśa ekaḥ  dhātuḥ ca yathā cakṣuḥ āyatanam tayā śrotra ghrāṇa jihvā kāya rūpa śabda gandha rasa spraṣṭa vya āyatanāni manaā āyatana saṃgrahe kati skandhāḥ kati dhātavaḥ ekaḥ skandhaḥ sapta dhātavaḥ dharma āyatana saṃgrahe kati skandhāḥ kati dhātavaḥ trayāṇām skandhānā meka deśa ekaḥ  dhātuḥ ca tadvat  tad anye dharmāḥ skandha dhātu āyatanaiḥ nirdṛśyante anye ca na skandha dhātu āyatanaiḥ nirddiśyante yathā dravyam antar  prajñā āptimantaḥ saṃvṛtimantaḥ parama artham antaḥ  jñeyā vijñeyā abhijñeyā rūpiṇaḥ  arūpiṇaḥ sa nidarśanā anidarśanā iti evamādayaḥ pūrvam nirdṛṣṭāḥ teṣām yathāyogam skandha dhātu āyatanaiḥ itaretara saṃgraheveditavyaḥ parama artha saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ skandha dhātu āyatanānām tathatā saṃgraha kuśalaḥ kam anuśaṃsa labhate ālambane abhisaṃkṣepa anuśaṃsam pratilabhate yathā yathā ālambaneṣu citta abhisaṃkṣepaḥ tathā tathā kuśala mūla abhivṛddhiḥ 0 atha mahāyāna abhidharma samuccaya śāstre mūla vastuni saṃprayoga paricchedaḥ tṛtīyaḥ saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ samāsatas  saṃprayogaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ avinirbhāga saṃprayogaḥ miśrībhāva saṃprayogaḥ samavadhāna saṃprayogaḥ sahabhāva saṃprayogaḥ kṛtya anuṣṭhāna saṃprayogaḥ saṃpratipatti saṃprayogaḥ ca avinirbhāga saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ sarveṣām deśinām paramāṇu paryāpannānām rūpa aṃśikānām anyonyam avinirbhāgaḥ miśrībhāva saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ paramāṇoḥ ūrdhvam sarveṣām deśinām rūpa aṃśikānām parasparam miśrībhāvaḥ samavadhāna saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ deśinām eva samudāyinām rūpa paraṃparāyām samavadhānam sahabhāva saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ ekasmin kāye skandha dhātu āyatanānām saha kāla pravṛttiḥ samam utpatti sthiti nirodhāḥ kṛtya anuṣṭhāna saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ ekasmin kṛtyāṃnuṣṭhāne parasparam saṃprayogaḥ yathā dvayoḥ bhikṣvoḥ anyatara bhikṣoḥ kriyā anuṣṭhāne anyaḥ  ayam saṃprayogaḥ saṃpratipatti saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ citta caitasikānām ekasmin  ālambane anyonyam saṃpratipattiḥ sa saṃpratipatti saṃprayogaḥ punar aneka arthakaḥ yathā para bhāvena saṃprayogaḥ na svabhāvena aviruddhyoḥ saṃprayogaḥ  na viruddhayoḥ sadṛśa kālayoḥ saṃprayogaḥ  avisadṛśa kālayoḥ sa bhāga dhātu bhūmikayoḥ avisa bhāga dhātu bhūmikayoḥ sarvatraga saṃprayogaḥ tad yathā vedanā saṃjñā cetanā sparśa manaskāra vijñānānām api khalu kliṣṭa sarvatragaḥ saṃprayogaḥ  manasi caturṇṇām kleśānām kādācid kaḥ saṃprayogaḥ tad yathā citte śraddhā ādīnām kuśalānām rāga ādīnām ca kleśa upakleśānām āvasthikaḥ saṃprayogaḥ sukhāyāḥ  vedanāyāḥ sa saṃprayogāyāḥ evam duḥkhāyāḥ  aduḥkha asukhāyāḥ avicchinnaḥ saṃprayogaḥ sa cittikāyām avasthāyām vicchinnaḥ saṃprayogaḥ  acittaka samāpatti antaritasya bahirmukhaḥ saṃprayogaḥ  yad bhūyasā kāma pratisaṃyuktānām citta caitasikānām antarmukhaḥ saṃprayogaḥ yad bhūyasā samāhita bhūmikānām citta caitasikānām ucitaḥ saṃprayogaḥ pārthagjanikānām citta caitasikānām tad ekatyānām ca śaikṣā śaikṣāṇām anucitaḥ saṃprayogaḥ loka uttarāṇām citta caitasikā nām ādya tad uttarāṇām loka uttara pṛṣṭha labdhānām ca saṃprayoga kuśalaḥ kam anuśaṃsam pratilabhate cittamātre vedanā ādīnām sāṃkleśikānāṃ vyāvadānikānāñca dharmāṇām saṃprayogam jānāti tad ca jānana ātmā vedayate saṃjānāti cetayate smarati saṃkliśyate vyavadāyate cetayati bhiniveśam prajahāti nairātmyam avatarati atha abhidhama samuccaya śāstre mūla vastuni samanvāgama paricchedaḥ caturthaḥ samanvāgamaḥ katamaḥ lakṣaṇataḥ pūrvavat  tad prabhedaḥ punar  trividhaḥ bīja samanvāgamaḥ vaśitā samanvāgamaḥ samudācāra samanvāgamaḥ ca vīja samanvāgamaḥ katamaḥ kāmadhātau jātaḥ  bhūtaḥ kāma pratisaṃyuktaiḥ kleśa upakleśaiḥ rūpa ārūpya pratisaṃyuktaiḥ ca kleśa upakleśaiḥ vīja samanca āgamena samanca āgataḥ upapatti prātilābhikaiḥ ca kuśalaiḥ rūpa dhātau jātaḥ  bhūtaḥ kāma pratisaṃyuktaiḥ klaiśa upakleśaiḥ vīja samanvāgamena samanvāgataḥ  asamanvāgataḥ ca vaktavyaḥ rūpa pratisaṃyuktaiḥ ārūpya pratisaṃyuktaiḥ ca klaiśa upakleśaiḥ bīja samanvāgamena samanvāgataḥ  asamanvāgataḥ ca vaktavyaḥ ārūpya pratisaṃ yu ktaiḥ kleśa upakleśaiḥ bīja samanvāgamena samanvāgataḥ upapatti prāti lābhikaiḥ ca kuśalaiḥ traidhātu kapratipakṣa lābhī yasya yasya prakārasya pratipakṣa utpannaḥ tasya bīja samanvāgamena asamanvāgataḥ yasya pratipakṣaḥ  na utpannaḥ tasya bīja samanvāgamena samanvāgataḥ vaśitā samanvāgamaḥ katamaḥ prayogikānām dharmāṇām vaśitā samanvāgamena samanvāgataḥ laukikānām loka uttarāṇām vā dhyāna vimokṣa samādhi samāpatti ādīnām tad eka tyājām ca vyākṛtānām samudācāra samanvāgamaḥ katamaḥ skandha dhātu āyatanānām yaḥ  ya eva dharmaḥ saṃmukhībhūtaḥ kuśalaḥ  vā akuśalaḥ  vā avyākṛtaḥ  vā tasya samudācāra samanvāgamena samanvāgataḥ samucchinna kuśala mūlaḥ kuśalānām dharmāṇām bīja samanvāgamena samanvāgataḥ  asamanvāgataḥ ca vaktavyaḥ ātyantikaḥ punar  saṃkleśa samanvāgamaḥ aparinirvāṇa dharmakāṇām icchantikānām draṣṭavyaḥ mokṣa hetu vaikalyāt ātyantika eṣām hetu asamanvāgamaḥ samanvāgama kuśalaḥ kam anuśaṃsam pratilabhate ācaya apacayajñaḥ  bhavati dharmāṇām tathā ācaya apacayajñaḥ  na kasyām cillaukikyām saṃpattau vipattau vā ekāntika saṃjñī bhavati yāvat eva anunaya pratigha prahāṇāya abhidharma samuccaye lakṣaṇa samuccayaḥ  nāma prathamaḥ samuccayaḥ [atha abhidharma samuccaya śāstre viniścaya samuccaye satya paricchedaḥ prathamaḥ ] viniścayaḥ katamaḥ satya viniścayaḥ  dharma viniścayaḥ prāpti viniśca sāṃkathya viniścayaḥ ca satya viniścayaḥ katamaḥ catvāya āri satyāni duḥkham samudayaḥ  nirodhaḥ  mārgaḥ ca duḥkha satyam katasat  tad sattva janma taḥ  janma adhiṣṭa ānataḥ ca veditavyam sattva janma katamat  naraka sattva janma tiryak preteṣu manuṣyeṣu pūrva videheṣu apagodānīyeṣu jāmbūdvīpeṣu uttareṣu kuruṣu deveṣu catur mā hā rājakāyikeṣu trāyastriṃśeṣu yāmeṣu tuṣiteṣu nirmāṇaratiṣu paranirmitavaśavartiṣu brahma purohiteṣu mahā brāhma iṣu parīttā abheṣu pramāṇa ābheṣu ābhāsvareṣu parītta śu bheṣu pramāṇa śubheṣu śubha kṛtsneṣu anabhrakeṣu puṇya prasaveṣu vṛhat phaleṣu saṃjñi sattveṣu abṛheṣu atapeṣu sudṛśeṣu sudarśaneṣu akaniṣṭheṣu ākāśānantyāyataneṣu vijñāna ānantyāyataneṣu ākiñcani āyataneṣu na eva saṃjñāna asaṃjñā yataneṣu janma adhiṣṭhānam katamat  bhājana lokaḥ vāyu maṇḍale apmaṇḍalampratiṣṭhitam ap maṇḍale pṛthivī maṇḍalam pṛthivī maṇḍale sumeruḥ sapta kāñcana parvatāḥ catvāraḥ  dvīpāḥ aṣṭau  antara dvīpāḥ abhyantaraḥ samudraḥ  vāhya samudraḥ catasraḥ sumeru pariṣaṇḍāḥ catur mahā rāja kāyikānām vāpastriṃśānām sthāna antarāṇi cakracāḍaḥ parvataḥ ākāśe vimānāni yāmānām tuṣitānām nirmāṇa ratīnām paranirmita vaśavarttinām devānām rūpāvacarāṇām ca asurāṇām sthāna antarāṇi nārakāṇām sthāna antarāṇi uṣṇa narakāḥ śīta narakāḥ pratyeka narakāḥ ca tad ekatyānām ca tiryak pretānām sthāna antarāṇi yāvat ādityāḥ paricarantaḥ  diśaḥ  avabhāsayante vairocanāḥ tāvat sāhasrake loke sahasram candrāṇām sahasram sūryaṇām sahasram sumerūṇām parvata rājāṇām sahasram caturṇām dvīpānām sahasram catur mahā rāja kāyikānām devānām sahasram trāyastriṃśānām sahasram yāmānām sahasram tuṣitānām sahasram nirmāṇa ratīnām sahasram paranirmita vaśavarttinām sahasram brahmalaukikānām idam ucyate sahasracūḍikaḥ  lokadhātuḥ sahasram sahasra cūḍikānām dhātūnām ucyate dvitīyaḥ  madhyama sāhasraḥ  lokadhātuḥ sahasram madhyama sāhasra dhātūnām ucyate tṛtīyaḥ  mahā sāhasraḥ  lokadhātuḥ evam sa tri sāhasraḥ  mahā sāhasraḥ  lokadhātuḥ mahācakravāḍa parvata maṇḍala pariveṣṭitaḥ sa ca tri sāhasra mahā sāhasraḥ  lokadhātuḥ sa prasaṃvartta vivarttaḥ tathā ca devaḥ cakra ākārān vṛṣṭi vindūn nirantaram niravacchinna mā ākāśāt  varṣati tathā ca pūrvasyām diśi nirantaram niravacchinna mapramāṇaḥ  lokadhātuḥ saṃvarttiṣyate vā vivarttiṣyate vā saṃvarttate vā saṃvṛttaḥ tiṣṭhati vā vivarttate vā vivṛttaḥ tiṣṭhati vā yathā pūrvasyām diśi tathā sarvāsu daśasu dikṣu yaḥ ca sattva lokaḥ  yaḥ ca bhājana lokaḥ karma kleśaḥ janitaḥ karma kleśa ādhipateyaḥ ca sarvam ucyate duḥkha satyam pariśuddha lokadhātuḥ tu na duḥkha satya saṃgṛhīḥtaḥ  na karma kleśa janitaḥ na karma kleśa ādhipateyaḥ ca kevalam mahā praṇidhānena vyavadāna kuśala mūla adhipatinā ākṛṣyate tad utpatti sthānam ca acintyam kevalam buddhena budhyate na dhyāyinām dhyāna gocaraḥ kim punar  cintayatām api khalu duḥkha lakṣaṇa prabhedā aṣṭau  jātiḥ duḥkham jarā duḥkham vyādhi duḥkham maraṇam duḥkham apriya saṃprayogaḥ  duḥkham priya viprayogaḥ  duḥkham yad api icchat   labhate tad api duḥkham saṃkṣiptena pañca upādāna skandhā duḥkham  jātiḥ kim upādāya duḥkham saṃbādha duḥkha tām tad anya duḥkha āśraya tām ca upādāya jarā kim upādāya duḥkham kāle viparīṇati duḥkha tām upādāya vyādhi kim upādāya duḥkham bhūteṣu viparīṇati duḥkha tām upādāya maraṇam kim upādāya duḥkham jīvita vipraṇāśa duḥkha tām upādāya apriya saṃprayogaḥ kim upādāya duḥkham saṃyoga ja duḥkha tām upādāya priya viprayogaḥ kim upādāya duḥkham viprayoga ja duḥkha tām upadāya yad api icchat   labhate tad  kim upādāya duḥkham kāmya phala abhāva ja duḥkha tām upādāya saṃkṣiptena pañca upādāna skandhāḥ kim upādāya duḥkham dauṣṭhulya duḥkha tām upādāya evam aṣṭau saṃgṛhītāni ṣaṣ  bhavanti saṃvādha duḥkham vipariṇati duḥkham saṃprayoga duḥkham viprayoga duḥkham kāmya phala abhāva duḥkham dauṣṭhulya duḥkham ca evam ṣaṣ  bāhulyena aṣṭau bhavanti ṣaṣ  samānāni aṣṭau bhavanti yad uktam tisraḥ  duḥkha tāḥ tāsu aṣṭau duḥkhāni saṃgṛhitāni bhavanti tatra katham tisṛṣu saṃgṛhītāni aṣṭau aṣṭasu vā saṃgṛhītāḥ tisraḥ pāraṃparṣa lakṣaṇa saṃgrahāt  jātiḥ dukham jarā duḥkham vyādhiḥ duḥkham maraṇam duḥkham apriya saṃprayogaḥ  duḥkham iti santāna duḥkha duḥkha tā priya viprayogaḥ  duḥkham yad api icchat   labhate tad api duḥkham tad vipariṇāma duḥkha tā saṃkṣiptena pañca upādāna skandhā duḥkham tad  saṃskāra duḥkha tā yad uktam dvividhe duḥkhe iti tad  saṃvṛti satyena duḥkham parama artha satyena duḥkham ca katamat  saṃvṛti satyena duḥkham katamat  parama artha satyena duḥkham jātiḥ duḥkham yāvat  yad api icchat    labhate tad api duḥkham iti saṃvṛti satyena duḥkham yad uktam saṃkṣiptena pañca upādāna skandhā duḥkham iti parama artha satyena duḥkham duḥkha satyasya sāmānya lakṣaṇam katamat  anitya lakṣaṇam duḥkha lakṣaṇam śūnya lakṣaṇam anātma lakṣaṇam ca anitya lakṣaṇam katamat  samāsatas  dvādaśavidham asat lakṣaṇam vināśa lakṣaṇam vipariṇati lakṣaṇam viyoga lakṣaṇam sannihita lakṣaṇaṃdharmatā lakṣaṇam kṣaṇa lakṣaṇam prabandha lakṣaṇam vyādhi ādi lakṣaṇam citta citta ākāra vṛtti lakṣaṇam bhoga saṃpattiḥ vipatti lakṣaṇam bhājana loka saṃvartta vivartta lakṣaṇam asat lakṣaṇam katamat  skandha dhātu āyataneṣu sarva kāli kātma ātmīyatā nitya abhāvaḥ vināśa lakṣaṇam katamat  saṃskārāṇām utpannānām nirodhaḥ taktālam bhūtvā abhāvaḥ vipariṇati lakṣaṇam katamat  saṃskārāṇām anyathā bhāvaḥ prabandhā sādṛśyena pravṛttiḥ viyoga lakṣaṇam katamat  saṃskāreṣu vaśitva bhraṃśaḥ paraiḥ svīkaraṇam vā sannihita lakṣaṇam katamat  samupasthitā anitya tā yad tadānīm eva anubhūyamāna anitya tā dharmatā lakṣaṇam katamat  āgāminī anitya tā yāma avaśyam anubhaviṣyati kṣaṇa lakṣaṇam katamat  saṃskārāṇām kṣaṇāt ūrddham anavasthānam prabandha lakṣaṇam katamat  anādimati saṃskāre utpanna niruddhā na am prabandhā prahāṇam vyadhyādi lakṣaṇa katamat  caturṇām bhūtānām kāla upabhogaḥ jīvita vipariṇāmaḥ citta citta ākāra vṛtti lakṣaṇam katamat  kadācid  sārāgam cittam saṃbhavati kadācid  vīta rāgam cittam saṃbhavati yadvat  sa dveṣam vā vīta dveṣam vā sa moham vā vīta moham vā saṃkṣiptam vā vihisām vā nimnam vā unnatam vā uddhatam vā anuddhatam vā upaśāntam vā anupaśāntam vā samāhita vā asamāhitam vā evamādi citta saṃsāra vṛttiḥ bhoga saṃpatti vipatti lakṣaṇam katamat  saṃpattīnām ante vipattiḥ vināśaḥ bhājana loka saṃvartta vivartta lakṣaṇam katamat  agni ambu vāyubhiḥ trividhaḥ saṃvartta vivarttaḥ tisṛṇām saṃvarttarnānām śīrṣāṇi dvitīya tṛtīya caturtha dhyānāni caturtha dhyāne vāhyānām vimānānām tu vāhya abhāvat eva saṃvartta vivarttaḥ kevalam taiḥ devaiḥ tāni vimānāni saha nirvarttante saha nirudhyante etad ucyate saṃvartta vivarttaḥ api khalu trayaḥ  antara kalpāḥ durbhikṣa vyādhi śastraiḥ bhavanti hīnasya trividha kalpā asya ante taiḥ śastra ādibhiḥ niryāṇam bhavati yadālokadhātuḥ saṃvṛttaḥ  bhavati ekaḥ  antara kalpa prathamaḥ apakarṣaḥ eka antara kalpaḥ paścima utkarṣaḥ aṣṭādaśa antara kalpā utkarṣa apakaya evam ca viṃśatim antara kalpān lokadhātuḥ saṃvarttate viṃśati mātara kalpāt  lokadhātuḥ vivarttate viṃśatim antara kalpān lokadhātuḥ vivṛttaḥ tiṣṭhati saṃkalikāḥ ca ete aśītiḥ antara kalpā ekaḥ  mahākalpaḥ  bhavati tayā kalpa saṃkhyāyāḥ  rūpārūpya ācarāṇām devānām āyuḥ pramāṇam varṇyate yad uktam anyatare  sattvā āyuḥ kṣayāt  vā puṇya kṣayāt  vā karma kṣayāt  vā tasmāt adhiṣṭhānāt cyavante iti tatra āyudāyaḥ katamaḥ kāle maraṇam puṇya kṣayaḥ katamaḥ akāle maraṇam apuṇya maraṇam yena sattvā āsvāda samāpattyām rajyante puṇya kṣayāt ca hetoḥ te jīvitāt cyavante karma kṣayaḥ katamaḥ upapadya vedanīya karmaṇaḥ apara paryāvedanīya karmaṇaḥ ca ubhayaḥ kṣayāt maraṇa duḥkha lakṣaṇam katamat  tisraḥ  duḥkha tāḥ aṣṭākā vā duḥkham ṣaṣ ākāram vā duḥkham bāhulyena pūrvam uktam tad  duḥkham nāma kim pratītyasūtre uktam yad anityam tad  duḥkham iti ubhaya aṃśikīm anitya tām pratītya duḥkha lakṣaṇam prajñāyate utpāda aṃśikīm anitya tām pratītya duḥkha duḥkha tā prajñāyate vyayāṃśikīm anitya tām pratītya vipariṇāma duḥkha tā prajñāyate ubhaya aṃśīkim anitya tām pratītya saṃskāra duḥkha tā prajñāyate tathā ca saṃskāra anitya tām saṃskāra vipariṇāma tām ca saṃdhāya uktam bhagavatā mayā yad kiṃcid  veditam idam atra duḥkhasya iti api khalu utpāda vyaya dharma dvaya anugateṣu saṃskāreṣu jātyādayaḥ  aṣṭau duḥkhāni prajñāyante iti abhisaṃdhāya buddhena bhāṣitam yad anityam tad  duḥkham iti api ca anityeṣu saṃskāreṣu jāti ādikam duḥkham prajñāyate iti anityataḥ  duḥkham na sarve saṃskārā iti atra ādhisandhiḥ veditavyaḥ śūnyatā lakṣaṇam katamat  teṣu tasya abhāvaḥ anena nayena samanupaśyanā śūnyatā punar  teṣu anyasya bhāvaḥ anena nayena yathā bhūta jñāna bhāvaḥ etad  vatāra śūnyatā ucyate yathā bhūta jñānam aviparītaḥ  arthaḥ teṣu abhāvaḥ katamaḥ skandha dhātu āyataneṣu nitya dhruva kūṭa sthā vipariṇāma dharma ātma ātmīya abhāvaḥ anena nayena teṣām śūnyatā teṣu anyasya bhāvaḥ katamaḥ te ṣu eva nairātmyam tad ca ātmanaḥ  na astitā anātmanaḥ  astitā satī śūnyatā etad abhisaṃdhāya uktam bhagavatā sataḥ  yathābhūta jñānam bhāvaḥ asataḥ  yathā bhūta jñānam abhāvaḥ api khalu trividhā śūnyatā svabhāva śūnyatā tathā abhāva śūnyatā prakṛti śūnyatā ca ādyā parikalpitā draṣṭavyā tṛtīyā pariniṣpanna svabhāvā draṣṭavyā anātma lakṣaṇam katamat  yathā ātma vāde sthitasya ātma lakṣaṇasya skandha dhātu āyataneṣu tad lakṣaṇasya abhāvaḥ skandha dhātu āyataneṣu ātma lakṣaṇa abhāva tām upādāya idam ucyate anātma lakṣaṇam etad abhisaṃghāya uktam bhagavatā sarve dharmā anātmāna iti api ca uktam bhagavatā na etad  sarvam mama na eṣaḥ aham asmi na me sa ātmā iti evam etam yathābhūtam saṃprajñāya draṣṭhavyam iti tasya kaḥ  artha  uktaḥ bahis dhāvastabhisaṃdhāya uktam na etad  sarvam mama iti kuta etad  bahis dhāvastuni kalpita ātmīya lakṣaṇam atas  ātmīya niṣkarṣaṇam adhyātma vastuni parikalpita ātma ātmīya lakṣaṇam ata ātma ātmīya ubhaya niṣkarṣaṇam pūrvam uktam anityam kṣaṇa lakṣaṇam iti tad  katham jñāyate yathā citta caitasikānām kṣaṇika tā tathā rūpa ādīnām api kṣaṇika tā draṣṭavyā citta upātta tām upādāya citta eka yogakṣema tām upādāya citta vikāra tad vikāra tām upādāya citta āśraya tām udāpādāya citta ādhipatya saṃbhūta tām upādāya cittva śava rttinām ca upādāya api khalu atyanta vikāra upālabdhi tām upādāya utpannasya ca anapekṣya pratyayam svarasa vināśi tām upādāya rūpasya api kṣaṇika tā draṣṭavyā yad uktam yad kiṃcid rūpam sarvantad catvāri mahābhūtāni catvāri ca mahābhūtāni upādāya iti tad kim sandhāya uktam saṃbhavam sandhāya uktam eka deśa āśrayībhāva artha  upādāya arthaḥ yatra punar  samudāye yad bhūtam upalabhyate tad tatrā stiti vaktavya asti ekabhautikaḥ asti dvi bhautikaḥ asti yāvat sārvabhautikaḥ upādāya rūpe api yad upādāya rūpam yasmin samudāya upalabhyate tad tatra asti iti veditavyam yad punar ūcyate paramāṇu saṃcittaḥ  rūpa samudāya iti tatra niḥśarīraḥ paramāṇuḥ veditavyaḥ buddhyā paryanta prabhedataḥ tu paramāṇu vyavasthānam piṇḍa saṃjñā vibhāghana tām upādāya rūpe dravyāḥ pariniṣpatti praveśatām ca upādāya tad  punar etad  duḥkham asti vipulam asaṃlikhitam saṃlikhitam saṃlikhitā saṃlikhitam ca asti madhyama saṃlikhitam asti tanu kam asaṃlikhitam asti tanuttaram saṃlikhitam asti tanutamam saṃlikhitam asti aduḥkham duḥkha pratibhāsam mahāsaṃlekha pratyupasthānam ca katamat vipulam duḥkham asaṃlikhitam yad kāma avacaram anupacita kuśala mūlānām katamat saṃlikhitam tad eva utpanna mokṣa bhāgīyānām katamat saṃlikhita asaṃlikhitam tad eva laukika vairāgyāya avaropita kuśala mūlānām katamat madhyama saṃlikhitam rūpa dhātu upapannānām vivarjita mokṣa bhāgīyānām katamat tanu kam asaṃlikhitam ārūpya upapannānām vivarjita mokṣa bhāgīyānām katamat tanuttaram saṃlikhitam yad śaikṣāṇām katamat tanutamam saṃlikhitam yad aśaikṣāṇām jīvita indriya pratyayam ṣaṣ āyatanam katamada duḥkham duḥkha pratibhāsam mahāsaṃlekha pratyupasthānam yad pārami prāptānām bodhisattvānām acintya bhava upapattiṣu yad uktam maraṇam duḥkham iti tatra maraṇam trividham kuśala cittasya avyākṛta cittasya ca paṭuke citta prakāre sva kuśala mūla balā dhānataḥ  vā para upasaṃhāra taḥ  vā kuśala cittasya maraṇam draṣṭavyam paṭuka eva citta prakāre svā kuśala mula bala ādhā nataḥ  vā para upasaṃhāra taḥ  vā akuśala cittasya maraṇam draṣṭavyam paṭuke vā citta prakāre apaṭuke vā tad ubhaya vai kalyāt abhisaṃskāra asamarthasya vā avyākṛta cittasya maraṇam draṣṭavyam śubha kāriṇaḥ adhaḥkāya stat prathamatas  śītībhavati aśubha kāriṇaḥ punar  ūrdhvaṃkāyaḥ śītībhavati tatra aśubha kāriṇaḥ  antarā abhavaḥ  abhinirvarttate tad yathā kṛṣṇasya kutapasya nirbhāsaḥ  andhakāra tamisrāyā vā rātryāḥ aśubha kāriṇaḥ tad yathā śuklasya parasya nirbhāsa jyotsnāyā vā rātryāḥ antarā abhavaḥ kāmadhātau rūpa dhātau ca upapadyamānasya arūpa dhātoḥ cayamānasya sa ca manaḥ mayaḥ  gandharva iti api param sapta aham tiṣṭhati antareṇa cyavate ekadā ca vyāvarttate tatrasthaḥ ca karma upacinoni sa bhāgān  ca sattvān paśyati yatra ca upapadyate tad ākṛtiḥ apratihata gatiḥ ca ṛddhimān iva vā āśu gāmī upapatti āyatane pratihanyate upapatti āyatane tulā avanāma unnāma yogena cyavate pratisandhi ca vadhnāti antarā abhava sthaḥ ca upapatti āyatane rāgam utpādayati yad anyaḥ ca kleśaḥ pratyayaḥ bhavati saha rāgeṇa antarā abhavaḥ  nirudhyate kalalam ca sa vijñānakam utpadyate sa ca vipākaḥ tata ūrdhvam indriya abhinrivṛttiḥ yathā pratitya samutpāde catṛ sṛṣva ayoniṣu aṇḍa jāyām jarayujāyām saṃsveda jāyām upapadukāyañca 0 atha viniścaye satya paricchede pratheme dvitīyaḥ  bhāgaḥ samudaya satyam katamat
