kleśaḥ kleśa adhipateyañca karma prādhānya nirddeśaḥ tu ḷ śāstu bhagavatā tṛṣṇā paunarbhavikī nandī rāga sahagatā tatra tatra abhinandinī samudaya satyanirdeśena nirdiṣṭā prādhānya arthaḥ katamaḥ yaḥ sarvatraga arthaḥ sarvatraga arthaḥ katamaḥ tatha hi tṛṣṇā vastu sarvatragā avasthā sarvatragā adhva sarvatragā dhātu sarvatragā eṣaṇā sarvatragā prakāra sarvatragā ca keśaḥ katamaḥ parisaṃkhyānataḥ  api lakṣaṇataḥ  api utthāna taḥ api ālambanataḥ  api saṃprayogataḥ  api paryāyataḥ  api vipratipattitaḥ  api dhatutaḥ api nikāyataḥ  api prahāṇataḥ  api kleśaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ parisaṃkhyānam katamat  ṣaḍ  kleśā daśa vā ṣaḍ  kleśāḥ katamat  rāgaḥ pratighaḥ  mānaḥ  avidyā vicikitsā dṛṣṭiḥ ca ta eva dṛṣṭeḥ pañcākārja bhedena daśa bhavanti lakṣaṇam katamat  yaḥ  dharma utpadyamānaḥ  apraśānta lakṣaṇa utpadyamānena yena kāya citta prabandhā praśama pravṛttiḥ idam kleśa lakṣaṇam utthānam katamat  kleśa anuśayaḥ ca aprahīṇaḥ  bhavati kleśa sthānīyaḥ ca dharma ābhāsa gataḥ  bhavati tatra ca ayaḥ niśaḥ manaskāraḥ pratyavasthitaḥ  bhavati evam kleśa utpadyate idam ucyate utthānam ālambanam katamat  sarva kleśa prayogaḥ sarva kleśa ālambanam sarva kleśa vastu ālambanam ca api khalu kāma avacaraḥ kleśaḥ sthāpayitvā avidyā dṛṣṭi vicikitsām ca tad anyaḥ urdhva bhūmi anālambanaḥ ūrdhva bhūmikaḥ kleśaḥ adhas bhūmi anālambanaḥ tad bhūmitaḥ  vīta rāga tvāt  nirodha mārga satyā lambanaḥ kleśaḥ  nirodha marga ālambanānabhiśliṣṭaḥ tad parikalpaḥ tu asya ālambanam iti ucyate kleśaḥ punar dvividhaḥ avastuka ālambanaḥ sa vastuka ālambanaḥ ca avastuka ālambanaḥ katamaḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ  dṛṣṭi saṃprayuktāḥ ca dharmāḥ tad anyaḥ sa vastuka ālambana iti ucyate saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ rāgaḥ pratighena na saṃprayujyate pratighavat vicikitsayā api na saṃprayujyate śiṣṭeṣu saṃprayogaḥ  labhyate yathā rāgaḥ tathā pratighaḥ  api draṣṭavyaḥ pratighaḥ  rāgeṇa mānena dṛṣṭyā ca na saṃprayujyate mānaḥ pratighena vicikitsayā ca na saṃprayujyate avidyā dvividhā sarva kleśa saṃprayuktā avidyā asāmānyā avidyā asāmānya avidyā katamā satyeṣu ajñānam dṛṣṭiḥ pratighena vicikitsayā ca na saṃprayujyate krodha ādaya upakleśā anyaḥ  anyam na saṃprayujyante āhrīkyam anapatrāpyam ca sarvatra akuśale sāmānyena saṃprayujyete styānam auddhatyam āśraddhyam kausīdyam pramādaḥ ca sarvatra kliṣṭe saṃprayujyate paryāyaḥ katamaḥ sarva kleśā nānā artha āśrayā na anavasthāḥ paryāyāḥ saṃyojanam bandhanam anuśayaḥ upakleśaḥ paryavasthānam oghaḥ yogaḥ upādānam granthaḥ nivaraṇam khilaḥ malaḥ nighaḥ śalyaḥ kiṃcanaḥ duścaritam āsravaḥ vighātaḥ paridāhaḥ raṇaḥ jvaraḥ vanasaḥ vibandhaḥ saṃyojanāni kati katham saṃyojanam kutra saṃyojanam saṃyojanāni nava anunaya saṃyojanam pratigha saṃyojanam māna saṃyojanam avidyā saṃyojanam dṛṣṭi saṃyojanam parāmarśa saṃyojanam vicikitsā saṃyojanam īrṣyā saṃyojanam mātsarya saṃyojanam ca anunaya saṃyojanam katamat  traidhātukaḥ  rāgaḥ anunaya saṃprayojanena saṃprayuktaḥ traidhātukam na udvejayati anudvegena kuśala samudācāraḥ kuśalāsam udācāraḥ ca tena āyatyām duḥkha abhinivṛttaḥ  duḥkhena saṃyujyate pratigha saṃyojanam katamat  sattveṣu duḥkhe duḥkha sthānīyeṣu na dharmeṣu cittasya vihiṃsā pratigha saṃyojanena saṃprayuktaḥ  pratigha nimitteṣu cittam na upekṣate anupekṣayā ca akuśala samudācāraḥ kuśalāsam udācāraḥ ca tena āyatyām laukika duḥkha abhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate māna saṃyojanam katamat  sapta mānāḥ mānaḥ  atimānaḥ  mānatimānaḥ  asmimān aḥ  abhimāna ūna mānaḥ  mithyāmānaḥ ca mānaḥ katamaḥ hīnān śreyān asmi sadṛśena sadṛśaḥ  asmi iti vā yā cittasya unnatiḥ atimānaḥ katamaḥ sadṛśāt  śreyān asmi śreyasā sadṛśaḥ  asmi iti vā yā cittasya unnatiḥ māna atimānaḥ katamaḥ śreyasaḥ śreyān asmi iti yā cittasya unnatiḥ asmimānaḥ katamaḥ pañca su upādāna skandheṣu ātma ātmīya abhiniveśa ādyā cittasya unnatiḥ abhimānaḥ katamaḥ aprāpta uttare viśeṣā dhik ame prāptaḥ  mayā iti yā cittasya unnatiḥ ūna mānaḥ katamaḥ vahu antara viśiṣṭāt alpa antara hīnaḥ  asmi iti yā cittasya unnatiḥ mithyāmānaḥ katamaḥ aguṇavataḥ  guṇavān asmi iti yā cittasya unnatiḥ māna saṃyojanena saṃprayukta ātma ātmīyau na saṃjānāti asaṃjñānāt  ātma ātmīya grahaḥ akuśala samudācāraḥ kuśalā samudācāraḥ ca tena āyatyām duḥkha abhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate avidyā saṃyojanam katamat  traidhātukam ajñānam avidya saṃyojanena saṃprayuktā duḥkha dharmān samudaya dharmān na adhyavasyati anadhyavasāyena akuśala samudācāraḥ kuśalāsam udācāraḥ ca tena āyatyām laukika duḥsva abhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate dṛṣṭi saṃyojanam katamat  tisraḥ  dṛṣṭhayaḥ sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ antā grāha dṛṣṭiḥ mithyāḥdṛṣṭiḥ ca dṛṣṭi saṃyojanena saṃprayuktaḥ  mithyā niḥsaraṇam parikalpita vipratisāram paryeṣane abhiniviśate mithyā niḥsaraṇa abhiniveśena akuśala samudācāraḥ kuśalāsam udācāraḥ ca tena āyatyām laukika duḥkha bhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate parāmarśa saṃyojanam katamat  dṛṣṭi parāmarśaḥ śīla vrata parāmarśaḥ ca parāmarśa saṃyojanena saṃprayuktaḥ  mithyā niḥsaraṇa upāyam kalpayati abhiniviśate mithyā niḥsaraṇa upāyāmi niveśena akuśala samudācāraḥ kuśalāsam udācāraḥ ca tena āyatyām laukika duḥkha abhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate vicikitsā saṃyojanam katamat  satyeṣu vimatiḥ vicikitsā saṃyojanena saṃprayuktaḥ  buddha dharma saṃgheṣu ratneṣu vicikitsate ratnatrayam na samudāvarati ratna traya asam udācāreṇa akuśala samudācāraḥ kuśala asanudācāraḥ ca tena āyatyām laukika duḥkha abhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate īrṣyā saṃyojanam katamat  lābha satkāra adhyavasitasya para saṃpattau  amarṣa kṛtaḥ cetasaḥ  vyāroṣaḥ īrṣyā saṃyojanena saṃprayuktaḥ  lābha satkārān anunayati dharmam na gurukaroti lābha satkāra guru kāreṇā kuśala samudācāraḥ kuśalāsam udācāraḥ ca tena āyatyām laukika duḥkha bhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate mātsarya saṃyojanam katamat  lābha satkāra adhyavasitasya pariṣkāreṣu cetasa āgrahaḥ mātsarya saṃyojanena saṃprayukta upacayam anunayati ta dvarjana tām ca na satkaroti upacaya anunayena akuśala samudācāraḥ kuśalāsam udācāraḥ ca tena āyatyām laukika duḥkha bhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate bandhanam trividham rāga bandhanam dveṣa bandhanam moha bandhanam ca rāga bandhanena sattvānām viparīṇa āma duḥkha tāyām bandhanam dveṣa bandhanena sattvānām duḥkha duḥkha tāyām bandhanam moha bandhanena sattvānām saṃskāra duḥkha tāyām bandhanam apica rāga dveṣa mohāt niśritya kuśala samudācāreṣu na vaśa varttitām labhate ata ucyate bandhanam anuśayāḥ sapta kāma rāga anuśayaḥ pratigha anuśayaḥ bhava rāga anuśayaḥ māna anuśayaḥ avidyā anuśayaḥ dṛṣṭayanu śayaḥ vicikitsā anuśayaḥ ca kāma rāga anuśayaḥ katamaḥ kāma rāga pakṣīyam dauṣṭhulyam pratigha anuśayaḥ katamaḥ pratigha pakṣīyam dauṣṭhulyam bhava rāga anuśayaḥ katamaḥ rūpārūpya rāga pakṣīyam dauṣṭhulyam māna anuśayaḥ katamaḥ māna pakṣīyam doṣṭhulyam avidyā anuśayaḥ katamaḥ avidyā pakṣīyam dauṣṭhulyam dṛṣṭi anuśayaḥ katamaḥ dṛṣṭi pakṣīyam dauṣṭhulyam vicikitsā anuśayaḥ katamaḥ vicikitsā pakṣīyam dauṣṭhulyam kāma eṣāṇāyā aviratasya kāma rāga pratigha anu śayau  anuśayāte bhaveṣaṇāyāḥ  aviratasya bhava rāga anuśayaḥ  anuśete mithyā brahmacarya eṣaṇāyāḥ  aviratasya māna avidyā dṛṣṭi vicikitsā anuśayā anuśerate te sattvā hīna pratipakṣam labhante madaḥ  mānaḥ ca utpadyate ārya satyeṣu saṃmohaḥ ca mithyāmokṣam mokṣa upāyam ca saṃtorayanti buddha śāsana dharma vinayeṣu vimatiḥ vicikitsā ca upakleśaḥ tu ya kleśāḥ te upakleśā api bhavanti upakleśāḥ tu na kleśāḥ kleśān sthāpayitvā tad anyaḥ kliṣṭaḥ saṃskāra skandha saṃgṛhītaḥ sarvaḥ caitasikaḥ  dharmaḥ sa punar  katamaḥ ṣaṣ rāga ādīn kleśān sthāpayitvā kliṣṭaḥ saṃskāra skandha saṃgṛhītaḥ krodha ādikaḥ caitasikaḥ  dharmaḥ api khalu rāgaḥ  dveṣaḥ  mohaḥ ca caitasikā upakleśā ucyante yaiḥ citte upakleśaḥ  na vairāgyam na viumokṣaḥ  na āvaraṇa prahāṇam ata ucyante upakleśāḥ tathā ca bhagavatā uktam dīrgharātram vaḥ  rāga dveṣa mohā upakliśyantui vikṣipanti citram saṃkliśyanti paryavasthānāni aṣṭau styānam middham auddhatyam kaukṛtyam īrṣyā mātsarya māhikyam anapatrāpyam ca punar  punar  udvegena cittam paryayanahyanti iti paryavasthānāni tathā ca śamatha pragraha nimitta bhāvanā kāle tad sanniśraya brahmacaryā diśuddhi saṃgṛhīta śīla kāle cittam paryavanahyanti oghaḥ caturvidhaḥ kāma oghaḥ mava oghaḥ dṛṣṭcoghaḥ avidya oghaḥ ca strotaḥ  anukūlaḥ pravāha āvartta ogha arthaḥ saṃkeśa anvayataḥ ādyaḥ kāma eṣaṇā bhāvanā dvitīyaḥ bhava eṣaṇā bhāvanā aparau  ubhau mithyā brahmacarya eṣaṇā bhāvanā āśraya āśrita saṃbandha yogena yogaḥ caturvidhaḥ kāma yogaḥ bhava yogaḥ dṛṣṭi yogaḥ avidyā yogaḥ ca visaṃyoga paripantha karaḥ yoga arthaḥ viśuddhi viparyayataḥ te punar yathāyoga meṣaṇā traya bhāvanā upādānāni catvāri kāma upādānam dṛṣṭi upādānam śīla vrata upādānam ātma vāda upādānam ca vivāda mūla upādānam paunarbhavikopa ādānam ca upādānam draṣṭavyam tena kim bhavati kāma rāga vibandha gredhā saṃkleśa hetunā gṛhiṇaḥ  anyaḥ  anyam vivadanti tad u vivāda mūlam prathamam upādanam dṛṣṭi rāga vibandha gredhā saṃkleśa hetunā pravrajitā anyaḥ  anyam vivadanti tad  vivāda mūlam aparam upādāna trayam dvāṣaṣṭiḥ dṛṣṭi gatayaḥ dṛṣṭi upādānam na anā āvṛta śīlaiḥ kṛcchram tapaḥ śīla vrata upādānam tad āśritā ca sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ ātma vāda upādānam dṛṣṭi śīla vrata upādānābhyām tīrthyā anyaḥ  anyam vivadanti ātma vāda upādāne tu tīrthyā anyaḥ  anyam na vivadanti dhārmikaiḥ sārdham anyaḥ anyam vivadanti evam ca vivāda mūle abhiniveśāt  paunarbhavika duḥkha vipāka upādāna ākṣepāt ca upādānāni ucyante granthāḥ catvāraḥ abhidhyākāya granthaḥ vyāpāda kāya granthaḥ śīla vrata parāmarśa kāya granthaḥ tad satya abhiniveśa upādāna kāya granthaḥ ca samāhita manaḥ svabhāvasya kāyasya parigrantha arthena granthaḥ  veditavyaḥ tena kim bhavati caturvidham cittam vikṣipyate vitta ādiṣu anunaya hetoḥ cittam vikṣipyate vivādaḥ tuṣu apratipatti hetoḥ cittam vikṣipyate duṣkara śīla vrata duḥkha hetoḥ cittam vikṣipyate ayaḥ niśaḥ jñeya santi īraṇa hetoḥ cittam vikṣipyatee nivaraṇāni pañca kāma  chanda nivaraṇam vyāpāda nivaraṇam styānam iddha nivaraṇam auddhatya kaukṛtya nivaraṇam vicikitsā nivaraṇam ca kuśala pakṣasya asaṃprakhyānam nivaraṇam draṣṭavyam tad ca pravrajyāyām abhiratau codanāyām pratipattau śamathe pragrahe upekṣāyām ca khilaḥ trividhaḥ rāgakhilaḥ  dveṣakhilaḥ  mohakhilaḥ ca rāga dveṣa mohāt niśritya pūrva abhyāsena rāga ādi caryā pariniṣpādanam cittasya adānta tayā akarmaṇyatayā durvimokṣa tayā ca sattvaiḥ tasyāḥ caryāyāḥ  durbhedya tvāt  khila iti ucyate malāḥ trayaḥ rāgamalaḥ  dveṣa malaḥ  moha malaḥ ca tad ca rāga dveṣa mohāt niśritya dauśīlam tad  saṃprajā anabdiḥ sabrahmacāribhiḥ grāme vā araṇye vā tathā kurvantam paśyadbhiḥ ucyate ayam khalu āyuṣmān karoti evam kṛtyam carati evam ācaritam grāmakaṇṭaka āmiṣaḥ  aśuciḥ atas  malā nāma nighāḥ trayaḥ rāga nighaḥ dveṣa nighaḥ mohanighaḥ ca rāga dveṣa mohāt niśritya dīrgha kālam punar  punar jāti maraṇeṣu vilaśyante iti ucyante nighāḥ śalyāḥ trayaḥ rāga śalyaḥ  dveṣa śalyaḥ  moha śalyaḥ ca rāga dveṣa mohāt niśritya bhave bhava upakaraṇeṣu vā adhyeṣaṇā samutpādena prabandhān upacchedena buddhe dharme saṃghe duḥkha samudaya nirodha mārgeṣu vā vicikitsā samutpādena vā śalyā nāma kiṃcanāḥ trayaḥ rāga kiṃcanaḥ dveṣa kiṃcanaḥ moha kiṃcanaḥ ca rāga dveṣa mohāt niśritya vitta saṃcayeṣu sa bhayāḥ sa vairā bhūyaḥ vihāra vikṣepāḥ kiṃcanā nāma duścaritāni trīṇi rāga duścaritam dveṣa duścaritam moha duścaritam ca rāga dveṣa mohāt niśritya kāya vāc manaḥ duścaritāni caranti iti duścaritāni iti ucyate punar  rāga dveṣa mohāt niśritya utpannānām bahūnām akuśala duścaritānām akuśala mūla tvena tribhiḥ vyavasthānam tad  katham sattvā loke āmiṣa kiṃcid kahataḥ  caranti loke apakāra nimitta parikalpa hatoḥ duścaritam caranti loke mithyā dharma abhiniveśa hetoḥ duścaritam caranti iti te rāga dveṣa mohā duścaritāni akuśala mūlāni āsrava asrayaḥ kāma āsravaḥ  bhava āsravaḥ  avidyā sravaḥ ca citta avesāram stratam kurvantī tyāsravāḥ iti ucyante te punar  katham bahirdhā visāram niśritya kāma āsravaḥ antardhā visāram niśritya bhava āsravaḥ tad ubhaya āśraya visāram niśritya avidyā sravaḥ vighātāḥ trayaḥ rāga vighātaḥ  dveṣa vighātaḥ  moha vighātaḥ ca rāga dveṣa mohāt niśritya bhave pariṣkareṣu vā eṣaṇā abhāve vighāte sarvadā dāridya duḥkha ādibhiḥ kliṣṭā bhavanti iti vighātāḥ paridāhāḥ trayaḥ rāga paridāhaḥ  dveṣa paridāhaḥ  moha paridāhaḥ ca rāga dveṣa moha sanniśrayeṇa ayaḥ niśaḥ nimitta abhiniveśaḥ  anuvyañjana abhiniveśaḥ ca tena nimitta anuvyañjana abhiniveśena kāyam cittam ca paridahanti iti paridāhāḥ upāyāsāḥ trayaḥ rāga upāyāsaḥ  dveṣa upāyāsaḥ  moha upāyasaḥ ca rāga dveṣa moha sanniśrayeṇa tatra tatra ratiḥ adhyavasānam ca tad vipariṇāme śoka paridevanā duḥkha daurmanasya upāyasaiḥ spṛṣṭā bhavanti iti u pāyāsāḥ raṇāḥ trayaḥ rāgaraṇaḥ  dveṣa raṇaḥ  moha raṇaḥ ca rāga dveṣa moha sanniśrayeṇa śastra ādāna daṇḍa ādibhiḥ raṇayanti nānāvidham bhaṇḍanam kalaham kurvanti iti rāgādayaḥ  raṇā ucyante jvarāḥ trayaḥ rāga jvaraḥ  dveṣa jvaraḥ  moha jvaraḥ ca rāga dveṣa moha sanniśrayeṇa adharma rāgeṇa mahā dahanena paridahanti viṣama lobhena mahā dahanena paridahanti mithyā adharmeṇa mahā dahanena paridahanti iti jvarā nāma vanasāḥ trayaḥ rāga vanasaḥ  dveṣa vanasaḥ  moha vanasaḥ ca rāga dveṣa moha sanniśrayeṇa jāti maraṇa mūleṣu saṃskāreṣu saṃyojayanti saṃjanayanti sattvān nānāvidha kāyeṣu pañcagati saṃsāreṣu abhinirvarttayanti iti rāgādayaḥ  vanasā iti ucyante vibandhāḥ trayaḥ rāga vibandhaḥ  dveṣa vibandhaḥ  moha vibandhaḥ ca rāga dveṣa moha sanniśrayeṇa kāya sa apekṣatā vitta sa apekṣa tā bodhya bhāvaḥ kolāhala ratiḥ paritta kuśala dharma lābhe api santoṣaḥ taiḥ kuśala dharmān na bhāvayanti iti vibandhāḥ ucyante evamādayaḥ kleśa arthānām paryāyā apramāṇāḥ vipratipattiḥ katamā rāgaḥ pratighaḥ ca dvau kleśau viṣaye dṛṣṭau ca vipratipannau mānaḥ sattveṣu dṛṣṭau ca vipratipannaḥ sat kāya anta grāha mithyā dṛṣṭayaḥ jñeye vipratipannāḥ dṛṣṭi parāmarśa śīla vrata parāmarśau dṛṣṭau vipratipannau vicikitsā pratipakṣe vipratipannā avidyā sarvatra vipratipannā daśa kleśā duḥkhe samudaye ca vipratipannāḥ tad nidāna pada sthānataḥ punar  daśa kleśā nirodhe mārge ca vipratipannāḥ taiḥ tatra utrāsa saṃjana nataḥ dhātu katamaḥ pratigham sthāpayitvā tad anye sarve traidhātuka pratisaṃyuktāḥ pratighaḥ tu kāmadhātu pratisaṃyuktaḥ api khalu rāgaḥ kāmadhātau sukha saumanasya upekṣābhi saṃprayujyate yathā kāmadhātau tathā prathama dvitīya dhyānayoḥ tṛtīya dhyāne sukha upekṣābhyām saṃprayujyate tad ūrdhvam upekṣayā saṃprayujyate pratighaḥ  duḥkha daurmanasya usukha upekṣābhiḥ saṃprayujyate mānaḥ kāmadhātau saumanasya upekṣābhiḥ saṃprayujyate prathama dvitīya dhyāna yaḥ sukha saumanasya upekṣābhiḥ saṃprayujyate tṛtīya dhyāne sukha upekṣābhyām saṃprayujyate tad ūrdhvam upekṣayā eva saṃprayujyate yathā mānaḥ tathā sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ anta grāha dṛṣṭiḥ dṛṣṭi parāmarśaḥ śīla vrata parāmarśaḥ ca mithyādṛṣṭiḥ kāmadhātau daurmanasya saumanasya upekṣābhiḥ saṃprayujyate rūpa dhātā vārupya dhātau ca yathā veditam saṃprayujyate vicikitsā kāmadhātau dauramanasya upekṣābhyām saṃprayujyate rūpa dhātau  ārūpya dhātau ca yathā veditam saṃprayujyate avidyā dvividhā saṃprayuktā asāmānyā ca sarva kleśa saṃprayogataḥ saṃprayuktā avidyā yathā veditam saṃprayujyate āsāmānyā avidyā kāmadhātau daurmanasya upekṣābhyām saṃprayujyate tad ūrdhva dhātau yathā veditam saṃprayujyate katham sarva kleśā upekṣayā saṃprayujyante sarva kleśānām audāsīnyam āgamya asta gamana tām upādāya api khalu rāgaḥ kāmadhātau ṣaṣ vijñāna kāyikaḥ yathā rāgaḥ tathā pratighaḥ  avidyā ca rāgaḥ  rūpa dhātau catur vijñāna kāyikāḥ ārūpya dhātau manaḥ vijñāna kāyikaḥ yathā rāgaḥ tathā avidyā mānaḥ  dṛṣṭiḥ vicikitsā ca sarvatra manaḥ vijñāna kāyikāḥ api khalu rāgaḥ pratighaḥ  mānaḥ ca kāmadhātau vastu eka deśa pravṛttikāḥ kāmadhātuvat  rūpa dhātau  ārūpya dhātau  api śiṣṭāḥ kleśāḥ sarvatra sarva vastu pravṛttikāḥ nikāyaḥ katamaḥ dvau kleśa nikāyau darśana prahāta vyanikāyaḥ  bhāvanā prahāta vyanikāyaḥ ca darśana prahātavya nikāyaḥ punar caturvidhaḥ duḥkha darśana prahātavya nikāyaḥ samudaya darśana prahātavya nikāyaḥ nirodha darśana prahātavya nikāyaḥ mārga darśana prahāta vyanikāyaḥ ca kāmadhātau duḥkha darśana prahātavyā daśa kleśāḥ duḥkha darśana prahāta vyavat  samudaya darśana prahātavyāḥ nirodha darśana prahātavyā mārga darśana prahātavyāḥ ca rūpa dhātau duḥkha ādi caturvidha darśana prahātavyāḥ pratyekam nava kleśāḥ sthāpayitvā pratigham rūpa dhātuvat ārūpya dhātau  api evam ca darśana prahāta vya kleśanikāyā dvādaśa adhikam śatam kleśāḥ kāmadhātau bhāvanā prahātavyāḥ ṣaṣ kleśāḥ sahajā sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ anta prāha dṛṣṭiḥ rāgaḥ pratighaḥ  mānaḥ  avidyā ca rūpa dhātau bhāvanā prahātavyāḥ pañca kleśāḥ sthāpayitvā pratigham rūpa dhātuvat ārūpya dhātau  api evam ca bhāvanā prahāta vyanikāyāḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ kleśāḥ prahāṇam katamat  tathā paryāya prahāṇam tena manaskāreṇa prahāṇam tasmāt  pratilambhāt  prahāṇam tathā paryāya prahāṇam katamat  parijñānataḥ parivarjanataḥ pratipakṣa lābhataḥ ca parijñānam katamat  tad nidāna vastu parijñānam svabhāva parijñānam ādīnava parijñānam ca parivarjanam katamat  tad kāla utpanna sya anādānam pratipakṣa lābhaḥ katamaḥ anutpannasya anutpādata utpannasya varjanataḥ  vā pratipakṣa lābha mārgaḥ tena manaskāreṇa prahāṇam kīdṛśena manaskāreṇa kim prajahāti asaṃbhinna ālambanena manaskāreṇa sarva dharmā anātmāna iti paśyati anitya ākārā iti kleśān prajahāti anitya ākāra parikarmataḥ tasmāt  pratilambhāt  prahāṇam kasmāt  pratilambhāt  prajahāti na atītāt niruddhataḥ na anāgatāt anutpannataḥ na pratyutpannāt  asahabhāvataḥ kevalam kleśa dauṣṭhulya pratilambhāt  prajahāti iti prahāṇam yathā yathā dauṣṭhulyam utpadyate tathā tathā pratipakṣa utpadyate yathā yathā pratipakṣa utpadyate tathā tathā dauṣṭhulya nirodhaḥ samam samam yathā loke jyotiḥ utpadyate tamaḥ ca nirudhyate tad visaṃyogataḥ  yadā anāgata kleśaḥ  anutpanna dhamaṣu avatiṣṭhate tad  prahāṇam ucyate kleśa ādhipateyam karma katamat  cetanā karma cetayitvā karma ca sarvam karma lakṣaṇam nāma punar  karma pañcavidham upalabdhi karma kāritra karma vyavasāya karma pariṇati karma prāpti karma ca asmin  tu arthe yad  bhūyasā vyavasāya karma abhipretam cetanā karma katamat  puṇya karma apuṇya karma āniṃjya karma ca cetayitvā karma katamat  kāya karma vākkarma manaskarma ca tāni trīṇi kāya vāc manaskarmāṇi akuśalāni kuśalāni ca akuśalāni katamāni daśa akuśala karma pathāḥ prāṇa atipātaḥ adatta ādānam kāma mithyā ācāraḥ mṛṣāvādaḥ piśuna vāc  paruṣa vāc  saṃbhinna pralāpaḥ abhidyā vyāpādaḥ mithyādṛṣṭiḥ ca kuśalāni katamāni daśa kuśala karma apathāḥ prāṇa atipātāt  viratiḥ adatta ādānāt viratiḥ kāma mithyā ācārāt viratiḥ mṛṣāvādāt viratiḥ piśuna vācaḥ  viratiḥ paruṣa vācaḥ  viratiḥ saṃbhinna pralāpāt viratiḥ anabhidhyā avyāpādaḥ samyak dṛṣṭiḥ ca apica prāṇa atipāta ādīnām yathāyogam pañca lakṣaṇa prabhedāḥ vastutas  āśayataḥ prayogataḥ kleśataḥ niṣṭhā gamanataḥ ca yad uktam sūtre cetanā karma katamāni cetanā karmāṇi parājñapti saṃcetanīya tā karma parama saṃjñapti saṃcetatīyatā karma avijñāya saṃcetanīya tā karma mūla abhiniveśa sa cetanīya tā karma viparyāsa saṃcetanīya tā karma ca teṣu mūla abhiniveśa saṃcetanīya tā karma viparyāsaṃcetana yatā karma ca teṣu mūla abhiniveśa saṃcetanīya tā karma viparyāsa saṃceta nīya tā karmabhyām yadi kṛtam bhavati upacitam ca na na asya vipākaḥ pratisaṃvedyate kṛtam samudācāra samutthāpitam upacitam ca vāsanā samupacitam yadu uktam sūtre niyata vedanīyam karma iti katame niyaptāḥ karma kiyā niyamaḥ vipāka pati saṃvedanā niyamaḥ avasthā niyamaḥ ca tad na daśānām akuśalānām karma pathānām vipāka phalam triṣu apāyeṣu mṛdū madhya adhimātrāṇām tiryak preta narakeṣu vipākaḥ nipyanda phalam pratyekam tad ānurūpyeṇa manuṣyeṣu upanannānā mā ātma bhāva parigrahayoḥ vipattiḥ adhipati phalam pratyekam tad ānurūpyeṇa eva vāhyānām bhāvānām vipattiḥ yathā uktam sūtre daśānām kuśalānām karma pathānām vipāka phalam deva manuṣyam atiṣu upapadyamānānām deveṣu manuṣyeṣu vā vipākaḥ niṣyanda phalam tad āyataneṣu pratyekam tad ānurūpyeṇa ātma abhāva parigrahayoḥ saṃpattiḥ abhinirvarttate adhipatti phalam tad āyataneṣu pratyekam tad ānurūpyeṇa eva vāhyānām bhāvānām saṃpattiḥ abhinirvarttate kuśalānām akuśalānām ca karmaṇām sugatau durgatau ca vipākaḥ  abhinirvarttate tad ca ākṣepakeṇa karmaṇā paripūrakeṇa ca karmaṇā ākṣepakam karma katamat  yena phala vipākaḥ  abhinirvarttate paripūrakam karma katamat  yena upapanna iṣṭa aniṣṭa phalam vedayate yena ekena karmaṇā ekam ātma bhavana ākṣipati vā anekena karmaṇā ekam ātma bhāvam ākṣipati vā anekena karmaṇā anekam ātma bhāvam ākṣipati vā ekaḥ sattvaḥ  anekena karmaṇā samanvāgataḥ tatra vipāka phala vedanāyāḥ kaḥ kramaḥ kāye yad  audārikam pūrvam pacyate cyuti kāle pratyupasthitam vā pūrvam bahulīkāra tām gatam vā atrasamācaritam vā tad vipākaḥ pūrvam pacyate yad uktam sūtre trividham karma puṇya karma apuṇya karma āniṃjya karma ca puṇya karma katamat  kāma pratisaṃyuktam kuśalam karma apuṇya karma katamat  akuśalam karma āniṃjya karma katamat  rūpārūpya pratisaṃyuktam kuśalam karma yad uktam sūtre avidyā ālambanāḥ saṃskārāḥ puṇya aniṃjyā apuṇya aniṃjyāḥ ca iti katame puṇya aniṃjyā avidyā ālambanāḥ saṃskārā utpadyante dvividhaḥ saṃmūḍhaḥ phala vipāka saṃmūḍhaḥ tattva artha saṃmūḍhaḥ ca phala vipāka saṃmūḍhasya apuṇyāḥ saṃskārāḥ tattva artha saṃmūḍhasya puṇya aniṃjyāḥ saṃskārāḥ prāṇa atipātasya karma pathasya lobha dveṣa mohaiḥ prayogaḥ dveṣeṇa eva niṣṭhā prāṇa atipātavat  paruṣa vāc avyāpādayoḥ api karma pathayoḥ adatta ādānasya karma pathasya lobha dveṣa mohaiḥ prayogaḥ lobhena eva niṣṭhā adatta ādānavat  kāma mithyā ācāra abhidhyayoḥ karma pathayoḥ mṛṣāvādasya karma pathasya lobha dveṣa mohaiḥ prayogaḥ trayāṇām anyatamena niṣṭhā mṛṣāvādavat  saṃbhinna pralāpa piśuna vācoḥ karma pathayoḥ mithyā dṛṣṭeḥ karma pathasya rāga dveṣa mohaiḥ prayogaḥ mohena eva niṣṭhā yad uktam sūtre sādhāraṇam karma asādhāraṇam karma valavat karma durvalam karma ca sādhāraṇam karma katamat  yad karma bhājana loke nānāvidham vikalpam karoti asādhāraṇam karma katamat  yad karma sattva loke nānavidham vikalpam karoti api ca sattvānām anyonya ādhipateyam karma api yena karma balena sattvānām anyonya adhipati pratyayaḥ proktaḥ teṣām anyonya adhipatibalataḥ tad api ucyate sādhāraṇam karma yatas  sūtre uktam yathā sattva anāmānyaiḥ sattvaiḥ saha anyonyam darśana ādikam na upabhogaḥ  na upalabdhiḥ balavat karma katamat  pratipakṣa balavat pugdalasya saṃcetanīyam akuśalam karma pratipakṣa vala viskā ambhaṇena vedanīya naraka karma pravṛtteḥ dṛṣṭa dharma vedanāyāḥ pariniṣpādanam dṛṣṭa dharma vedanīya naraka karma pravṛtteḥ anutpādaḥ yena tad karma balavat iti ucyate prātipakṣika karma balavataḥ sarvam saṃcetanīyam kuśalam karma balavat iti ucyate tad karma niśritya uktam bhagavatā mama ārya śrāvakā apramāṇa vaipulya karmaṇi cittam kuśalam paribhāvayanti abhisaṃskṛte sa pramāṇe karmaṇi na ākṣipanti na avasthāpayanti na parihāpayanti tad saṃkhyāte yad api pratipakṣa durbala pugdalasya saṃcetanīyam akuśalam karma tad api kuśalāt karmaṇaḥ  balavat iti ucyate yad  punar  saṃcetanīyam karma niyata vipākam aprahīṇam aparijñātam tad  balavat  karma iti ucyate tad manasi nidhāya uktam sarvam ca kuśala akuśalam karma niyata vipākam ārya mārgeṇa prahīṇam balavat  karma iti ucyate yad api kāma pratisaṃyuktam akuśalam karma yad api pūrvam abhyastam yad api pada stham yad api asādhyam abhisaṃskṛtam karma aparinirvāṇa dharmataḥ tad api prakṛtyā balavat  karma iti ucyate kṣetrataḥ  api citta abhisaṃskāra taḥ  api balavat  karma veditavyam punarnavabhiḥ ākāraiḥ balavat  karma veditavyam tad yathā kṣetrataḥ vastutas  svabhāvataḥ āśrayataḥ manasikārataḥ āśayataḥ sahāyataḥ bahulīkā rataḥ bāhu janyatas ca tad viparyeṇa durbalam karma bhagavatā uktam ya evam vadet yathā ayam puruṣa pugdalaḥ karma karoti upacinoti tathā tathā vipākam pratisaṃvedayata iti evam sati brahmacarya bhāsaḥ na bhavati avakāśaḥ ca na prajñāyate samyak  duḥkha kṣayāya duḥkhasya anta kriyāyai yaḥ tu evam vadet yathā ayam puruṣa pugdalaḥ  yathāvedanīyam karma karoti upacinoti tathā tathā yathāvedanīyam vipākam pratisaṃvedayata iti evam sati brahmacarya bhāsaḥ bhavati avakāśaḥ ca prajñāyate samyak  duḥkha kṣayāya duḥkhasya anta kriyāyai iti yad uktam sūtre tatra kaḥ  abhisaṃdhiḥ tatra buddhā manasi evam mithyā vacanam pratiṣeddhum kāmayante yad  sukha sahagatasya karmaṇaḥ sukha sahagata eva vipākaḥ  abhinirvarttate duḥkha sahagatasya karmaṇaḥ  duḥkha sahagata eva vipākaḥ  abhinirvarttate aduḥkha asukha sahagatasya karmaṇaḥ tad sahagata eva vipākaḥ  abhinirvarttate iti evam uktam samyak vacanam tu evam anumanyate sukha sahagatasya karmaṇaḥ sukha vedanīyasya sukha vipākaḥ  anujñāyate duḥkha vedanīyasya duḥkha vipākaḥ  anujñāyate aduḥkha asukha vedanīyasya aduḥkha asukha vipākaḥ  anujñāyate duḥkha sahagatasya karmaṇaḥ sukha vedanīyasya sukha vipākaḥ  anujñāyate duḥkha vedanīyasya duḥkha vipākaḥ  anujñāyate aduḥkha asukha vedanīyasya aduḥkha asukha vipākaḥ  anujñāyate aduḥkha asukha sahagatasya karmaṇaḥ sukha vedanīyasya sukha vipākaḥ  anujñāyate duḥkha vedanīyasya duḥkha vipākaḥ  anujñāyate aduḥkha asukha vedanīyasya aduḥkha asukha vipākaḥ  anujñāyate eṣaḥ  abhisandhiḥ tatra sūtre api khalu karma prabhedaḥ trividhaḥ saṃvara karma asaṃvara karma na eva saṃvaranā saṃvara karma ca saṃvara karma katamat  prātimokṣa saṃvara saṃgṛhītam karma dhyāna saṃvara saṃgṛhītam karma anāsrava saṃvara saṃgṛhītam karma ca prātimokṣa saṃvara saṃgṛhītam karma katamat  sapta saṃgha upapannānām saṃvarāḥ bhikṣu saṃvaraḥ bhikṣuṇī saṃvaraḥ śikṣam āṇavasaṃvaraḥ śrāmaṇeḥ asaṃvaraḥ śrāmaṇerī saṃvaraḥ upāsaka saṃvaraḥ upāsikā saṃvaraḥ upavāsa saṃvaraḥ ca katamam puc dalam adhikṛtya pravrajita saṃvaraḥ  vyavasthāpitaḥ duścarita viveka caritam kāma viveka caritam puc dalam adhikṛtya kam puc dalam adhikṛtya upāsaka upāsikā saṃvaraḥ  vyavasthāpitaḥ duścarita viveka caritam adhikṛtya naḥ tu kāma viveka caritam pugdalam kam puc dalam adhikṛtya upavāsa saṃvaraḥ  vyavasthāpitaḥ na eva duścarita viveka caritam na kāma viveka caritam puc dalam adhikṛtya upāsakānām ekatyānām śikṣāsyānīyānām śikṣa samavāgama iti ucyate upāsaka saṃvaraḥ  asamanvāgama iti ucyate uktaḥ samanvāgamaḥ śīla vipattiḥ api ucyate yathā ṣaṇḍa paṇḍakānām teṣā mupāsaka saṃvaraḥ pratiṣidhyate na vā teṣām upāsaka saṃvaraḥ  na pratiṣidhyate kevalam teṣām upāsaka tvam pratiṣidhyate bhikṣubhikṣuṇīnām ubhaya pravrajitānām saṃghasya pakṣasya saṃseva upāsana ayogya tvāt  paṇḍakaḥ punar  pañcavidhaḥ jāti paṇḍakaḥ īrṣyā paṇḍakaḥ pakṣa paṇḍakaḥ āsecana kapaṇḍakaḥ āpad paṇḍakaḥ ca dhyāna saṃvara saṃgṛhitam karma katamat  dauḥśīlya samutthāpakānām kleśānām vīja upaghāte sati kāmebhyaḥ  vīta rāgasya yā viratiḥ prathama dhyāna vīta rāgasya yā viratiḥ dvitīya dhyana vīta rāgasya yā viratiḥ tṛtīya dhyāna vīta rāgasya yā viratiḥ sā ucyate dhyāna saṃvara saṃgṛhītam kāya vāc karma anāsrava saṃvara saṃgṛhītam karma katamat  satya darśanena anāsrava manaskāra balena pratilabdhā anāsravā viratiḥ sā ucyate anāsrava saṃvara saṃgṛhītam karma asaṃvara karma katamat  abhijanmataḥ  vā tad karma samādānataḥ vā tad karma adhyācāra niścayaḥ asaṃvara iti ucyate te punar asaṃvarāḥ katame aurabhrikāḥ kaukkṛṭikāḥ śaukarikāḥ śākunikāḥ mātsyikāḥ lubdhakāḥ vāgurikāḥ corāḥ ghātakāḥ gaḥ vaṃdhakāḥ nāga vaṃdhakāḥ māṇḍalikāḥ nāgamaṇḍalikāḥ kārāgārikāḥ sūcakāḥ upaghātakāḥ prabhṛtayaḥ na eva saṃvaranā saṃvara saṃgṛhītam karma katamat  na eva saṃvaranā saṃvara vihāraḥ kuśala akuśalam karma punar  karma prabhedaḥ trividhaḥ sukha vedanīyam karma duḥkha vedanīyam karma aduḥkha asukha vedanīyam karma ca sukha vedanīyam karma katamat  kāma avacarāt  tṛtīya dhyānam yāvat  yad  kuśalam karma duḥkha vedanīyam karma katamat  akuśalam karma aduḥkha asukha vedanīyam karma katamat  tṛtīya dhyānāt ūrdhvam yad  kuśalam karma karma prabhedaḥ punar trividhaḥ dṛṣṭa dharma vedanīyam karma upapadya vedanīyam karma apara paryāya vedanīyam karma ca dṛṣṭa dharma vedanīyam karma katamat  tad karma dṛṣṭe dharme yasya vipākaḥ  vipacyate tad ca maitrī samāpatteḥ uccalitasyam parihāṇim vṛddhim vā kurvataḥ dṛṣṭe dharme vipākaḥ  labhyate yathā maitrī samāpatteḥ uccalitasya tathā araṇa samāpatteḥ uccalitasya niurodha samāpatteḥ uccalitasya strotāpatti phalāt uccalitasya arhattva phalāt uccalitasya ca buddha pramukhe saṃghe kuśalam akuśalam ca kurvataḥ dṛṣṭe dharme vipākaḥ  labhyate anyeṣām tīvra āśaya prayogeṇa kuśala akuśala karma pratipannānām api dṛṣṭe dharme vipākaḥ  labhyate upapadya vedanīyam karma katamat  tad karma anantare janmani yasya vipākaḥ  vipacyate tad yathā paṃcana antarya karmāṇi api ca yāni anyāni kuśala akuśalāni karmāṇi yeṣām anantare janmani vipākaḥ  vipacyate tad sarvam ucyate upapadya vedanīyam karma apara paryāya vedanīyam karma katamat  tad karma yasya anantara janmanaḥ  apara paryāyeṣu vipākaḥ  vipacyate tad ucyate apara paryāya vedanīyam karma punar  karma prabhedaḥ caturvidhaḥ kṛṣṇam kṛṣṇa vipākam karma śuklam śukla vipākam karma kṛṣṇa śuklam kṛṣṇa śukla vipākam karma akṛṣṇa śukla avipākam vyāmiśram karma kṛṣṇam kṛṣṇa vipākam karma katamat  akuśalam karma śuklam śukla vipākam karma katamat  traidhātukam kuśalam karma kṛṣṇa śuklam kṛṣṇa śukla vipākam karma katamat  kāma pratisaṃyuktam karma yad  karma vā āśayataḥ prayogataḥ  vā śuklam yad  karma vā prayogataḥ kṛṣṇam āśayataḥ śuklam akṛṣṇa śukla avipākam vyāmiśram karma katamat  prayoga ānantarya mārge anāsravam karma aviśeṣeṇa ca sarvasya anāsrava karmaṇaḥ paripantham ānukūlya svabhāvam adhikṛtya vaṃka doṣa kaṣāyāṇām śauceyānām mauneyānām ca karmaṇām yathākramam vyavasthānam veditavyam tathā ca dānāni śauceyāni karmāṇi dāna karma katamat  nidānataḥ utthānataḥ pradeśataḥ svabhāvataḥ ca dāna karma vikalpyate nidānam alobhaḥ  adveṣaḥ  amohaḥ ca kuśala mūlāni utthānam tāni eva cetanā sahagatāni pradeśaḥ  deyāni vastūni svabhāvaḥ  dāna saṃpatti kāle kāya vāc manaskarmāṇi dāna saṃpad  katamā abhīkṣṇa dānataḥ apakṣapāta dānataḥ icchā paripūraṇa dānataḥ ca dāna saṃpad veditavyā api ca aniśrita dānataḥ mahā śuci dānataḥ parama  prahṛṣṭa dānataḥ abhikṣṇa dānataḥ kṣetra bhājana dānataḥ nava purāṇa saṃvibhāga dānataḥ ca dāna saṃpad veditavyā deya saṃpad  katamā anabhiduta deya vastutas  apara apakṛta deya vastutas  akuthita vimala deya vastutas  śuci deya vastutas  dharma arjita deya vastutas ca deya saṃpad  veditavyā tathā ca uktam sūtre śīla samanvāgataḥ prātimokṣa saṃvara saṃvṛta ācāra gocara saṃpannaḥ  aṇu mātreṣu avadyeṣu mahābhaya darśī śikṣate śikṣā padeṣu iti katham śīla samanvāgataḥ  bhavati viśuddha śīlanupkṣaṇa upapannataḥ katham prātimokṣa saṃvara saṃvṛtaḥ  bhavati nairyāṇika śīla saṃdhāraṇataḥ katham ācāra gocara saṃpannaḥ  bhavati viśuddha śīla sahabhāvataḥ  agarhitānām katham aṇu mātreṣu avadyeṣu mahābhaya darśī bhavati tīvreṇa gauraveṇa śīla śikṣaṇataḥ katham śikṣate śikṣā padeṣu śikṣā śīlānām śikṣaṇataḥ atas  param śīlam ārabhya yad  buddhena sūtreṣu nirdṛṣṭam kāyena saṃvṛtaḥ  bhavati iti evamādi katham ucyate kāyena vācā saṃvṛtaḥ  bhavati saṃprajanya parigṛhītatas katham kāya vāc saṃpattyā saṃpannaḥ  bhavati āpatti anāpatti dānataḥ katham pariśuddha kāya vāc samudācāraḥ  bhavati avipratisāra ādīnām krameṇa saṃpratipattyā yāvat  samādhi lābha sanniśraya taḥ katham kuśala kāya vāc samudācāraḥ  bhavati kliṣṭa vitarka vyavatīrṇataḥ katham anavadyakāya vāc samudācāraḥ  bhavati mithyā praṇidhi parivarjanena brahmacarya bhāvanātaḥ katham avyāvadhya kāya vāc samudācāraḥ  bhavati pareṣām anavajñayā sukha saṃvāsataḥ katham ānulomikāyavāk samudācāraḥ  bhavati nirvāṇa prāpti anukūlataḥ katha manucchavika kāya vāc samudācāraḥ  bhavati kuśalasya cchādanataḥ akuśalasya prakāśanataḥ ca katham aupayika kāya vāc samudācāraḥ  bhavati sa brahmacarya grahaṇa śīlataḥ katham pratirūpa kāya vāc samudācāraḥ  bhavati guruṣu guru sthānīyeṣu ca anihita mānataḥ katham pradakṣiṇa kāyāya vāk samudācāraḥ  bhavati avavāde pradakṣiṇa prāhitatas katham atapta kāya vāc samudācāraḥ  bhavati kaṣṭa pohī na adhimukti vivarjitatas katham atanu tāpi kāya vāc samudācāraḥ  bhavati samutsṛṣṭa bhoga karmāntā vipratisāritaḥ katham avipratisārikāya vāk samudācāraḥ  bhavati alpa mātreṇa asaṃtuṣṭā vipratisāritayā yad uktam bhagavatā yathā sattvāḥ karmasvakā karma dāyādāḥ karma yonīyāḥ karma pratisaraṇāḥ karma sarvān sattvān vibhajati ucca nīca tayā hīna praṇīta tayā iti katham sattvāḥ karmasvakā bhavanti svayaṃkṛta karma nipāka pratisaṃvedana ātām upādaya katham karma dāyādā bhavanti svayam kṛta karma vipāka pratisaṃvedana tāyām kuśala akuśalānām karmaṇām anyonya dāyādatām upādāya katham karma yonīyā bhavanti sattvānām mahetu viṣama hetu vivarjita yoni tām upādāya katham karma pratisaraṇā bhavanti pratipakṣa karma viśiṣṭa karma bandhana āśraya tām upādāya katham karmaṇā sattvaḥ  ucca nīcā bhavanti yad  karmaṇā sugatau durgatau vā ātma bhāva prabhedam labhante katham hīna praṇītā bhavanti yad  sattvā guṇa doṣa prabhedena samanvāgatā bhavanti yad uktam bhagavatā sattvānām karma vipākaḥ  acintya iti tatra katham karma vipākaḥ cintyaḥ katham karma vipākaḥ  acintyaḥ kuśalasya karmaṇaḥ  deva manuṣya gati su iṣṭa vipākalā bhaḥ cintyaḥ akuśalasya karmaṇaḥ  hīnāsu tisṛṣu durgatiṣu aniṣṭa vipāka lābhaḥ cintyaḥ ayam cintyaḥ yena karmaṇā sattvānām ātma bhāva vipāka vaicitryam abhunirvarttate saḥ  acintyaḥ tad eva kuśala akuśalam karma sthāna vastu hetu vipāka prakāra ādi prabhedeḥ acintyam vividha vāhya vastu vaicitrya abhinirvarttakam karma acintyam maṇi mantra aupadhi muṣṭi yoga pratisaṃyuktam karma acintyam yoginām prabhāva karma cintyuam bodhisattvānām vaśitābhiḥ kriyamāṇam karmā citnyam tad yathā āyuḥ vaśitayā citta vaśitayā pariṣkāra vaśitayā karma vaśitayā upapatti vaśitayā adhimukti vaśitayā praṇidhāna vaśitayā ṛddhi vaśitayā jñāna vaśitayā dharma vaśitayā evam ca bodhisattvānām mahāsattvānām evamādibhiḥ vaśitābhiḥ yad karma kriyate tad acintyam sarveṣām buddhānām vuddha kṛtya anuṣṭhānam karma acintyam tathā ca samudaya satyam samāsatas  lakṣaṇa prabhedena caturvidham hetu lakṣaṇam samudaya lakṣaṇam prabhava lakṣaṇam pratyalakṣaṇam ca hetu lakṣaṇam katamat  punarbhava vāsanāyā āhārakam kāraṇam hetuḥ iti hetu lakṣaṇam veditavyam samudaya lakṣaṇam katamat  teṣām teṣām upacita vāsanānām sattvānām tasmin  tasmin sattva nikāye udayasya kāraṇam iti samudaya lakṣaṇam veditavyam prabhuva lakṣaṇam katamat  pratyātmam santānānām sarva prakāra prakarṣa udbhavasya kāraṇam iti prabhava lakṣaṇam veditavyam pratyalakṣaṇam katamat  sattva anāṣān paprāpti atyaya kāraṇam iti pratyaya kāraṇam veditavyam atha viniścaye satya paricchede prathame tṛtīyaḥ  bhāgaḥ nirodha satyam katamat  lakṣaṇataḥ gāmbhīryataḥ saṃvṛtitaḥ paramārthataḥ aparipūritaḥ paripūritaḥ niralaṃkārataḥ sa alaṃkārataḥ śeṣatas  aśeṣatas  agratas  paryāyataḥ ca nirodha satyam veditavyam lakṣaṇataḥ katamat  tathatāyām ārya mārge kleśānām anutpādaḥ  yaḥ  nirodha āśrayaḥ  nirodhakaḥ  nirodha svabhāvaḥ  vā tad nirodha satya lakṣaṇam yad uktam bhagavatā cakṣuḥ śrotre ghrāṇa jivhākāyāḥ manaḥ ca teṣu āyataneṣu nāma rūpayoḥ ātyantika nirodhaḥ  na śeṣaḥ iti yad ca uktam tad āyatanam veditavyam yathā cakṣuḥ ca nirudhyate rūpa saṃjñā ca virajyate yāvat  manaḥ ca nirudhyate dharma saṃjñā ca virajyate iti anena nayena ālambanānām prāpaṇam tathatāyām ālambanāt ūrdhvam sa āsravāṇām dharmāṇām nirodhaḥ tad nirodha satya lakṣaṇam gāmbhīryataḥ katamat  yad  teṣām saṃskārāṇām uparamān nirodhaḥ tathā uparamāt  teṣām saṃskārāṇām nirodhaḥ  na anyaḥ  vācyaḥ na ananyaḥ  vācyaḥ na api anyaḥ  na api ananyaḥ  vācyaḥ na na eva anyaḥ  na ananyaḥ  vācyaḥ kutas  niṣprapañcataḥ asmin  tu arthe prapañca utpattiḥ na saṃcintyā na mārgeṇa na nyāyena na kuśala prayogeṇa cintyā iti yad uktam bhagavatā teṣām ṣaṇṇām spraṣṭā vyayatanānām kṣayaḥ  virāgaḥ  nirodhaḥ  vyupaśamaḥ  astaṃgama iti evamādi syāt anyaḥ syāt ananyaḥ syāt anyaḥ  api na anyaḥ  api syāt na eva anyaḥ  na ananyaḥ  api iti niṣprapañca prapañca utpadyate yāvat  ṣaṣ āyatanāni tāvat  prapañcāḥ yadā ṣaṣ āyatanānām nirodhaḥ chedaḥ tadā prapañcānām viratiḥ saṃvṛtitaḥ katamat  laukika mārgaiḥ vīja nigraheṇa yaḥ  nirodhaḥ  labhyate atas  bhagavatā tadā aṃśika nirvāṇam iti ucyate paramārthataḥ katamat  ārya prajñayā bīja nirmūlanena yaḥ  nirodhaḥ  labhyate aparipūritaḥ katamat  śaikṣāṇām strota āpanna phala saṃgraheṇa vā sakṛdāgami phala saṃgraheṇa vā anāgāmi phala saṃgraheṇa vā yaḥ  nirodhaḥ paripūritaḥ katamat  aśaikṣyāṇām arhattva phala saṃgraheṇa yaḥ  nirodhaḥ niralaṃkārataḥ katamat  prajñā vimuktānām arhatām yaḥ  nirodhaḥ sa alaṃkārataḥ katamat  ubhaya bhāga vimuktānām traividyānām ṣaṣ abhijñānām arhatām yaḥ  nirodhaḥ śeṣatas  katamat  sa upadhi śeṣaḥ  yaḥ  nirodhaḥ aśeṣatas  katamat  nirupadhi śeṣaḥ  yaḥ  nirodhaḥ agratas  katamat  buddhānām bodhisattvānām apratiṣṭhita nirvāṇa saṃgraheṇa yaḥ  nirodhaḥ sparśa vihāriṇām sarveṣām sattvānām hita sukha adhiṣṭhānataḥ paryāyataḥ katamat  aśeṣa prahāṇam pratiniḥsargaḥ vyantībhāvaḥ kṣayaḥ  virāgaḥ  nirodhaḥ  vyupaśamaḥ  astaṃgama iti evamādi kim upādāya ucyate aśeṣa prahāṇam pariśiṣṭāni padāni upādāya kim upādāya ucyate pratiniḥsargaḥ paryavasthāna pratiniḥsaraṇa tām upādāya kim upādāya ucyate kṣayaḥ darśana mārgeṇa pratipakṣa visaṃyoga lābha tā mupādāya kim upādāya ucyate virāgaḥ bhāvanā mārgeṇa pratipakṣa visaṃyoga lābha tām upādāya kim upādāya ucyate nirodhaḥ āyatyām tad phala duḥkha anutpatti tām upādāya kim upādāya ucyate vyupaśamaḥ dṛṣṭe dharme tad phala cetta duḥkhā samudācāra tām upādāya kim upādāya ucyate astaṃgamaḥ sa upadhiśeṣa nirodha tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar asaṃskṛtam iti ucyate lakṣaṇa traya viraha tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar durdarśa iti ucyate carma cakṣuṣaḥ  divya cakṣuṣaḥ ca gocarātikamaṇa tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar acalam iti ucyate matiṣu saṃcāra birahamām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar amata miti ucyate tṛṣṇā traya viraha tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar amṛtam iti ucyate skandha māra viraha tām upādāya kim uipādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar anāsravam iti ucyate sarva kleśa māra viraha tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar layanam iti ucyate anavadya prīti sukha saṃniśraya tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar dvīpam iti ucyate traidhātuka pariccheda tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar trāṇam iti ucyate sarva mahā duḥkha upadrava apagama tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar  śaraṇam iti ucyate āśaya prayogayoḥ avandhya pada sthāna tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar  parāyaṇam iti ucyate sarvasya parama āryatvasya āgamana pada sthāṇa tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar acyutam iti ucyate jāti viraha tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodha punar nirvāram iti ucyate sarva kleśa santāpa virahatām sarva icchā lābha duḥkha mahā santāpa virahatām ca upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar niṣpadāri dāham iotyute sarva śoka paridevanā duḥkha daurmanasya vikṣepa viraha tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar  kṣemam iti ucyate hiṃsā bhaya rahita vihāra pada sthāna tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar  śivam iti ucyate lābha vastu pada sthāna tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar  sauvarṇikam iti ucyate parama artha sukha adhiṣṭhāna tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar  svastyayanam iti ucyate tad sukha prayoga prāpti pada sthāna tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar ogyam iti ucyate sarva āvaraṇaraḥ  gavirahatām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar ārnijyam iti ucyate sarva vikṣepa viraha tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar nirvāṇam iti ucyate animitta śānta mahā sukha vihāra pada sthāna tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar ajātam iti ucyate pratisaṃdhi upapatti viraha tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar abhūtam iti ucyate tad uttara kāla utpatti viraha tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar askṛtam iti ucyate pūrva anta karma kleśa balavadā vedha viraha tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar asaṃskṛtam iti ucyate vartamāna karma kleśān abhisaṃskāra pada sthāna tām upādāya kim upādāya sa nirodhaḥ punar anutpannam iti ucyate anāgata santati utpāda viraha tām upādāya tathā nirodha satyasya samāsatas catvāraḥ  lakṣaṇa prabhedāḥ nirodha lakṣaṇam śānta lakṣaṇam praṇīta lakṣaṇam niḥsaraṇa lakṣaṇam ca kim upādāya nirodha lakṣaṇam kleśa visaṃyoga tām upādāya kim upādāya śānta lakṣaṇam duḥkha visaṃyoga tām upādāya kim upādāya praṇīta lakṣaṇam sukha śucī adhiṣṭhāna tām upādāya kim upādāya niḥsaraṇa lakṣaṇam nitya hita adhiṣṭhāna tām upādāya atha viniścaye satya paricchede prathame caturthaḥ  bhāgaḥ mārga satyam katamat  yena duḥkham parijānīte samudayam prajahāti nirodham sākṣātkaroti mārgam bhāvayati etad  saṃkṣepeṇa mārgasatyalakṣaṇam iti ucyate punar  mārgaḥ pañcavidhaḥ saṃbhāra mārgaḥ prayoga mārgaḥ darśana mārga bhāvanā mārgaḥ niṣṭhā mārgaḥ ca saṃbhāra mārgaḥ katamaḥ pṛthagjanānām śīlam indriya dvāra rakṣā bhojane mātrā jña tā prathama rātrau tad uttara rātriṣu vā nityam amiddham vīrya bhāvanā śamatha vipaśyanā saṃprajanya vihāraḥ ca yad vā punar anyat aupaniṣadam kuśalam śruta mayī prajñā cintā mayī prajñā bhāvanā mayī prajñā tad bhāvanayā abhisamaya vimokṣa sthāna bhājanām pratilabhate prayoga mārgaḥ katamaḥ yaḥ saṃbhāra mārgaḥ sa prayoga mārgaḥ yaḥ tu prayoga mārgaḥ sana saṃbhāra mārgaḥ saṃbhāra mārga upacitāni nirvedha bhāgīyāni kuśala mūlāni ūṣma gataḥ mūrdhānaḥ satya anukūla kṣānti laukika agra dharmaḥ ca ūṣma gatam katamat  pratyātmam satye pvāloka labdhaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā saṃyogaḥ ca mūrdhānam katamat  pratyātmam satyeṣu āloka vṛddhaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā saṃyogaḥ ca satya anukūla kṣāntiḥ katamā pratyātmam satyeṣu eka deśa praviṣṭa anusṛtaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā saṃyogaḥ ca laukika agra dharmaḥ katamaḥ pratyātmam satyeṣu ānantarya citta samādhiḥ prajñā saṃyogaḥ ca darśana mārgaḥ katamaḥ samāsatas  laukikā gradharma anantaram anupalambhaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā saṃyogaḥ ca sama samālambya ālambanajñām api tad  pratyātmam apanīta sattva saṃketa dharma saṃketa sarvatas  apanīta ubhaya saṃketa ālambana dharma jñānam api tad  prabhedaśaḥ śunardarśana mārgaḥ  laukika agra dharma anantaram duḥkhe dharma jñāna kṣāntiḥ  duḥkhe dharma jñānam duḥkhe anvaya jñāna kṣāntiḥ duḥkhe anvaya jñānam samudaye dharma jñāna kṣāntiḥ samudaye dharma jñānam samudaye anvaya jñāna kṣāntiḥ samudaye anvaya jñānam nirodhe dharma jñāna kṣāntiḥ nirodhe dharma jñānam nirodhe anvaya jñāna kṣāntiḥ nirodhe anvaya jñānam mārge dharma jñāna kṣāntim mārge dharma jñānam mārge anvaya jñāna kṣāntiḥ mārge anvaya jñānam evaṃca ṣoḍaśa jñāna kṣāntibhiḥ darśana mārga prabhedāḥ dukham katamat  duḥkha satyam duḥkhe dharmaḥ katamaḥ duḥkha satya ādhipateyaḥ śāsana dharmaḥ dharma jñānam katamat  prayoga mārge satya ādhipateyam dharma vicāraṇa ajñānam jñāna kṣāntiḥ katamā pūrva adhipati bala vicāraṇām upādāya pratyātmam duḥkha satye pratyakṣa anubhāvinī anāsravā prajñā yayā prajñāyā duḥkha darśana prahātavyān sarva kleśān prajahāti tasmāt ucyate duḥkhe dharma jñāna kṣāntiḥ iti duḥkhe dharma jñānam katamat  kṣānti anantaram yena jñānena pūrva uktebhyaḥ kleśebhyaḥ  vimuktim sākṣātkaroti tasmāt ucyate duḥkhe dharma jñānam iti duḥkhe anvaya jñāna kṣāntiḥ katamā duḥkhe dharma jñāna kṣāntyām duḥkhe dharma jñāne ca pratyātmam pratyakṣa anubhāvinī anāsravā prajñā utpadyate yad uttaram anvaya eṣa ārya dharmāṇām tasmāt ucyate duḥkhe anvaya jñāna kṣāntiḥ duḥkhe anvaya jñānam katamat  tad anantaram anāsravam jñānam utpadyate yena jñānena duḥkhe anvaya jñāna kṣāntim upadhārayati tad  duḥkhe anvaya jñānam iti ucyate tadvat anyeṣu satyeṣu yathāyogyam kṣāntiḥ jñāna kṣayaḥ  jñeyaḥ tatra avasthāyām dharma kṣānti jñānaiḥ grāhyā vanoghaḥ anvaya kṣānti jñānaiḥ grāhaka avabodhaḥ api ca eṣu sarveṣu kṣānti jñāneṣu animitta prekṣā vihārī veditavyaḥ ime ṣoḍaśa cittakṣaṇā darśana mārga ākhyātaḥ jñeye jñāna utpatti parisamāptiḥ ekaścitta lakṣaṇaḥ  veditavyaḥ sarvam hi mārga satyam caturbhiḥ prakāraiḥ anugantavyam vyavasthānataḥ vikalpanataḥ anubhavataḥ paripūritaḥ ca vyavasthānataḥ katamat  yathā svam adhigama niṣṭhā prāptāḥ śrāvaka ādayaḥ tad pṛṣṭha labdhena jñānena prāpaṇa nimitta pramāṇaiḥ nāma pada vyañjana kāyaiḥ mārga satyam vyavasthāpayanti vikalpanataḥ katamat  abhisamaya prayuktā laukikena jñānena yathāvyavasthānam vikalpoyantaḥ  yad abhyasyanti anubhavataḥ katamat  tathā abhyasyantaḥ  mayā ḷyadā ditaḥ  darśana mārga ākhyām lokottarām niṣprapañca avasthām pratyātmam anubhavati paripūritaḥ katamat  tad ūrdhvam yām āśraya parivṛttim paripūrya yāvat adhigama niṣṭhām prāpnuvanti tena punar adhigama niṣṭhā prāptāḥ tad pṛṣṭha labdhena jñānena nāma pada vyañjana kāyaiḥ mārga satyam vyavasthāpayanti yad uktam sūtre virajñaḥ  vīta m alam dharmeṣu dharma cakṣuḥ u udapādi iti tad darśana mārgam adhikṛtya uktam tatra dharma kṣāntibhiḥ virajaḥ dharma jñānaiḥ vīta malam parijñayā prahāṇena mārga śuddhi lābhena ca yad uktam sūtre dṛṣṭa dharmā prāpta dharmā vidita dharmā paryavagāḍha dharmā sarvaiḥ tīrṇaka aṃkṣaḥ tīrṇa vicikitsaḥ apara pratyayaḥ śāstuḥ śāsanaḥ  ananyaneyaḥ dharmeṣu vaiśāradya prāpta iti tad api darśana mārgam adhikṛtya uktam dṛṣṭa dharmā dharma kṣāntibhiḥ prāpta dharmā dharma jñānaiḥ vidita dharmā anvaya kṣāntibhiḥ paryavagāḍha dharmā anvaya jñānaiḥ sarvaiḥ tīrṇaka aṃkṣaḥ svādhigame kṣānti jñānaiḥ kāṃkṣā bhāvena tīrṇa vicikitsaḥ parādhigame tad avasthasya vimati abhāvena apara pratyayaḥ mārga bhāvanāyām na paratas  svayam kuśala āvarjanena śāstuḥ śāsane ananyaneyaḥ buddha śāsane anya tīrthyaiḥ aneya tām upādāya dharmeṣu vaiśāradya prāptaḥ adhigamana āramya paripraśna dharmeṣu alīna citta tām upādāya bhāvanā mārgaḥ katamaḥ darśana mārgāt ūrdhvam laukikaḥ  mārgaḥ  loka uttara mārgaḥ mṛdu mārgaḥ  madhya mārgaḥ  adhimātraḥ  mārgaḥ prayoga mārgaḥ ānantarya mārgaḥ vimukti mārgaḥ viśeṣa mārgaḥ ca laukikaḥ  mārgaḥ katamaḥ laukikam prathamam dhyānam dvitīyam tṛtīyam caturtham dhyānam ākāśānattya āyatanam vijñāna ānanti āyatanam ākiñcati āyatanam na eva saṃjñāna asaṃjñā yatanam ca ta ete dhyāna ārūpyāḥ saṃkleśa vyavadāna vyavasthāna viśuddhibhiḥ veditavyāḥ katham saṃkleśataḥ catvāri avyākṛta mūlāni tṛṣṇā dṛṣṭiḥ mānaḥ  avidyā ca tṛṣṇayā āsvāda saṃkleśena saṃkliśyate dṛṣṭyā dṛṣṭi uttara dhyāyitayā saṃkliśyate mānena māna uttara dhyāyitayā saṃkliśyate avidyayā vicikitsā uttara dhyāyitayā saṃkliśyate tathā ca saṃkliṣṭa cetasām rūpārūpya avacarāḥ kleśa upakleśāḥ pravarttante katham vyavadānataḥ śuddhakā dhyāna ārūpyāḥ kuśala tvāt  vyavadātā iti ucyante katham vyavasthānataḥ aṅga vyavasthānataḥ samāpatti vyavasthānataḥ mātrā vyavasthānataḥ saṃjñā karaṇa vyavasthānaḥ ca katham aṅga vyavasthānataḥ prathamam dhyānam pañcāṅgam pañcāṅgāni vitarkaḥ  vicāraḥ prītiḥ sukham citta ekāgra tā ca dvitīyam dhyānam catur aṅgam catvāri aṅgāni adhyātma saṃprasādaḥ prītiḥ sukham citta eka apratā ca tṛtīyam dhyānam pañcāṅgam pañcāṅgāni upekṣā smṛtiḥ saṃprajanyam sukham citta ekāgra tā ca caturtham dhyānam catur aṅgam catvāri aṅgāni upekṣā pariśuddhiḥ smṛti pariśuddhiḥ aduḥkha asukhā vedanā citta ekāgra tā ca pratipakṣa aṅgam upādāya anuśaṃsā aṅgam upādāya tad ubhaya āśraya svabhāva aṅgam ca upādāya ārupya iṣu aṅga vyavasthānam na asti śamatha eka rasa tām upādāya katham samāpatti vyavasthānataḥ saptabhiḥ manaskāraiḥ prathamam dhyānam samāpadyate evam yāvat na eva saṃjñāna asaṃjñā yatanam ca sapta manaskārāḥ katame lakṣaṇa prati saṃvedī manaskāraḥ ādhimokṣikaḥ prāvivejaḥ rati saṃgrāhakaḥ mīmāṃsakaḥ prayoga niṣṭhaḥ prayoga niṣṭhāphalaḥ ca manaskāraḥ katham mātrā vyavasthānataḥ prathamam dhyānam su dupari bhāvitam madhya paribhāvitam adhimātra paribhāvitaḥ ca [tat yathā] prathamam dhyāna metram śiṣṭāni dhyānāni ārūpyāḥ ca mṛdu madhya adhimātra paribhāvitasya prathamasya dhyānasya phalam trividhā prathamā dhyāna upapattiḥ yathā prathamasya dhyānasya evam śiṣṭānām dhyānānām trividhā dhyāna upapattiḥ ārūpyeṣu sthāna antara abhāvam upādāya upapatti bhedaḥ  na asti tatra mṛdu madhya adhimātra paribhāvita tvāt ārūpyāṇām upapattau  ucca nīca tā hīna praṇīta tā prajñāyate katham saṃjñā karaṇa vyavasthānataḥ prathama dhyāna saṃgṛhītānyāvataḥ samādhīn buddha bodhisattvāḥ samāpadyante teṣām śrāvaka pratyekabuddhā nāma abhijñā api na bhavanti yathā prathama dhyāna saṃgṛhītān evam avaśiṣṭa dhyāna saṃgṛhīta anyat uta dhyāna pāramitām niśritya katham viśuddhitaḥ prānta koṭikam prathamam dhyānam yāvat na eva saṃjñāna asaṃjñā āyatanam viśuddhiḥ iti ucyate loka uttaraḥ  mārgaḥ katamaḥ bhāvanā mārge duḥkha samudaya nirodha mārga jñānāni dharma jñāna anvaya pakṣyāṇi taiḥ ca saṃprayuktaḥ samādhiḥ prathamam vā dhyānam yāvat ākiñcanī āyatanam na eva saṃjñāna asaṃjñā yatanaṃ  laukikam eva apari sphuṭam saṃjñā pracāra tām upādāya tatas  śca animittam iti ucyate yathā uktam bhagavatā yāvat eva saṃjñā samāpattiḥ tāvat ājñā prativedha iti nirodha samāpattiḥ lokottarā manuṣyeṣu abhinirhiyate manuṣyeṣu bhinirhṛtā manuṣya iṣu rūpa dhātau vā saṃmukhīkriyate ārūpyeṣu syāḥ saṃmukhībhāvaḥ  na asti śānta vimokṣa vipāka vihārīṇām tad yatna anārambha tām upādāya mṛdu mārgaḥ katamaḥ mṛdu mṛduḥ mṛdu madhyaḥ  mṛdvadhimātraḥ ca yena traidhātukā vacarāṇā kleśānām bhūmau bhūmau  adhimātra adhimātram adhimātra madhyam adhimātrā mṛdum kleśa prakāra prajahāti madhyaḥ mārgaḥ katamaḥ madhya mṛduḥ madhya madhyaḥ madhya adhimātraḥ ca yena traidhātuka avacarāṇām kleśānām bhūmau bhūmau madhya adhimātram madhya madhyam madhya mṛdum kleśa prakāram prajahāti adhimātraḥ  mārgaḥ katamaḥ adhimātra mṛduḥ adhimātra madhyaḥ  adhimātra adhimātraḥ ca yena traidhātuka avacarāṇām kleśānām bhūmau bhūmau mṛdvadhi mātram mṛdu madhyam mṛdu mṛdum kleśa prakāram prajahāti prayoga mārgaḥ katamaḥ yena kleśam prajahāti ānantarya mārgaḥ katamaḥ yasya anantaram nirantaraḥ kleśaḥ prahīṇaḥ  bhavati vimukti mārgaḥ katamaḥ yena prahīṇe kleśe vimuktim sākṣātkaroti viśeṣa mārgaḥ katamaḥ tad anyasya kleśa prakārasya prayoga ānantarya vimukti mārgāḥ viśeṣa mārgaḥ api khalu kleśa prahāṇa prayogam nirākṛtya dharma cintāyām vā prayuktasya dharma vihāre vā samāpatti viśeṣe vā yaḥ  mārgaḥ api khalu vaiśeṣikān guṇān abhinirharataḥ  vā yaḥ  mārgaḥ mārga bhāvanā katamā pratilaṃbha bhāvanā niṣevaṇa bhāvanā nirdhāvana bhāvanā pratipakṣa bhāvanā ca pratilambha bhāvanā katamā anutpannānām kuśalānām dharmāṇām utpādāya yā bhāvanā niṣevaṇa bhāvanā katamā utpannānām kuśalānām dharmāṇām sthitaye asaṃmoṣāya bhūyas bhāvāya vṛddhi vipula tāyai yā bhāvanā nirdhāvana bhāvanā katamā utpannānām pāpakānām akuśalānām dharmāṇām prahāṇāya yā bhāvanā pratipakṣa bhāvanā katamā anutpannānām pāpakānām akuśakunām dharmāṇām anutpādāya yā bhāvanā api khalu mārga utpadyamānaḥ svām vāsanām ava sthāpayati sā pratilambha bhāvanā sa eva saṃmukhībhūtaḥ  bhāvanām gacchati sā niṣevaṇa bhāvanā svam āvaraṇam vijahāti sā nirdhāvana bhāvanā vihīna śca āvaraṇam āyatyām anutpatti dharma tāyām avasthāpayati sā pratipakṣa bhāvanā api khalu caturvidhaḥ pratipakṣaḥ vidūṣaṇa apratipakṣaḥ prahāṇa pratipakṣaḥ ādhāra pratipakṣaḥ dūrībhāva pratipakṣaḥ ca pratipakṣa bhāvanā iti ucyate vidūṣaṇa apratipakṣaḥ katamaḥ sa āsraveṣu saṃskāreṣu ādīn avadarśanam prahāṇa pratipakṣaḥ katamaḥ prayoga antarya mārgaḥ ādhara pratipakṣaḥ katamaḥ vimukti mārgaḥ dūrībhāva pratipakṣaḥ katamaḥ tad u parimaḥ mārgaḥ api khalu vastu parīkṣā mārgaḥ vyāvasāyikaḥ  mārgaḥ samādhi parikarma mārgaḥ abhisamaya prāyogikaḥ  mārgaḥ abhisamaya śliṣṭaḥ  mārgaḥ abhisamaya mārgaḥ viśuddhi nairyāṇikaḥ  mārgaḥ niśraya indriya bhinnaḥ mārgaḥ śikṣā traya pariśodhanaḥ  mārgaḥ sarva guṇa nirhāra kaḥ  mārgaḥ mārga saṃgraha mārgaḥ ca mārga iti ucyate sa punar eṣa yathākramam saptatriṃśat abodhi pakṣā dharmāḥ catasraḥ pratipadaḥ catvāri dharma padāni śamatha ai vipaśyanā triṇī ca indriyāṇī smṛti upasthānānām ālam vanam svabhāvaḥ sahāyaḥ bhāvanā bhāvanā phalañca veditavyam yathā smṛti upasthānānām evam avaśiṣṭānām bodhi pakṣāṇām smṛti upasthānānām ālambanam katamat  kāyaḥ  vedanā cittam dharmāḥ api khalu ātma āśraya vastu ātma upabhoga vastu ātma vastu ātma saṃkleśa vyavadāna vastu ca svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ prajñā smṛtiḥ ca sahāyaḥ katamaḥ tad saṃprayuktāḥ citta caitasikā dharmāḥ bhāvanā katamā adhyātmam kāya ādiṣu kāya ādi anupaśyanā yathā adhyātmam evam bahirdhā adhyātma vahirdhā adhyātmam kāyaḥ katamaḥ yāni asmin kāye ādhyatmikāni rūpīṇi āyatanāni bahirdhākāyaḥ katamaḥ bahirdhā rūpīṇi āyatanāni adhyātmavahirddhā kāyaḥ katamaḥ ādhyātmika āyatana saṃbaddhāni bāhyāni āyatanāni indriya adhiṣṭhānāni pārasāntānikāni ca ādhyātmikāni rūpīṇi āyatayāni kāye kāyānupaśyanā katamā yā vikalpa pratibimba kāyena prakṛti bimba kāyasya samatā apaśyanā adhyātmam vedanā katamā adhyātmam kāyam upādāya utpannā vedanā bahirddhā vedanā katamā bahirddhā kāyam upādaya utpannā vedanā adhyātma bahirddhā vedanā katamā adhyātma ābahiṛddhā kā ayam upādāya utpanna āvedanā yathā vedanā evam cittam dharmāḥ yathā kāye kāyānupaśyanā evam vedanā ādiṣu vedanā ādi anupaśyanā yathāyogam veditavyāḥ api khalu bhāvanā chandaḥ vīryam vyāyāma utsāhaḥ utsūḍhiraprativāṇiḥ smṛtiḥ saṃprajanyam apramādaḥ ca chandabhāvanā amanasikara upakleśa pratipakṣeṇa vīrya bhāvanā kausīdya upakleśa pratipakṣeṇa vyāyāma bhāvanā laya auddhatya upakleśa pratipakṣeṇa utsāha bhāvanā cetasaḥ  alīnatva upakleśa pratipakṣeṇa utsūḍhi bhāvanā viṣāda parisrava parikheda upakleśa pratipakṣeṇa aprativāṇi bhāvanā kuśala pakṣeṇa alpa mātra saṃtuṣṭi upakleśa pratipakṣeṇa smṛti bhāvanā bhagavataḥ śāsane saṃmoṣa upakleśa pratipakṣeṇa saṃprajanya bhāvanā āpatti vipratisāra upakleśa pratipakṣeṇa apramāda bhāvanā kuśaleṣu nikṣipta dhura topa kleśa pratipakṣeṇa bhāvanā phalam katamat  catu rviparyāsa prahāṇam catuḥ satya avatāraḥ kāya ādi visaṃyogaḥ catuḥ samyak prahāṇānām ālambanam katamat  utpanna an utpanna vipakṣa pratipakṣāḥ svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ vyāyāmaḥ sahāyaḥ katamaḥ tad saṃprayuktāḥ citta caitasikā dharmāḥ bhāvanā katamā tad uktam sūtre chandam janayati vyāyacchate vīryam ārabhate cittam pragṛṇhāti cittam pradadhāti iti evamādibhiḥ padaiḥ tatra vīrya āśraya bhāvanā paridīpitā āśrayaḥ chandaḥ vīryam udyogaḥ śamatha gra graha upekṣā nimitta manasikāreṣu chandam janayati laya auddhatya apakarṣaṇe vīryam ārabhate evam tad anantaram cittam pragṛṇhāti pradadhātī pratyucyate bhāvanā phalam katamat  aśeṣa vipakṣa hāniḥ pratipakṣa pratilambhaḥ pratipakṣa vṛddhiḥ ca tad ucyate bhāvanā phalam catur ṛddhi pādānām ālambanam katamat  niṣpajñena samādhinā yad karaṇīyam kṛtyam svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ samādhiḥ sahāyaḥ katamaḥ chandaḥ vīryam cittam mīmāṃsā tad saṃprayuktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ chanda samādhiḥ katamaḥ yad satkṛtya prayogam āgamya spṛśati cittasya ekāgra tām vīrya samadhiḥ katamaḥ yad sātatya prayogam āgamya spṛśati cittasya ekāgra tām citta samādhiḥ katamaḥ pūrva samādhi bhāvanām āgamya svarasena spṛśati cittasya ekāgra tām mīmāṃsā samādhiḥ katamaḥ deśanā dharma śravaṇam āgamya pratyātmam pratisaṃkhyāya spṛśati cittasya ekāgra tām punar  chanda samādhiḥ yad  chandam janayan spṛśati cittasya ekagra tām vīrya samādhiḥ yad  vīrya māra pramāṇaḥ spṛśati cittasya ekāgra tām citta samādhiḥ yad  cittam pradadhat  spṛśati cittasya egratām mīmāṃsā samādhiḥ yad  cittam pragṛṇhan spṛśati cittasya ekāgra tām bhāvanā katamā aṣṭānām prahāṇa saṃskārāṇām abhyāsaḥ katame aṣṭau chandaḥ vyāyāmaḥ śraddhā praśrabdhiḥ smṛtiḥ saṃprajanyam cetanā upekṣā ca te punar aṣṭau samāsatas caturdhā saṃgṛhyante vyāyasāyikaḥ anugrāhakaḥ aupanivandhikaḥ prātipakṣikaḥ ca chanda vīrya citta mīmāṃsā bhāvanā punar dvividhā nidānam saṃkṣepa vikṣepa parivarjana bhāvana alīnatva avikṣepa tad ubhaya āśraya anukūla bhāvanā ca phalam katamat  kuśala samādhi parikarmataḥ yathākarmam dharma abhijñā yathācittam abhijñā pradarśanam api ca teṣu teṣu dharmeṣu adhigamaḥ prātiḥ karmaṇya tā vaśitā kāritram yatheṣṭam nānā vidhānāmṛdudhi ādīnām vastūnām niṣpādanam adhi guṇānām nirhāraḥ ca pañca indriyāṇām ālambanam katamat  catvāri ārya satyāni svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ śraddhā vīrya smṛtiḥ samādhiḥ prajñā ca sahāya katamaḥ tad saṃprayuktāḥ citta caitasikā dharmāḥ bhāvanā katamā yad  śraddhā indriyeṇa satyeṣu abhisaṃpratyaya samutthānam prayoga bhāvanā vīrya indriyeṇa satyeṣu utpanna abhisaṃpratyayasya abhisaṃbodhi artham vyāyāma samutthāna prayoga bhāvanā smṛti indriyeṇa satyeṣu ārabdha vīryasya smṛti saṃprayogā dharma saṃmopa samutthāna prayoga bhāvanā samādhi indriyeṇa satyeṣu saṃprayukta smṛteḥ citta ekāgra tā samutthāna prayoga bhāvanā prajñā indriyeṇa satyeṣu samāhita cittasya pravicaya samutthāna prayoga bhāvanā bhāvanā phalam katamat  satya abhisamaya samutthānataḥ uṣma gata mūrdha parikarmataḥ ca kṣānti laukika agra dharma nirhāraḥ yathā pañca indriyāṇi tathā pañca balāni eṣām viśeṣaḥ taiḥ vipakṣa antarāya nirllekhaḥ  anavamudyata iti balāni iti ucyante sapta bodhi aṅgānām ālambanam katamat  caturṇām ārya satyānām yathābhūta tā svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ smṛtiḥ dharma vicayaḥ vīryam prītiḥ praśrabdhiḥ samādhiḥ upekṣā ca smṛtiḥ saṃniśraya aṅgam dharma vicayaḥ svabhāva aṅgam vīryam niryāṇa aṅgam prītiḥ anuśaṃsā aṅgam praśrabdhiḥ samādhiḥ upekṣā ca asaṃkleśa aṅgam asaṃkleśataḥ asaṃkleśa āśrayataḥ asaṃkleśa svabhāvataḥ ca sahāyaḥ katamaḥ tad saṃprayukta āśritta caitasikā dharmāḥ bhāvanā katamā viveka niśritam virāga niśritam nirodha niśritam vyavasarga pariṇatam smṛti saṃbodhi aṅgam yathā smṛti saṃbodhi aṅgam tathā yāvat  upekṣā saṃbodhi aṅgam ebhiḥ catubhiḥ padaiḥ yathākramam catuḥsatya ālambanā bodhi aṅga bhāvanā paridīpitā bhāvanā phalam katamat  darśana heyānām kleśānām prahāṇam aṣṭānām ārya mārga aṅgānām ālambanam katamat  tad uttara kālam caturṇām ārya satyānām yathābhūta tā svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ samyak dṛṣṭiḥ samyak karmmāntaḥ samyak ājīvaḥ samyak vyāyāmaḥ samyak smṛtiḥ samyak samādhiḥ ca samyak adṛṣṭiuḥ pariccheda aṅgam samyak saṃkalpa para saṃprāpaṇa aṅgam samyak vāc karma antājīvāḥ para saṃprati apāṅgam darśana śīlā jīva viśuddhi tām upādāya samyak vyāyāmaḥ kleśa āvaraṇa viśodhana aṅgam samyak samādhiḥ vaiśeṣika guṇa āvaraṇa viśodhana aṅgam sahāyaḥ katamaḥ tad saṃprayuktāḥ citta caitasikā dharmāḥ bhāvanā katamā bhāvanā tu bodhi aṅgavat  bhāvanā phalam katamat  paricchedaḥ para saṃprāpaṇam para saṃpratyayaḥ kleśa āvaraṇa viśodhanam upakleśa āvaraṇa viśodhanam vaiśeṣika guṇa āvaraṇa viśodhanam ca catasraḥ pratipadaḥ katamāḥ duḥkhā pratipad  dhandhā abhijñā duḥkhā pratipad  kṣipra abhijñā sukhā pratipad  dhandhā abhijñā sukhā pratipad  kṣipra abhijñā prathamā mṛd u indriyāṇām anupalabdha maula dhyānam dvitīyā tīkṣṇa indriyāṇām anupalabdha maula dhyānam tṛtīyā mṛd u indriyāṇām upalabha maula dhyānam caturthī tīkṣṇa indriyāṇām upalabdha maula dhyānam catvāri dharma padāni katamāni alobhāt veṣāṇām samyak  smṛtiḥ samyak  samādhiḥ alobhāt veṣāṇām adhi śīla śikṣā viśuddhiḥ samyak smṛtānām adhicitta śikṣā viśuddhiḥ samyak samādhitānām adhiprajña śikṣā viśuddhiḥ śamathaḥ katamaḥ adhyātmam cittasya upanibandhaḥ sthāpanā saṃsthāpanā avasthāpanā upasthāpanā damanam śamanam vyupaśamanam ekotīkaraṇam samādhānam ca vipaśyanā katamā yā dharmān vicinoti pravivinoti parivitarkkayati parimīmāṃsam āpataye ca kāma pratipakṣa dauṣṭhulya nimitta saṃyojanataḥ kāma abhibhavānām viparyāsataḥ aviparyasta cittasya avasthā apanataḥ ca api khalu śamatha vipaśyanām āgamya catvāraḥ  mārgāḥ ekatyaḥ śamathasya lābhī na vipaśyanāyāḥ tad prakāram śamatham niśritya vipaśyanāma apanā ekatyaḥ vipaśyanāyā lābhī na śamathasya tad prakārām vipaśyanā niśritya śamatha bhāvanā ekatyaḥ na śamathasya lābhī na api vipaśyanāyāḥ tad saṃbaddha cittasya layau ddhatya apakarṣaṇāt  yugapad ubhaya mārga bhāvanā ekatyaḥ śamathasya lābhī vipaśyanāyāḥ ca tasya śamatha vipaśyana ubhaya mārga yuktasya samam yugapad  pravṛttiḥ trīṇi indriyāṇi ajñātam ājñā asyāmi indriyam ājña indriyam ājñāta avi indriyam ca ajñātam ājñā asyāmi indriyam katamat  prayoga mārge pañcadaśasu ca darśana mārga citta kṣaṇeṣu yad indriyam ājña indriyam katamat  ṣoḍaśāt  darśana mārga citta kṣaṇāt rūdhvam sarvasmin śaikṣa mārge yad indriyam ājñāta avi indriyam katamat  aśaikṣa mārgeyat indriyam prathama dhyāna bhūmikānām bhāvanā mārge kāmāvacarāṇi kuśala mūlakāni api bhāvanām gacchanti teṣu vibhutva lābhataḥ yathā prathama dhyāna bhūmikānām kāmāvacarāṇi kuśala mūlakāni bhāvanām gacchanti tathā sarva īpāmūrdva bhūmikānām bhāvanā mārge adhas bhūmikāni kuśala mūlakāni bhāvanām gacchanti teṣu vibhutva lābhataḥ niṣṭhā mārgaḥ katamaḥ vajra upamaḥ samadhiḥ sarva dauṣṭhulyānām pratipraśrabdheḥ sarva saṃyogānām prahāṇāt  sarva visaṃyogānām adhigamāt ca tad anantaram nirantara āśraya pravṛttiḥ prāpta kṣaya jñānam anutpāda jñānam daśā śaikṣā dharmāḥ katame daśa aśaikṣasya samyak dṛṣṭiḥ yāyada śaikṣasya samyak samādhiḥ aśaikṣasya samyak vimokṣaḥ aśaikṣasya samyak  jñānam ca evamādayaḥ  dharmā niṣṭhā mārga ucyate katamāni sarva dauṣṭhulyāni saṃ kṣepataḥ catur viśatiḥ tad yathā sarvatragam abhilāpa dauṣṭhulyam vedita dauṣṭhulyam kleśa dauṣṭhulyam karma dauṣṭhulyam vipāka dauṣṭhulyam kleśa āvaraṇāt auṣṭhulyam karma āvaraṇa dauṣṭhulyam vipāka āvaraṇa dauṣṭhulyam nivaraṇa dauṣṭhulyam vitarkka dauṣṭhulyam āhāra dauṣṭhulyam maithuna dauṣṭhulyam svapna dauṣṭhulyam vyādhi dauṣṭhulyam jarā dauṣṭhulyam maraṇa dauṣṭhulyam pariśrama dauṣṭhulyam dṛḍha dauṣṭhulyam audārika dauṣṭhulyam madhya dauṣṭhulyam sūkṣma dauṣṭhulyam samāpatti āvaraṇa dauṣṭhulyam jñeya āvaraṇa dauṣṭhulyam ca saṃyogaḥ katamaḥ dauṣṭhulya āciteṣu saṃyoga lābha ta iti vijñaptiḥ visaṃyogaḥ katamaḥ dauṣṭhulya vikṣipteṣu visaṃyoga lābha ta iti vijñaptiḥ vajra upamaḥ samādhiḥ katamaḥ bhāvanā mārga gatasya tad uttaram saṃyojana prahāṇa mārgava sthāyām yaḥ samādhiḥ prayoga mārga saṃgrahaḥ  vā ānantarya mārga saṃgrahaḥ  vā prayoga mārga saṃgrahaḥ tu tatas  param sarvaiḥ āvaraṇaiḥ acchādyaḥ sarva āvarāṇānām ca bhedaka iti ānantarya mārga saṃgrahaḥ tu yad anantaram kṣaya jñāna anutpāda jñāna utpattiḥ sa ca samādhiḥ nirantaraḥ dṛḍhaḥ ekarasaḥ vyāpī ca etad artha pratibimbana artham bhagavatā uktam tad yathā mahā śaila parvataḥ  akhaṇḍaḥ acchidraḥ  aśuṣira eka ghanaḥ su saṃvṛttaḥ  daśa diś vāta akampyaḥ ca katamā nāma nirantara āśraya pravṛttiḥ aśaikṣa mārga lābhinaḥ trividhā āśraya pravṛttiḥ katamāḥ tisraḥ citta āśrayam apravṛttiḥ māryā śrapa pravṛttiḥ dauṣṭhulya āśraya pravṛttiḥ ca kṣaya jñānam katamat  hetu kṣayeṇa yad  śānam labhyate kṣaya viṣayā lambanam vā anutpāda jñānam katamat  phala prahāṇena yad  jñānam labhyate phala anutpatti viṣaya ālambanam vā daśā śaikṣā dharmāḥ tu aśaikṣāṇām śīla skandham samādhi skandham prajñā skandham vimukti skandham vimukti jñāna darśana skandham ca adhikṛtya veditavyāḥ tathā ca mārga satyasya catvāraḥ prakāra bhedāḥ mārga lakṣaṇam nyāya lakṣaṇam pratipad lakṣaṇam nairyāṇika lakṣaṇam ca kim upādāya mārga lakṣaṇam tattva artha parimārgaṇa tām upādāya kim upādāya nyāya lakṣaṇam kleśa pratipakṣatām upādāya kim upādāya pratipad lakṣaṇam citta aviparyāsa pratipādana ātām upādāya kim upādāya nairyāṇika lakṣaṇam nitya padayāna tām upādāya satyeṣu ṣoḍaśa ākārāḥ laukikā lokottarāḥ ca laukikānām loka uttarāṇām ca katamaḥ prabhedaḥ jñeye akuśala praveśa kuśalya praveśa stra bhāva prabhedataḥ sa āvaraṇa nirāvaraṇa svabhāva prabhedataḥ sa vikalpa nirvikalpa svabhāva prabhedataḥ ca kena hetunā satyeṣu anitya duḥkha ādayaḥ ṣoḍaśa lauaukika ākārāḥ tathāgata aprativedhataḥ kleśa anuśayataḥ abhilāpa mukhena prapañcanataḥ ca loka uttara ākārāḥ tad viparyayeṇa loka uttara ākāreṣu varttamānaḥ  anitya artham paśyati sākṣāt anubhavati na utu nityam paśyati abhilāpa prapañca mukhena yathā anitya ākārā anitya arthe evam śiṣṭhākarāḥ śiṣṭa artheṣu yathāyogam veditavyāḥ atha viniścaye dharma paricchedaḥ  dvitīyaḥ  bhāgaḥ dharma viniścayaḥ katamaḥ ārya śāsanam dvādaśa aṅga dharmaḥ katamāni dvādaśa aṅgāni sūtram geyam vyākaraṇam gāthā udānam nidānam avadānam itivṛtakam jātakam vaipulyam adbhuta dharmaḥ upadeśaḥ ca 1  sūtram katamat  yad abhipreta artham sūcana ākāreṇa gadya bhāṣitam daśa anuśaṃsān saṃpaśyan tathāgataḥ sūcana ākāreṇa dharmam deśayati sukham vyavasthāpayati sukham deśayati śrotā api sukham udgṛṇhāti dharma gaurava tayā kṣipram bodhi saṃbhārān paripūrayati āśudharma tām pratividhyati buddhe avetya prasādam labhate dharme saṃghe ca avetya prasādam labhate parama dṛṣṭa dharma sukha vihāram spṛśati sāṃkathya viniścayena satām cittam ārādhayati paṇḍitaḥ paṇḍita iti saṃkhyām gacchati 2  geyam katamat  sūtrāṇām madhye vā ante vā gāthayā yad  gīyate sūtreṣu anirūpitaḥ  arthaḥ  vā yad  vyākhyāyate atas  geyam iti ucyate 3  vyākaraṇam katamat  tad  sthāneṣu samatikrāntānām atītānām ārya śrāvakāṇām prāpti utpatti prabheda vyākaraṇam api ca sūtreṣu nirūīpita arthasya sphuṭīkaraṇam vivṛtya abhisandhi vyākaraṇāt 4  gāthā katamā sūtreṣu pāda yogena deśyate dvipadī tripadī catuṣpadī paṃcapadī ṣaṭpadī vā 5  udānam katamat  sūtreṣu kadācid  tathāgatena ātta manaskena yad udāhṛtam 6  nidānam katamat  pṛṣṭena yad  bhāṣitam sa utpattikam śikṣā prajñā āptekam vā atas  api nidānam 7  avadānam katamat  sūtreṣu sa dṛṣṭāntakam bhāṣitam 8  itivṛttakam katamat  yad ā ārya śrāvakāṇām pūrva laukikam vṛttam deśayati 9  jātakam katamat  yad  bodhisattva carita piṭaka saṃprayuktam vṛttam deśayati 10  vaipulyam katamat  bodhisattva piṭaka saṃprayuktam bhāṣitam yad ucyate vaipulyam tad  vaidalyam api ucyate vaitulyam api ucyate kimartham vaipulyam ucyate sarva sattvānām hita sukha adhiṣṭhānataḥ udāra gambhīra dharma deśanātaḥ ca kimartham ucyate vaidalyam sarva āvaraṇa vidalanataḥ kimartham ucyate vaitulyam upamāna dharmāṇām tulanā bhāvataḥ 11  adbhuta dharmaḥ katamaḥ yatra śrāvaka bodhisattva tathā gatānām paramā dbhuta āścarya dharmāṇām deśanā 12  upadeśaḥ katamaḥ sarva gambhora gūḍha dharma lakṣaṇānām aviparītam vyākhyānam evam sūtra ādīni dvādaśa aṅgāni ārya śāsanāni triṣu piṭakeṣu saṃgṛhītāni bhavanti katamāni trīṇi sūtra piṭakam vinaya piṭakam abhidharma piṭakam ca tāni punar dvividhāni śrāvaka piṭakam bodhisattva piṭakam ca sūtram geyam vyākaraṇam gāthā udānam ca etāni pañca śrāvakāṇām piṭakasya sūtra piṭake saṃgṛhītāni bhavanti nidānam avadānam iti vṛttakam jātakam ca etāni catvāri dvayoḥ piṭakayoḥ sa parivāre vinaya piṭake saṃgṛhītāni bhavanti vaipulyam adbhuta dharmaḥ ca ete dve bodhisattva piṭakasya sūtra piṭake saṃgṛhīte bhavataḥ upadeśa ekaḥ śrāvaka bodhisattva piṭakayoḥ abhidharma piṭake saṃgṛhītaḥ  bhavati kim upādāya tathāgatasya piṭaka traya vyavasthānam vicikitsā upakleśa pratipakṣakā matām upādāya sūtra piṭaka vyavasthānam anta dvaya anuyoga upakleśa pratipakṣa kāma tām upādāya vinaya piṭaka vyavasthānam svayaṃdṛṣṭi parāmarśa graha upakleśa pratipakṣa kāma tām upādāya abhidharma piṭaka vyavasthānam punar  śikṣā traya vyutpatti kāma tām upādāya sūtra piṭaka vyavasthānam adhi śīla adhicitta śikṣā niṣpādana kāma tām upādāya vinaya piṭaka vyavasthānam adhiprajña śikṣā niṣpādana kāma tām upādāya abhidharma piṭaka vyavasthānam punar  samyak  dharma artha vyutpatti kāma tām upādāya sūtra piṭaka vyavasthānam dharma artha sākṣāt kriyā pada sthāna prabhāvitā mupādāya vinaya piṭaka vyavasthānam jñāninām sāṃkathya viniścaya dharma saṃbhoga sukha vihāra āśraya tām upādāya abhidharma piṭaka vyavasthānam sa eṣa piṭaka traya saṃgṛhītaḥ  dharmaḥ kasya gocaraḥ śruta maya cintā āmaya bhāvanāmayānām citta caitasikānām dharmāṇām gocaraḥ yad uktam sutre citta caitasikā dharmāḥ sa ālambanāḥ sa ākāraḥ sa āśrayāḥ sa saṃprayogāḥ ca teṣām asmin dharme ālambanam katamat  sūtra ādikam ākāraḥ katamaḥ skandha ādayaḥ tad saṃprayuktāḥ ca arthāḥ āśrayaḥ katamaḥ para vijñaptiḥ smṛtiḥ vāsanā ca saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ anyaḥ  anya sahāya bhāvena ālambane ākāraiḥ saṃpratipattiḥ dharme ālambana prabhedaḥ katamaḥ saṃkṣepeṇa caturvidhaḥ ākhyātaḥ vyāpya ālambanam carita viśodhana ālambanam kauśalya ālambanam kleśa viśodhana ālambanam ca vyāpya ālambanam punar caturvidham sa vikalpa pratibimba ālambanam nirvikalpa prativimba ālambanam vastu paryanta ālambanam kārya pariniṣpatti ālambanam ca sa vikalpa pratibimba ālambanam katamat  adhimukti manaskāreṇa yad  śamatha vipaśyanā viṣaya ālambanam nirvikalpa prativimba ālambanam katamat  tattva manaskāreṇa yad  śamatha vipaśyanā viṣaya ālambanam vastu paryanta ālambanam katamat  sarva dharmāṇām kṣaya bhāvika tā yathāvat bhāvika tā ca kṣaya bhāvika tā katamā skandha dhātu āyatanāni yathāvat bhāvika tā katamā catvāri ārya satyāni ṣoḍaśa ākārāḥ tathatā sarve anityāḥ saṃskārāḥ sarve duḥkhā saṃskārāḥ sarve anātmānaḥ  dharmāḥ nirvāṇam śāntam śūnyam apraṇihitam animittam ca kārya pariniṣpatti ālambanam katamat  āśraya parivṛttiḥ iyam āśraya parivṛttiḥ acintyā ṣoḍaśa ākāreṣu śūnye kati ākārāḥ saṃgṛhītā bhavanti dvau apraṇihite kati ākārāḥ saṃgṛhītā bhavanti ṣaḍ  animitte kati ākārāḥ saṃgṛhītā bhavanti aṣṭau carita viśodhana ālambanam pañcavidham bhūyas rāga caritānām aśubha viṣaya ālambanam bhūyas dveṣa caritānām karuṇā bhāvanā viṣaya ālambanam bhūyas moha caritānām nikāya pratyaya tā pratītyasamutpāda viṣaya ālambanam mada māna caritānām dhātu prabheda viṣaya ālambanam vitarkka caritānām avatāra aprativāṇi smṛti viṣaya ālambanam kauśalya ālambanam pañcavidham skandha kauśalyam dhātu kauśalyam āyatana kauśalyam prati ityua samutpāda kauśalyam sthāna āsthāna kauśalyam ca sthāna āsthāna kauśalyena kam artham paśyati jñeye pratitya samutpāda kauśalyam paśyati sthāna āsthāna kauśalya pratītyasamutpāda kauśalyayoḥ kaḥ prabhedaḥ yad  dharmā dharmān abhiniṣyandayanti na hi eṣām nirhetukaḥ  na api viṣama hetuka utpāda iti idam pratītyasamutpāda kauśalyam hetu phala ānurūpye vedayita utpāda iti idam sthāna āsthāna kauśalyam kleśa viśodhana lambanam katamat  yad  adhas bhūmikānām audarika tā ūrdhva bhūmikānām śānta tā tathatā catvāri asatyāni ca etāni kleśa viśodhana ālambanāni nāma tatra dharma mīmāṃsā kāmena katibhiḥ yuktibhiḥ vicāryate catasṛbhiḥ yuktibhiḥ apekṣā yuktiḥ kārya kāraṇa yuktiḥ upapatti sādhana yuktiḥ dharma tāyuktiḥ ca apekṣā yuktiḥ katamā yā saṃskārāṇām utpattau pratyaya apekṣā kārya kāraṇa yuktiḥ katamā pṛthak lakṣaṇānām dharmāṇām pratyekam kārya kāraṇāni upapatti sādhana yuktiḥ katamā upapatti sādhana artham sādhyasya arthasya prāmāṇa aviruddha upadeśaḥ dharmatāyuktiḥ katamā anādi kālāt  sva lakṣaṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇa sthita dharmeṣu yā dharma tā pariniṣpattiḥ sā dharmatā iti dharmeṣu vicāraṇā dharmeṣu katamāḥ paryeṣaṇāḥ saṃbhavanti catasraḥ paryeṣaṇāḥ saṃbhavanti nāma paryeṣaṇā vastu paryeṣaṇā svabhāva prajñapti paryeṣaṇā viśeṣa prajñapti paryeṣaṇā ca nāma paryeṣaṇā katamā dharmeṣu nāmakāya padakāya vyañjana kāyānām apariniṣpannam sva lakṣaṇam iti yā santi īraṇā vastu paryeṣaṇā katamā dharmāṇām skandha dhātu āyatanānām apari niṣpakṣam kha lakṣaṇam iti yā saṃtīraṇā svabhāva prajñapti paryeṣaṇā katamā dharmāṇā mabhidhāna abhidheya saṃbandhe svabhāva prajñapti mātrasya vyavahāra nimitta tā santi īraṇā viśeṣa prajñapti paryeṣaṇā katamā dharmāṇām abhidhāna abhidheya sambandhe viśeṣa prajñapti mātrasya vyavahāra nimitta tā santi īraṇā iti dharma paryeṣaṇa abhāvanā dharmeṣu yathābhūta parijñānāni katamāni saṃbhavanti catvāri yathābhūta parijñānāni nāma paryeṣitam yathābhūta parijñānam vastu paryeṣitam yathābhūta parijñānam svabhāva prajñapti paryeṣitam yathābhūta parijñānam viśeṣa prajñapti paryeṣitam yathābhūta parijñānam nāma paryeṣitam yathābhūta parijñānam katamat  yathābhūtasya nāma anupalabdhi jñānam vastu paryeṣitam yathābhūta parijñānam katamat  yathābhūtasya vastu lakṣaṇa anupalabdhi jñānam svabhāva prajñapti paryeṣitam yathābhūta parijñānam katamat  yathābhūtasya dravya svabhāva anupalabdhi jñānam viśeṣa prajñapti paryeṣitam yathābhūta parijñānam katamat  yathābhūtasya dravya viśeṣa anupalabdhi jñānam dharmam āśritya samādhi prayuktasya yoga bhūmiḥ katamā jñeyā pañca ākārāḥ ādhāraḥ ādhānam ādarśaḥ ālokaḥ āśrayaḥ ca ādhāraḥ katamaḥ saṃbhṛta bodhi saṃbhārasya ūṣma gata ādiṣu ārya satyeṣu ca yad  vāhuśrutyam ādhānam katamat  tad ālambanaḥ yoni śas  manaskāraḥ ādarśaḥ katamaḥ tad ālambanaḥ sa nimittaḥ samādhiḥ ālokaḥ katamaḥ grāhya grāhaka an upalabdhi jñānam etad adhikṛtya suṣṭhu uktam buddhena bhagavatā pratibimbam manaḥ paśyan bodhisattvaḥ samāhitaḥ vyāvarttya viṣaye saṃjñā sva saṃjñām upadhārayan evam ātma stha cittaḥ  asau grāhya abhāvam vibodhayet  tatas ca grāhaka abhāvam na upalambham spṛśet tatas  iti āśrayaḥ katamaḥ āśraya parivṛttiḥ katham dharmeṣu dharma kuśalaḥ  bhavati bahu śruta tām upādāya katham artha kuśalaḥ  bhavati abhidharme abhivinaye lakṣaṇa jña tām upādāya katham vyañjana kuśalaḥ  bhavati sva  nirukta vyañjana jña tām upādāya katham nirukti kuśalaḥ  bhavati ātma ātmīya iti janapada niruktim anabhiniviśya anuvyavahāra jña tām upādāya katham pūrva anta aparānta anusandhi kuśalaḥ  bhavati pūrva ante udgrahaṇam tām apara ante niḥsaraṇam tām upādāya katham dharmeṣu dharma vihārī bhavati bhāvanām anāgamya kevala śruta cintā prayogeṇa na dharma vihārī bhavati śruta cintām anagamya kevala bhāvanā prayogeṇa na dharma vihārī bhavati ubhayam āgamya ubhaya vihāreṇa dharma vihārī bhavati udgrahāya svādhyāya deśa nābhiḥ śruta mayam draṣṭavyam samadhiprayoga asantuṣṭibhyām bhāvanā mayam draṣṭavyam prayogaḥ sātatya satkṛtya prayogeṇa aviparīta prayogeṇa ca draṣṭavyaḥ asantuṣṭiḥ anāsvādita uttaśa maya prayogeṇa draṣṭavyā kena kāraṇena vaipulyam bodhisattvānām pāramitā piṭakam ucyate pāramitānām saṃkhyā nirddeśa tām upādāya lakṣaṇa nirddeśa tām upādāya krama nirdeśa tām upādāya nirukti nirdeśa tām upādāya bhāvanā nirdeśa tā mupādāya prabheda nirdeśa tām upādāya saṃgraha nirdeśa tām upādāya vipakṣa nirdeśa tām upādaya guṇa varṇana nirdeśa tām upādāya anyaḥ  anya viniścayatām ca upādāya kena kāraṇena vaipulyam audāryam gāmbhīrya ca deśyate sarva ākāra jña tā ma udāra gambhīra tām upādaya kena kāraṇena vaipulye ekatyāḥ sattvā audārya gāmbhīryam na adhimucyante uttrasanti dharmatā viyukta tām upādāya anavaropita kuśala mūla tām upādāya pāpa mitra parigraha tām ca upādāya kena kāraṇena vaipulye ekatyāḥ sattvā adhimucyante adhimucya mānā api na niryānti svayaṃdṛṣṭi parāmarśa sthāpitayā idam ca sandhāya uktam bhagavatā mahā dharma ādarśe dharma paryāye bodhisattvasya yathāruta mayaḥ niśaḥ dharmān vicinvataḥ aṣṭāviṃśati rasa dṛṣṭaya utpadyante aṣṭāviṃśati rasa dṛṣṭayaḥ katamāḥ nimitta dṛṣṭiḥ prajñapti apavāda dṛṣṭiḥ parikalpa apavāda dṛṣṭiḥ tattva apavāda dṛṣṭiḥ parigraha dṛṣṭiḥ pariṇati dṛṣṭiḥ anavadyatā dṛṣṭiḥ niḥsaraṇa dṛṣṭiḥ avajñā dṛṣṭiḥ prakopa dṛṣṭiḥ viparīta dṛṣṭiḥ prasava dṛṣṭiḥ anabhyupagama dṛṣṭiḥ kusṛti dṛṣṭiḥ satkāra dṛṣṭi dṛḍha mūḍha tā dṛṣṭiḥ mūla dṛṣṭiḥ dṛṣṭau  adṛṣṭa dṛṣṭiḥ prayoga nirākaraṇa dṛṣṭiḥ anairyāṇika dṛṣṭiḥ āvaraṇa upacaya dṛṣṭiḥ apuṇya prasava dṛṣṭiḥ vaiphalya dṛṣṭiḥ nigrāhya dṛṣṭiḥ abhyākhyāna dṛṣṭiḥ akathya dṛṣṭiḥ mahādṛṣṭiḥ abhimāna dṛṣṭiḥ ca yad uktam vaipulye niḥsvabhāvāḥ sarva dharmā iti tatra kaḥ  abhisandhiḥ svayam abhāva tām upādāya svena ātmanā abhāva tām upādāya sve bhāve anavasthita ātma tā mupādāya bāla grāhavat ca alakṣaṇa tām upādāya api khalu parikalpite svabhāve lakṣaṇa niḥsvabhāva tām upādāya paratantre utpatti niḥsvabhāva tām upādāya pariniṣpanne parama artha niḥsvabhāva tām upādāya anutpannā aniruddhā ādiśāntāḥ prakṛti parinirvṛtā iti kaḥ  abhisandhiḥ yathā niḥsvabhāvāḥ tathā anutpannāḥ yathā anutpannāḥ tathā aniruddhāḥ yathā anutpannāḥ ca aniruddhāḥ ca tathā ādiśāntāḥ yathā ādiśāntā stathā prakṛti parinirvṛtāḥ api khalu catvāraḥ  abhiprāyāḥ yaiḥ vaipulye tathāgatānām abhiprāyaḥ  anugantavyaḥ samatā abhiprāyaḥ kāla antara abhiprāyaḥ artha antara abhiprāyaḥ pugdala āśaya abhiprāyaḥ ca catvāraḥ  abhisandhayaḥ  yaiva pulye tathāgatānām abhisandhiḥ anugantavyaḥ avatāraṇa abhisaṃdhiḥ lakṣaṇa abhisandhiḥ pratipakṣa abhisandhiḥ pariṇāma na abhisandhiḥ ca vaipulye dharma samādhi kuśalaḥ  bodhisattvaḥ katham pratyavagantavyaḥ pañcabhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ pratikṣaṇam sarva dauṣṭhulya āśrayam drāvayati nānātva saṃjñā vigatām ca dharmārām ratim pratilabhate aparicchinna ākāram vā apramāṇām dharma avabhāsam saṃjñānāti viśuddha bhāgīyāni ca asya avikalpitāni nimittāni samudācaranti dharma kāya paripūri pariniṣpattaye ca uttarāt uttarataram hetu maya parigraham karoti tatra pañcavidhāyām bhāvanāyām phalam pañcavidham nirvattiḥ tam iti darśayati pañcavidhā bhāvanā saṃbhinna bhāvanā animitta bhāvanā anābhoga bhāvanā uttapta bhāvanā parivṛtti nibhaḥ ḷ bhāvanā yathākramam kena kāraṇena vaipulya dharmaḥ  dhūpa mālya ādibhiḥ pūjyaḥ  na tathā śrāvaka dharmaḥ sarva sattva hita sukha adhiṣṭhāna tām upādāya abhidharma samuccaye dharma viniścayaḥ  nāma tṛtīyaḥ samuccayaḥ mahāyāna abhidharma samuccaya śāstre viniścaye prāpti paricchede tṛtīye prathamaḥ  bhāgaḥ prāpti viniścayaḥ katamaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ  dvividhaḥ pudgala vyavasthānataḥ abhisamaya vyavasthāpanataḥ ca draṣṭavyaḥ pudgala vyavasthānam katamat  samāsatas  saptavidham roga carita prabhedataḥ niryāṇa prabhedataḥ ādhāra prabhedataḥ prayoga prabhedataḥ phala prabhedataḥ dhātu prabhedataḥ caryā prabhedataḥ ca roga carita prabhedaḥ katamaḥ saptavidhaḥ rāga caritaḥ dveṣa carita moha caritaḥ māna caritaḥ vitarka caritaḥ sama bhāga caritaḥ manda rajaska caritaḥ ca pudgala prabhedaḥ niryāṇa prabhedaḥ katamaḥ trividhaḥ śrāvaka yānikaḥ pratyekabuddha yānikaḥ mahāyānikaḥ ca pudgala prabhedaḥ ādhāra prabhedaḥ katamaḥ trividhaḥ asaṃbhṛta saṃbhāraḥ saṃbhṛta asaṃbhṛta saṃbhāraḥ saṃbhṛta saṃbhāraḥ ca pudgala prabhedaḥ prayoga prabhedaḥ katamaḥ śraddhā anusārī dharma anusārī ca pudgala prabhedaḥ phala prabhedaḥ katamaḥ saptaviṃśatividhaḥ śraddhā adhimuktaḥ dṛṣṭi prāptaḥ kāya sākṣī prajñā vimuktaḥ ubhayatas bhāga vimuktaḥ strotāpatti phala pratipakṣakaḥ strotaāpannaḥ sakṛdāgāmi phala pratipannakaḥ sakṛdāgāmī anāgāmi phala pratipannakaḥ anāgāmī arhattva phala pratipannakaḥ arhan saptakṛt bhava paramaḥ kulaṃkulaḥ ekavīcikaḥ antarā aparinirvāyī upapadi parinirvāyī anabhisaṃskāra parinirvāyī sa abhisaṃskāra parinirvāyī ūrddvan  trotāḥ parihāṇa dharmā arhan cetanā dharmā arhan anurakṣaṇa adharmā arhan sthita akampyaḥ arhan prativedha dharmā arhan akopya dharmā arhan ca pudgala prabhedaḥ dhātu prabhedaḥ katamaḥ kāma avacaraḥ pṛthagjanaḥ śīkṣaḥ  aśaikṣaḥ ca evam trividhaḥ kāma avacaraḥ  rūpāvacara ārupya avacaraḥ kāma avacaraḥ  rūpāvacaraḥ ca bodhisattvaḥ kāma avacaraḥ pratyekabuddhaḥ acintyaḥ ca tathāgataḥ pudgala prabhedaḥ caryā prabhedaḥ katamaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ pañcavidhaḥ adhimukti cārī bodhisattvaḥ adhyāśaya cārī bodhisattvaḥ nimitta cārī bodhisattvaḥ animitta cāri bodhisattvaḥ anabhisaṃskāra cārī bodhisattvaḥ ca pudgala prabhedaḥ rāga caritaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ tīvrā yatarāgaḥ evam dveṣa caritaḥ  moha caritaḥ  māna caritaḥ  vitarka caritaḥ ca pudgalaḥ tīvra āyata viśiṣṭaḥ sama bhāga caritaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ prakṛti stha kleśaḥ manda rajaska caritaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ prakṛti sthatanutara kleśaḥ śrāvaka yānikaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ yaḥ samāpannaḥ  vā asamāpannaḥ  vā śrāvaka dharmatā vihārī prakṛtyā mṛdu indriyaḥ sva vimuktaye praṇihitaḥ vairāgya bhāvanayā vimukta āśayaḥ śrāvaka piṭakam avalambya vīrya bhāvanayā dharma anudharma cārī duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti pratyekabuddha yānikaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ yaḥ samāpannaḥ  vā asamāpannaḥ  vā pratyekabuddha dharmatā vihārī prakṛtyā madhya indriyaḥ sva vimuktaye praṇihitaḥ vairāgya bhāvanayā vimukta āśayaḥ kevala bhāvanayā ca adhigata vodhya āśayaḥ śrāvaka piṭakam avalambya vīrya bhāvanayā dharma anudharma cārī anutpādita pūrva nirvedha bhāgīyaḥ utpādita pūrva nirvedha bhāgīyaḥ aprāpta pūrvaphalaḥ abuddha laukikaḥ adhyātma cetanayā ārya mārga saṃmukhībhūtaḥ khaḍga viṣāṇa kalpaḥ eka vihārī pratyeka jinaḥ varc gacāri duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti mahāyānikaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ yaḥ samāpannaḥ  vā asamāpannaḥ  vā bodhisattva dharmatā vihārī prakṛtyā tīkṣṇa indriyaḥ sarva sattva vimokṣāya praṇihitaḥ apratiṣṭhita nirvāṇa āśayaḥ bodhisattva piṭakam avalambya vīrya bhāvanayā dharma anudharma cārī sattvān paripācayati śuddhām buddha bhūmim bhāvayati vyākaraṇam ca pratilabhate samyaksaṃbodhim ca sākṣātkaroti asaṃbhṛta saṃbhāraḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ satya ādhipateyam dharmam ālambya mṛdu mātra samutthitaḥ śuddha śraddhā adhimuktaḥ mṛdu mātrā mokṣa bhāgīya samanvāgataḥ aniyata janma kālikaḥ saṃbhṛta asaṃbhṛta saṃbhāraḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ satya ādhipateyam dharmam ālambya madhya mātra samutthitaḥ śuddha śraddhā adhimuktaḥ madhya mātra mokṣa bhāgīya samanvāgataḥ  niyata janma kālikaḥ saṃbhṛta saṃbhāraḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ satya adhipatayam dharmam ālambya adhimātra samutthitaḥ śuddha śraddhā adhimuktaḥ adhimātra mokṣa bhāgīya samanvāgataḥ tad janma kālikaḥ punar  asaṃbhṛta saṃbhāraḥ satya ādhipateyam dharmam ālambya satyeṣu mṛdu mātrasatya dharma nidhyāna kṣānti samanvāgataḥ  mṛdu mātra nirvedha bhāgīyasanva āgata anivata janma kālikaḥ saṃbhṛta asaṃbhṛta saṃbhāraḥ satya ādhipateyam dharmam ālambya satyeṣu madhya mātrasatya dharma nidhyāna kṣānti samanvāgataḥ madhya mātra nirvedha bhāgīya samanvāgataḥ  nithata janma kālikaḥ saṃbhṛta saṃbhāraḥ satya ādhipateyam dharmam ālambya satyeṣu adhimātrasatya dharma nidhyāna kṣānti samanvāgataḥ adhimātra nirvedha bhāgīya samanvāgataḥ tad janma kālikaḥ tatra tri mātra nirvedha bhāgīyaḥ laukika agra dharmam sthāpayitvā laukika agra dharma prakṛtyā eva kṣaṇikaḥ aprāvandhikaḥ tad janma kālikaḥ abhisamayam samāpadyamānaḥ  apūrvavastha mṛdu madhya adhimātra mokṣa bhāgīyebhyaḥ  [nirvedha] bhāgīyebhyaḥ ca parihīyate tad ca samudācāra parihāṇitaḥ  naḥ tu vāsanā parihāṇitaḥ śraddhā anusārī pudgalaḥ katamaḥ saṃbhṛta saṃbhāraḥ  mṛdu indriyaḥ para upadeśam anusmṛtya yaḥ satya abhisamayāya prayujyate dharma anusārī katamaḥ saṃbhṛta saṃbhāraḥ tīkṣṇa indriyaḥ svayam eva satya ādhipateyam dharmam anusmṛtya yaḥ
