[satyābhi]samayāya prayujyate śraddhā adhimuktaḥ katamaḥ phala kāle śraddhā anusārī yaḥ pugdalaḥ dṛṣṭi prāptaḥ katamaḥ phala kāle dharma anusārī yaḥ pudgalaḥ kāya sākṣī katamaḥ śaikṣaḥ aṣṭa vimokṣa dhyāyī yaḥ pudgalaḥ prajñā vimuktaḥ katamaḥ kṣīṇa āsravaḥ  bhotu aṣṭa vimokṣa dhyāyaḥ  yaḥ pugdalaḥ ubhayatas bhāga vimu[ktaḥ kata]maḥ kṣīṇa āsravaḥ  aṣṭa vimokṣa dhyāyī yaḥ pudgalaḥ strotāpatti phala pratipannakaḥ katamaḥ nirvedha bhāgīyeṣu pañcadaśasu darśana mārga citta kṣaṇeṣu yaḥ pudgalaḥ strota āpakṣaḥ katamaḥ ṣoḍaśe darśana mārga citta kṣaṇe yaḥ pudgalaḥ darśana mārgaḥ satyakatva niyāma avakrāntiḥ dharma abhi[samaye]pi saḥ kāmeṣu avīta rāgaḥ pudgalaḥ samyaktva niyāmam avakrāman strotaāpannaḥ  bhavati yad bhūyas  vīta rāgaḥ samyaktva niyāmam avakrāman sakṛdāgāmī bhavati kāmebhyaḥ  vīta rāgaḥ samyaktva niyāmam avakrāman  anāgāmī bhavati yadā darśana prahātavyānām kleśānām prahāṇāt  [stota ā]pannaḥ  bhavati kena kāraṇena trayāṇām saṃyojanānām prahāṇāt  strotaāpannaḥ  bhavati pradhāna saṃgraha ta abhavati prādhānyam kim upādāya anuccalana kāraṇa tām upādāya uccalitasya mithyā niryāṇa kāraṇa tām upādāya samyak aniryāṇa kāraṇa tām ca upādāya api khalu jñeya vipra[ti patti]kāraṇa tām upādāya dṛṣṭi vipratipatti kāraṇa tām upādāya pratipakṣa vipratipatti kāraṇa tām ca upādāya sakṛdāgāmi phala pratipannakaḥ katamaḥ bhāvanā mārge kāma avacarāṇām pañca prakārāṇām kleśānām prahāṇa mārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ sakṛdāgāmī katamaḥ bhāvanā mārge kāma avacarasya ṣaṣṭhasya kleśa prakā[rasya pra] hāṇa mārge yaḥ pugdalaḥ anāgāmi phala pratipannakaḥ katamaḥ bhāvanā mārge kāma avacarāṇām saptama aṣṭamānām kleśa prakārāṇām prahāṇa mārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ anāgāmī pudgalaḥ katamaḥ bhāvanā marge kāma avacarasya navamasya kleśa prakārasya prahāṇa mārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ yadā sarveṣām kāma avacarā[ṇām bhāva]nā prahāta vyānām prahāṇāt anāgāmī bhavati kena kāraṇena pañcānām avara bhāgīyānām saṃyojanā prahāṇāt anāgāmī iti ucyate pradhāna saṃgraham upādāya prādhānyam kim upādāya gati avara kāraṇa tām dhātu apara kāraṇa tām ca upādāya arhattva phala pratipannakaḥ katamaḥ yāvat bhāva agrikāṇām aṣṭa prakārāṇām [kleśānāṃ] prahāṇa mārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ arhan katamaḥ bhāvāmrikasya navamasya kleśa prakārasya prahāṇa mārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ yadā traidhātukānām kāma avacarāṇām sarvva kleśānām prahāṇāt arhan bhavati kena kāraṇena ūrdbhabhāgīyānām prahāṇāt arhan  iti ucyate pradhāna saṃgraham upādāya pradhāna saṃgrahaḥ ki[m upādāya] vimokṣa upādāna kāraṇa tām upādāya ūrddvā parityāga kāraṇa tām ca upādāya sapta kṛt bhavara paramaḥ katamaḥ strotaāpanna eva pudgalaḥ sapta kṛtvā u api miśraḥ miśra deva manuṣyeṣu bhavāt  saṃsṛtya yaḥ  duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti kulaṃkulaḥ katamaḥ deveṣu vā kulāt kulam gatvā [manuṣye]ṣu vā yaḥ  duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti ekavīcikaḥ katamaḥ sakṛdāgāmī deveṣu eva yaḥ  duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti antarā aparinirvāyī katamaḥ upapatti saṃyojane prahīṇe abhinivṛtti saṃyojane aprahīṇe antarā abhavam abhinirvarttayan  eva yaḥ  mārgam saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti abhinivṛttaḥ  vā antarā abhave upapatti bhava gamanāya cetayan  evayaḥ mārgam saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti abhisaṃcetayitvā vā upapatti bhavam abhisaṃprasthitaḥ [bhava anu]papatti  chandam yaḥ  mārgam saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti upapadi parinirvāyī katamaḥ ubhaya saṃyojane aprahīṇe rūpa dhātau  upapanna mātra eva yaḥ  mārgam saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti anabhisaṃskāra parinirvāyī katamaḥ upapannaḥ anabhisaṃskāreṇa yaḥ  mārgam saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti abhisaṃskāra parinirvāyī katamaḥ upapannaḥ  abhisaṃskāreṇa yaḥ  mārgam saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti ūrdhvan  trotāḥ katamaḥ upapannaḥ  rūpāvacarāṇām bhūmau bhūmau yāvat akaniṣṭha gān praviśya tad nānā srava mārgam saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti puna kaścid  yāvat  bhava agra gān mārgam saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasya antam anuprāpnoti api ca vyavakīrṇa bhāvitasya caturthasya dhyānasya pañca prakārā prabhedāḥ mṛdu paribhāvitam madhya paribhāvitam adhimātra paribhāvitam adhimātra adhimātrā paribhāvita madhya adhimātra paribhāvitam ca taiḥ vyavakīrṇa abhāvitasya caturtha dhyānasya pañca prabhedaiḥ yathākramam paścasu śuddhāvāseṣu upapattiḥ parihāṇa dharmā arhan katamaḥ mṛd u indriya prakṛti kaḥ vikṣiptaḥ  vā avikṣiptaḥ  vā cetayitvā vā acetayitvā vā dṛṣṭa dharma sukha vihārāt  parihāṇam eti cetanā dharmā arhan katamaḥ mṛd u indriya prakṛti kaḥ vikṣiptaḥ  vā avikṣiptaḥ  vā acetayitvā dṛṣṭa dharma sukha vihārāt  parihāṇam eti cetayitvā na parihāṇam eti anurakṣaṇa adharmā arhan katamaḥ mṛd u indriya prakṛti kaḥ vikṣiptaḥ  dṛṣṭa dharma sukha vihārāt  parihāṇam eti avikṣiptaḥ  na parihāṇam eti sthita akampyaḥ arhan katamaḥ mṛdu indriya prakṛti kaḥ vikṣiptaḥ  vā avikṣiptaḥ  vā dṛṣṭa dharma sukha vihārāt  na parihāṇam eti na api indriyāṇi uttāpayati prativedhanā dharmā arhan katamaḥ mṛd u indriya aprakṛti kaḥ vikṣiptaḥ  vā avikṣiptaḥ  vā dṛṣṭa dharma sukha viharāt  na parihāṇam eti kevala mindriyā ṇi uttāpayati akopya dharmā arhan katamaḥ tīkṣṇa indriya prakṛti kaḥ vikṣiptaḥ  va avikṣiptaḥ  vā na dṛṣṭa dharma sukha vihārāt  parihāṇam eti kāma avacaraḥ pṛthagjanaḥ katamaḥ kāmadhātau  upapannaḥ  bhavati āryadha prāptaḥ pudgalaḥ ca kāma avacaraḥ śaikṣaḥ katamaḥ kāma ādhātau  upapannaḥ  bhavati adharmam ca prāptaḥ pudgalaḥ saṃyojanam ca avaśiṣyate kāma avacaraḥ  aśaikṣaḥ katamaḥ kāma ādhātau  upapannaḥ  bhavati ārya dharmam ca prāptaḥ pudgalaḥ saṃyojanam na avaśiṣyate yathā kāma avacarāḥ trayaḥ tathā rūpāvacarā ārupya vacarā api kāma avacaraḥ  rūpāvacaraḥ  bodhisattvaḥ katamaḥ ārūpya dhātu vyavakarṣitena dhyānena saṃprayuktaḥ  dhyāna sukhaiḥ viharati iti kāmadhātau  api upapannaḥ  rūpa dhātau  api upapannaḥ pudgala kāma avacaraḥ pratyekabuddhaḥ katamaḥ abuddha bhave kāmadhātau svatas  pratyekabuddha bodhim abhisaṃbuddhaḥ acintyaḥ tathāgataḥ katamaḥ kāmadhātau tuṣita bhavanayāsam ārabhya yāvat  mahāparinirvāṇam darśayati sarvām bodhisattva caryām buddhacaryām mahā caryām darśayati iti pudgalaḥ adhimukti cārī bodhisattvaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ adhimukti caryā bhūmau sthitaḥ  mṛdu madhya adhimātra bodhisattva kṣānti samanvāgataḥ pudgalaḥ adhyāśaya cārī bodhisattvaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ daśasu bhūmiṣu sthitaḥ  yaḥ  bodhisattvaḥ sa nimitta cārī bodhisattvaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ pramudita avimalā prabhā karī arciṣmatī su durjaya abhimukhībhūmiṣu sthitaḥ  yaḥ  bodhisattvaḥ animitta cārī bodhisattvaḥ pudgalaḥ katamaḥ duraṃgam abhūmau sthitaḥ  yaḥ  bodhisattvaḥ anabhisaṃskāra cārī bodhisattvaḥ pudgalaḥ katamataḥ acalā sādhu matī dharma meghāsu bhūmiṣu sthitaḥ  yaḥ  bodhisattvaḥ punar  khalu strotaāpannaḥ pugdalaḥ  yad uktaḥ sa dvividhaḥ kramanairyāṇikaḥ sakṛt nairyāṇikaḥ ca krasanaiḥ yāṇikaḥ  yathā purva m uktaḥ sa kṛnnaiḥ yāṇikaḥ satya abhisamayam abhisaṃpraviṣṭaḥ aprāpta samāpattim āśritya adhigatena loka uttaram agreṇa sakṛta traidhātukā vacarān sarva kleśān prajahāti prakāraśas  prajahāti dvayoḥ phalayaḥ  strotāpatti phala arhattva phalayoḥ prajñāpyate sa ca pudgalaḥ  bhūyaḥ dṛṣṭe dharme maraṇa kāle ājñām ārāgayati yadi na ārāgayati praṇidhāna vaśena tarhi praṇidhāna vaśena kāmadhātau  eva upapannaḥ avuddha bhave pratyeka jinobhavati atha viniścaye prāpti paricchede tṛtīye dvitīyaḥ  bhāgaḥ abhisamaya vyavasthānam katamat  samāsatas  daśavidham dharma abhisamayaḥ artha abhisamayaḥ tattva abhisamayaḥ pṛṣṭha abhisamayaḥ ratna abhisamayaḥ asamudācāra abhisamayaḥ niṣṭhā abhisamayaḥ śrāvaka abhisamayaḥ pratyekabuddha abhisamayaḥ bodhisattva abhisamayaḥ ca dharma abhisamayaḥ katamaḥ satya ādhipateyeṣu dharmeṣu adhimātrasya adhimukti prasādasya pratilambhaḥ yathā saṃpratyayam caryā ca artha abhisamayaḥ katamaḥ satya ādhipateyeṣu dharmeṣu adhimātrāyāḥ satyeṣu dhama nidhyāna kṣānteḥ pratilambhaḥ sā kṣānti nirvedha bhāgīya avasthām gatā sā punar trividhena yoni śas  manaskāreṇa prabhāvitā sa trividhaḥ tu adhimātra mṛduḥ adhimātra madhyaḥ  adhimātra adhimātraḥ ca tattva abhisamayaḥ katamaḥ ṣoḍaśe darśana mārga citta kṣaṇe ya ārya mārgam pratilabhate darśana mārge punar  satye vyavasthāpana ādi abhisamaya antikāni saṃmukhīkaroti bhāvanā mārge tad saṃvṛti jñānāni pratilabhate na tu saṃmukhīkaroti bhāvanā mārge tad saṃvṛti jñāna balena saṃmukhīkaroti pṛṣṭha abhisamayaḥ katamaḥ sarvaḥ  bhāvanā mārgaḥ ratna abhisamayaḥ katamaḥ buddhe avetya prasādaḥ dharme atya prasādaḥ saṃghe avetya prasādaḥ asamudācāra abhisamayaḥ katamaḥ akāraṇa saṃvara lābhāt  śikṣā gatasya yadā ātmanaḥ  naraka kṣayam tiryagyoni kṣayaḥ preta yoni kṣayaḥ avāṅpatana durgati kṣayaḥ iti na punar upādāya tad  durgati karma durgati vipākaḥ  abhinirvarttate niṣṭhā abhisamayaḥ katamaḥ yathā mārga satye niṣṭhā mārga uktaḥ śrāvaka abhisamayaḥ katamaḥ pūrva uktaḥ saptavidhaḥ  abhisamayaḥ śrāvakāṇām paratas  ghoṣam āgamya pratilambhataḥ śrāvaka abhisamaya iti ucyate pratyekabuddha abhisamayaḥ katamaḥ pūrva uktāḥ sapta abhisamayāḥ paratas  ghoṣam anāgamya pratilambhataḥ pratyekabuddha abhisamaya iti ucyate bodhisattva abhisamayaḥ katamaḥ pūrva ukteṣu sapta abhisamayeṣu yā samudāgama kṣāntiḥ naḥ tu sakṣāt kiryā kevalam bodhisattva pramuditā abhūmau bodhisattvasya samyaktva niyāma avakrāntiḥ sā bodhisattva abhisamayaḥ  veditavyāḥ śrāvaka abhisamayāt  bodhisattva abhisamayasya kaḥ  viśeṣaḥ saṃkṣepata ekādaśa ālambana viśeṣaḥ upastambha viśeṣaḥ prativedha viśeṣaḥ abhyupagama viśeṣaḥ niryāṇa viśeṣaḥ parigraha viśeṣaḥ vyavasthāna viśeṣaḥ pratiṣṭhā parivāra viśeṣaḥ abhijanma viśeṣaḥ janma viśeṣaḥ phala viśeṣaḥ ca phala viśeṣaḥ punar daśavidhaḥ āśraya parivṛtti viśeṣataḥ guṇa samṛddhi viśeṣataḥ pañca ākāra viśeṣataḥ trikāya viśeṣataḥ nirvāṇa viśeṣataḥ miśra upamiśra jñāna śakti lābha viśeṣataḥ āvaraṇa viśuddhi viśeṣataḥ miśra upamiśra karma kriyā viśeṣataḥ abhisaṃbodhi nirvāṇa sandarśana upāya viśeṣataḥ pañca ākāra paritrāṇa viśeṣataḥ ca veditavyaḥ apramāṇa ādi vaiśeṣika guṇānām katamaiḥ abhisamayaiḥ saṃgrahaḥ pṛṣṭha abhisamaya niṣṭhā abhisamayābhyām saṃgrahaḥ  veditavyaḥ teṣām saṃgrahaḥ punar  katamaḥ apramāṇāni vimokṣāḥ abhibhva āyatanāni kṛtsa āyatanāni araṇā praṇīdhi jñānam pratisaṃvidaḥ abhijñā lakṣaṇa anuvyañjanāni pariśuddhayaḥ valāni vaiśāradyāni smṛti upasthānāni arakṣāṇi asaṃpramoṣa dharma tā vāsanā samuddhātaḥ mahākaruṇā āveṇikā buddha dharmāḥ sarva ākāra jña tā iti evamādayaḥ  guṇā yathā sūtra antareṣu nirdiṣṭāḥ apramāṇāni katamāni catvāri apramāṇāni maitrī katamā dhyānam niśritya sattvāḥ sukhena saṃprayujyeran  iti vihāra samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā tad saṃprayuktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ karuṇā katamā dhyānam niśritya sattvā duḥkhena viyujyeran  iti vihāra samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  muditā katamā dhyānam niśritya sattvāḥ sukhena na viyujyeran  iti vihāra samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  upekṣā katamā dhyānam niśritya sattvā hita labheran  iti vihāra samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  vimokṣāḥ katame aṣṭau vimokṣāḥ katham rūpī rūpāṇi paśyati iti dhyānam niśritya adhyātmam draṣṭari rūpa saṃjñāyāḥ  avibhāvānād draṣṭarī rūpa saṃjñāyāḥ saṃniveśanāt  vā dṛśya rūpa ādi paśyati iti vihāra samṛddhaḥ  samādhiḥ prajñā tad saṃprayuktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ yāvat  nirmāṇa āvaraṇāt  vimuktiḥ katham adhyātmam rūpa saṃjñī vahirddhā rūpāṇi paśyati dhyānam niśritya draṣṭari rūpa saṃjñāyāḥ  vibhāvanāt  arūpa saṃjñāyāḥ saṃniveśanāt vā dṛśya rūpāṇi paśyati iti vihāra samṛddhau samādhi prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  katham śubham vimokṣam kāyena sākṣātkṛtya upasaṃpadya viharati iti dhyānam niśritya adhyātmam śubha aśubheṣu rūpeṣu anyonya apekṣā saṃjñāyāḥ  anyonya anugama saṃjñāyā anyonya eka rasa saṃjñāyāḥ ca labhāt  tatra labdhe vihāra samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  yāvat  śubha śubha nirmāṇāt  saṃkleśa utpatti āvaraṇāt ca vimuktiḥ ākāśānantya āyatana vimokṣaḥ katamaḥ vimokṣa anukūlā kāśānanti āyatana vimokṣaḥ tathā vijñāna ānanti āyatana ākiṃcanya āyatana na eva saṃjñāna asaṃjñā āyatana vimokṣā api draṣṭavyaḥ yāvat  vimokṣaḥ śāntaḥ  vimokṣaḥ asakti āvaraṇam ca saṃjñā vedayita nirodha vimokṣaḥ katamaḥ na eva saṃjñāna saṃjñā āyatana vimokṣam niśritya samatikrāntānām śiṣṭe śānte vimokṣe mokṣa anusadṛśaḥ  vihāraḥ vihāra samṛddhau ca citta caitasikānām nirodhaḥ saṃjñā vedayita nirodha āvaraṇāt  vimukti artham abhibhva āyatanāni katamāni aṣṭau  abhibhva āyatanāni pūrvāṇī catvāri abhibhva āyatanāni dvābhyām vimokṣābhyām vyavasthāpyante uttarāṇi catvāri abhibhvāvatanāni ekena vimokṣeṇa vyavasthāpyante tatra vimokṣaiḥ ālambanam adhimucyate abhibhva āyataneṣu ālambana prabhibhavati vaśa varttana tā mupādāya sattva saṃkhyātāni asattva saṃkhyātāni ca āśritya rūpāṇi parittādhimātrāṇi ucyante śubha aśubhāni āśritya rūpāṇi suvarṇa durvarṇāni ucyante mānuṣyaka divyāni āśritya rūpāṇi hīna praṇītāni ucyante śiṣṭāni yathā vimokṣeṣu uktāni ālambana abhibhavana tām upādāya abhibhva āyatanāni iti ucyante kṛtsnā āyatanāni katamāni daśa kṛtsnā āyatanāni kṛtsna spharaṇa ālambana tām upādāya kṛtsnā āyatanāni iti ucyate kṛtsna spharaṇa vihāra samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā tad saṃprayuktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ kṛtsnā āyatanāni iti ucyante kim upādāya kṛtsnā āyataneṣu pṛthivī ādi vyavasthāpanam taiḥ kṛtsnā āyatanaiḥ āśraya āśrita rūpāṇi paśyati iti kṛtsna spharaṇa tām upadaya śiṣṭāni yathāyogam vimokṣavat  tathā ca kṛtsnā āyatanaiḥ pariniṣpattiḥ vimokṣāṇām araṇā katamā dhyānam niśritya kleśa utpatti anurakṣā vihāra samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā tad saṃprayuktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ praṇidhi jñānam katamat  dhyānam niśritya jñeya jñāna praṇidhi samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  pratisaṃvidaḥ katamāḥ catasraḥ pratisaṃvidaḥ dharma pratisaṃvid  katamā dhyānam niśritya sarva dharma paryāyeṣu avyāghāta samṛddhau samādhīḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  artha pratisaṃvid  katamā dhyānam niśritya lakṣaṇe abhiprāye ca avyāghāta samṛddau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  nirukti pratisaṃvid  katamā dhyānam niśritya janapada bhāpāyām anuvyavahāre dharma nirvacane ca avyāghāta samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  pratibhāna pratisaṃvid  katamā dhyānam niśritya dharma prabhedeṣu avyāghāta samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  abhijñā katamāḥ ṣaḍabhijñāḥ ṛddhi abhijñā katamā dhyānam niśritya vicitrā ṛddhi vikurvita samṛddhau samādhiḥ prajñā tad sa prayuktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ divya śrotra abhijñā katamā dhyānam niśritya vicitrāṇām śabdānām anuśrava samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  cetaḥ paryāya abhijñā katamā dhyānam niśritya para sattveṣu citta carita paryāya praveśa samṛddhau yaḥ samādhi prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  pūrva nivāsa anusmṛti abhijñā katamā dhyānam niśritya pūrva anta caryā anusmaraṇa samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  cyuti upapāda abhijñā katamā dhyānam niśritya sattvānām cyuti upapāda prakāra saṃdarśana samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  āsrava kṣaya abhijñā katamā dhyānam niśritya āsrava kṣaya jñāna samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā tad saṃprayuktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ lakṣaṇa anuvyañjanāni katamāni dhyānam niśritya lakṣaṇa anuvyañjanaiḥ vibhrājamāna sandarśana samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā tad saṃprayūktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ tad samutthita vipākāḥ ca pariśuddhayaḥ katamāḥ catasraḥ pariśuddhayaḥ āśraya pariśuddhiḥ katamāḥ dhyānam niśritya yathākāma m aśrayasya upādāne sthāna parityāgānām samṛddhau yaḥ samādhīḥ prajñā tad saṃprayuktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ ālambana pariśuddhiḥ katamā dhyānam niśritya yathākāmam ālambana nirmāṇa pariṇāmana jñānānām samṛddhau yaḥ samādhi prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  citta pariśuddhiḥ katamā dhyānam niśritya yathākāmam samādhi mukha vaśa vartti samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  jñāna pariśuddhiḥ katamā dhyānam niśritya yathākāmam dhāraṇī mukha sandhāraṇa samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  balāni katamāni baśa tathāgata balāni sthāna āsthāna balam katamat  dhyānam niśritya sarva prakāra sthāna āsthāna jñāna samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā tad saṃprayuktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ karma svaka jñāna balam katamat  dhyānam niśritya sarva prakāra karma svaka jñāna samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  śiṣṭāni balāni yathāyogam veditavyāni vaiśāradyāni katamāni catvāri vaiśāradyāni abhisaṃbodhi vaiśāradyam katamat  dhyānam niśritya sva artham eva ārabhya sarva ākāra jñeya abhisaṃbodhi pratijñā pratiṣṭhāpana samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā tad saṃprayuktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ āsrava kṣaya vaiśāradyam katamat  dhyānam niśritya sva artham eva ārabhya sarva ākāra srava kṣaya pratijñā pratiṣṭhāpana samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  antarāyika dharma vaiśāradyam katamat  dhyānam niśritya para artham ārabhya sarva ākāra antarāyika dharma pratijñā pratiṣṭhāpana samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  nairyāṇika pratipada vaiśāradyam katamat  dhyānam niśritya para artham ārabhya sarva ākāra nairyāṇika mārga dharma pratijñā pratiṣṭhāpana samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  smṛti upasthānāni katamāni trīṇi eva smṛti upasthānāni gaṇa parikarṣaṇe sarva ākāra saṃkleśa asamudācāra samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam purvavat  arakṣāṇi katamāni trīṇi eḥ avārakṣāṇi gaṇa parikarṣaṇe yathā kāmam avavāda anuśāsanī prayoga samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  asaṃpramoṣa dharma tā katamā sarva ākārasya yathāvat  kṛta ssa bhāṣitasya ca abhilapana samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  vāsanā samudghātaḥ katamaḥ sarvajñasya sataḥ asarvajña ceṣṭitā samudācā ra samṛddau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  mahākaruṇā katamā nirantaram sarva prakāra duḥkha ālambana karuṇā vihāra samṛddau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  āveṇikā buddha dharmāḥ katame aṣṭādaśa āveṇikā buddha dharmāḥ asādhāraṇa kāyava aṅgana skartha pariśuddhi sa mṛddau sa āśrayāṇām saphalānām tathāgata indriyāṇam aprāpti āma parihāṇi samṛddhau asādhāraṇa karma samudācāra samṛddhau asādhāraṇa jñāna vihāra samṛddhau ca yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā śeṣam pūrvavat  sarva ākāra jña tā katamā skandha dhātu āyatanānām sarva ākāra jña tā samṛddhau yaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā tad saṃprayuktāḥ ca citta caitasikā dharmāḥ eteṣām guṇānam abhinirhāraḥ katamaḥ viśuddhāni catvāri dhyānāni niśritya anyatīrthīyaḥ śrāvakaḥ  bodhisattvaḥ  vā abhinirharati catvāri apramāṇāni evam pañca abhijñāḥ śeṣān guṇān prānta koṭikam caturtham dhyānam niśritya śrāvakaḥ  bodhisattvaḥ tathāgataḥ  vā abhinirharati tad punar  kim upādāya dhyāna sanniśrayeṇa yathā vyavasthāna manasikārava hulīkāra tām upādāya ta ete guṇā dvividhāḥ sva kāritra pratyupasthānāḥ ca vaihārikāḥ ca ye sva kāritra pratyupasthānāḥ te loka uttara pṛṣṭha labdhāḥ saṃvṛti jñāna svabhāvā draṣṭavyāḥ ye punar vaihārikāḥ te loka uttara jñāna svabhāvā draṣṭavyāḥ apramāṇaiḥ kim karma karoti vipakṣam jahāti anukampā vihāritayā puṇya saṃbhāram paripūrayati sattva paripāke ca na parikhidyate vimokṣaiḥ kim karma karoti nirmāṇa karma abhinirharati śubha nirmāṇe na saṃkliśyate śānteṣu vimokṣeṣu na sajjati parama praśāntena cārya vihāreṇa viharati adhimucyana tā mupādāya abhibhva āyatanaiḥ kim karma karoti trayāṇām vimokṣāṇām ālambanam vaśe varttayati ālambana abhi bhavana tām upādāya kṛtsnā āyatanaiḥ kim karma karoti vimokṣa ālambanam pariniṣpādayati kṛtsna spharaṇa tām upādāya araṇayā kim karma karoti ādeya vacanaḥ  bhavati praṇidhi jñānena kim karma karoti bhūta bhavya varttamānam vyākaroti bahu mataḥ ca bhavati lokasya pratisaṃvidbhiḥ kim karma karoti deśanayā sattva cittāni saṃtoṣayati abhijñābhiḥ kim karma karoti śāsane kāya karmaṇā āvarjayati vākkarmaṇā citta ādeśanayā āvarjayati sattva caritam ca jñātvā āgatim ca gatim ca niḥsaraṇe sattvān yathāvat avavadate lakṣaṇa anuvyañjanaiḥ kim karma karoti darśana mātrakeṇa mahāpuruṣa tve saṃpratyayam janayati cittāni abhiprasādayati pariśuddhibhiḥ kim karma karoti saṃcintya bhava upapattim parigṛṇhāti ākāṅkṣayan kalpam vā kalpa avaśeṣam vā tiṣṭhati āyuḥ saṃskārān vā utsṛjati dharmavaśavarttī bhavati samādhi vaśa vartī saddharmam ca sandhārayati balaiḥ kim karma karoti ahetu viṣama hetuvādam pratyākhāya akṛta abhyāgama vāde ca samyak bhyudaya mārgam deśayati sattva citta caritāni ca anupraviśya deśanā bhājana tām ca āśayam ca anuśayam ca ālambanam ca saṃbhāram ca bhavyatām ca niḥsaraṇam ca yathāvat niḥśreyasa mārgam deśayati sarvam ārān  ca nigṛṇhāti sarvatra ca praśnam pṛcchati pṛṣṭaḥ  vyākaroti vaiśāradyaiḥ kim karma karoti parṣadi samyak ātmanaḥ śāstṛ tvam vyavasthā apahati ca udakān  ca anya tīrthyāt nigṛṇhāti smṛti upasthānaiḥ kim karma gaṇam avavadate samanuśāsti asaṃmoṣa dharma tayā kim karma karoti buddha kṛtyam na hāpayati vāsanā samudghātena kim karma karoti niḥkleśaḥ kleśa pratirūpām ceṣṭān na da rśayati mahā karuṇayā kim karma karoti ṣaṣ kṛtvā u rātriṃdivasena lokam vyavalokayati āveṇikaiḥ buddha dharmaiḥ kim karma karoti sarva śrāvaka pratyekabuddhān kāya vāc manaskarma pariśuddhyā prāptyā cāreṇa vihāreṇa vā abhibhavati sarva ākāra jña tayā kim karma karoti sarva sattvānām sarva saṃśayām śchinatti dharmanetrīñca dīrgha kālam avasthāpayati yena paripakṣā ḷ kṣyāḥ sattvāḥ paripacyante paripakāḥ ca vimucyante eṣu abhisamayeṣu uttarottaram viśiṣṭam mārgam labhamānaḥ pūrvakam hīnam mārgam vijahāti saṃkalana prahāṇam ca sākṣātkaroti nirupadhi śeṣe nirvāṇa dhātau śrāvakaḥ sarvam mārga samavasarga vihānyā vijahāti naḥ tu bodhisattvaḥ ataeva bodhisattvā akṣaya kuśala mūlā akṣa ya guṇā iti ucyante yāni avyākṛta vastūni vyavasthāpitāni kim upādāya ayoniśaḥ paripraśna tām upādāya ayoniśaḥ paripraśna tā kim upādāya hetu phala saṃkleśa vyavadāna cintā pasri varjana tām upādāya 0 kena kāraṇena bodhisattvaḥ  bodhim anava vadyām avakrāntaḥ strota āpannaḥ  na bhavati strotaḥ pratipatti apariniṣpanna tām upādāya kena kāraṇena sakṛdāgāmī na bhavati apramāṇa saṃcintya bhava upapratti parigraha tām upādāya kena kāraṇena anāgāmī na bhavati dhyānaiḥ vihṛtya kāmadhātau  upapad yāna tām upādāya bodhisattvaḥ satyāni abhi samayena labdhvā daśasu mūmiṣu bhāvanā mārgeṇa jñeya āvaraṇa pratipakṣa mārgam bhāvayati na kleśa āvaraṇa pratipakṣa mārgam tathā ca bodhi prāptaḥ kleśa āvaraṇam jñeya āvaraṇam ca vijahāti arhan tathāgataḥ ca saṃpadyate sa ca bodhisattvaḥ sarva kleśa aprahāṇāt  mantra uṣadhayaḥ  viṣam iva sarva kleśān abhibhavati sarvān kleśān doṣān  ca na utpādayati sarvāsu bhūmiṣu arhan  iva kleśān prajahāti api khalu bodhisattvaḥ  jñeyeṣu bhāvanā kuśalaḥ  bhavati upāyeṣu bhāvanā kuśalaḥ  bhavati abhūta parikalpeṣu bhāvanā kuśalaḥ  bhavati nirvikalpeṣu bhāvanā kuśalaḥ  bhavati tena kālena kālam indriyāṇi uttāpayati jñeyam katamat  saṃkṣepeṇa ṣaḍvidham bhrāntiḥ bhrāntyāśrayaḥ abhrāntyāśrayaḥ bhrāntyabhrāntiḥ abhrāntiḥ abhrānti niṣyandaḥ ca upāya kauśalyam katamat  saṃkṣeparāḥ caturvidham sattva paripāka kauśalyam buddha dharma paripuraṇa kauśalyam kṣipra abhijñā kauśalyam mārga an upaccheda kauśalyam ca abhūta parikalpaḥ katamaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ  daśavidhaḥ mūla vikalpaḥ nimitti vikalpaḥ nimitta pratibhāsa vikalpaḥ nimitta vikāra vikalpaḥ nimitti pratibhāsa vikāra vikalpaḥ para upanīta vikalpaḥ ayoniśas vikalpaḥ yoni śovi kalpaḥ abhiniveśa vikalpaḥ vikṣepa vikalpaḥ ca sa punar  daśavidhaḥ abhāva vikalpa bhāva vikalpaḥ samāropa vikalpaḥ apavāda vikalpaḥ ekatva vi kalpaḥ pṛthaktu vikalpaḥ svabhāva vikalpaḥ viśeṣa vikalpaḥ yathā nāma artha vikalpaḥ yathārtha nām avikalpaḥ ca nirvikalpa tā katamā samāsatas trividhā santuṣṭi nirvikalpa tā aviparyāsa nirghi kalpatā niṣprapañca nirvikalpa tā ca tā imāḥ titraḥ pṛthagjana śrāvaka bodhisattvānām yathākramam veditavyāḥ yā asau nimittatas  niṣprapañca nirvikalpa tā tasyāḥ punar  abhāvasya pañca nimittāni na amanasikā rataḥ na manasikāra samatikramataḥ na vyupaśamataḥ na svabhāvataḥ na ālambane abhisaṃskārataḥ ca api khalu ālaṃbane anabhisaṃskārataḥ bodhisattvaḥ prakṛtyā tīkṣṇa indriyaḥ katham punar  indriya api uttāpayati iti tīkṣṇa mṛd u indriyam āśritya tīkṣṇa madhya indriyam abhinirharati punar  tīkṣṇa madhya indriyam āśritya tīkṣṇa tīkṣṇa indriyam abhinirharati iti abhidharma samuccaye prāpti viniścayaḥ  nāma caturthaḥ samuccayaḥ atha mahāyā anabhidharma samuccaya śāstre viniścaya bhāge sāṃkathya paricchedaḥ caturthaḥ sāṃkathya viniścayaḥ katamaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ saptavidhaḥ artha viniścayaḥ vyākhyā viniścayaḥ prabhidya saṃdarśana viniścayaḥ saṃpraśna viniścayaḥ saṃgraha viniścayaḥ vāda viniścayaḥ abhisandhi viniścayaḥ ca artha viniścayaḥ katamaḥ yatra ṣaṣ arthān ārabhya viniścayaḥ  bhavati katame ṣaṣ arthāḥ svabhāva arthaḥ hetu arthaḥ phala arthaḥ karma arthaḥ yoga arthaḥ vṛtti arthaḥ ca svabhāva arthaḥ traṃyaḥ svabhāvāḥ hetu arthaḥ trayaḥ  hetavaḥ utpatti hetuḥ pravṛtti hetuḥ siddhi hetuḥ ca phala arthaḥ pañca phalāni vipāka phalam niṣyanda phalam adhipati phalam puruṣakāra phalam visaṃyoga phalam ca karma arthaḥ pañca karmāṇi upalabdhi karma kāritra karma vyāvasāya karma pariṇati karma prāpti karma ca yoga arthaḥ pañca yogāḥ sāmūhikaḥ  yogaḥ ānubandhikaḥ  yogaḥ sāṃbandhikaḥ  yogaḥ āvasthikaḥ yogaḥ vaikārikaḥ  yogaḥ ca vṛtti arthaḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ lakṣaṇa vṛttiḥ avasthāna vṛttiḥ viparyāsa vṛttiḥ aviparyāsa vṛttiḥ prabheda vṛttiḥ ca vyākhyā viniścayaḥ katamaḥ yena sūtrāntān vyācaṣṭe sa punar  katamaḥ saṃkṣepeṇa ṣaḍvidhaḥ parijñeya vastu parijñeyaḥ  arthaḥ parijñā upaniṣad parijñā parijñā phalam tad pravedanā ca api khalu caturdaśa mukhāni vyākhyā viniścayasya katamāni caturdaśa vyākhyā saṃgraha mukham vastu saṃgraha mukham aṅga upāṅga mukham uggara uttara nirhāra mukham pratikṣepa mukham akṣara pariṇāma mukham nāśā nāśa mukham pudgala vyavasthāna mukham prabheda vyavasthāna mukham naya mukham parijñā ādi mukham balā bala mukham pratyāhāra mukham abhinirhāra mukham ca prabhidya saṃdarśana viniścayaḥ katamaḥ yathā nirdiṣṭeṣu skandha ādiṣu dharmeṣu yathāyogam ekāvacarakaḥ pūrvapadakaḥ paścāt padakaḥ dvi koṭikaḥ tri koṭikaḥ catuṣkoṭikaḥ oṃkāritaḥ prātikṣepika iti evamādayaḥ saṃpraśna viniścayaḥ katamaḥ aṣṭa ākāra kāya deśena aṣṭa ākārayāya deśane ca praśna vyākaraṇena sarva satya mithyā viniścayaḥ api khalu catvāraḥ saṃpraśna viniścaya mārgāḥ dūṣakaḥ pratiṣṭhāpakaḥ chedakaḥ bodhakaḥ ca saṃgraha viniścayaḥ katamaḥ daśabhiḥ sthānaiḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ  viniścayaḥ katamāni daśa sthānāni kṛtya anuṣṭhāna viniścaya sthānam avatāra viniścaya sthānam adhimukti viniścaya sthānam yukti viniścaya sthānam sāṃkathya viniścaya sthānam prativedha viniścaya sthānam viśuddhi viniścaya sthānam abhinirhāra pada prabheda viniścaya sthānam anābhoga ābhoga mātra sarva artha siddhi viniścaya sthānam ca vāda viniścayaḥ katamaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ saptavidhaḥ vādaḥ vāda adhikaraṇam vāda adhiṣṭhānam bāda alaṃkāraḥ vāda nigrahaḥ vāda niḥsaraṇam bāde bahu karā dharmāḥ ca prathamaḥ  vādaḥ punar  ṣaḍvidhaḥ vādaḥ pravādaḥ vivādaḥ apavādaḥ anuvāda avavāḥ ca vādaḥ sarva loka vacanam pravādaḥ loka anuśrutaḥ  vādaḥ loka jñāna pravādataḥ vivādaḥ parasparam viruddhayoḥ vāde avasthānam apavādaḥ parasparam kopa saṃrambha pāruṣya nacanam anuvādaḥ viśuddha jñāna darśana anukūlaḥ sāṃkathya viniścayaḥ avavādaḥ sattvānām asamāhita cittānām citta samādhānāya samāhita cittānām vimokṣa lābhāya deśanā vādaḥ dvitīyam vāda adhikaraṇam rāja kulam vā prajā kulam vā prāmāṇikānām sahāyakānām dharma artha kuśalānām śramaṇa brāhmaṇānām nāda sabhā vā tṛtīyam vāda adhiṣṭhānam yad adhiṣṭhāya vādaḥ kriyate saṃkṣepataḥ  dvividham sādhyam sādhanam ca sādhyam dvividham svabhāvaḥ  viśeṣaḥ ca sādhanāni aṣṭau pratijñā hetuḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ upanayaḥ nigamanam pratyakṣam anumānam āpta āgamaḥ ca sādhyasya svabhāvaḥ ātma svabhāvaḥ  dharma svabhāvaḥ  vā viśeṣaḥ ātma viśeṣaḥ  dharma viśeṣaḥ  vā pratijñā sādhyasya sva rucita arthasya para saṃprāpaṇa vijñāpanā hetuḥ tasmin  eva sādhye apratītasya arthasya saṃpratyaya nimittam pratyakṣa upalambhānupalambha samākhyānam dṛṣṭānta dṛṣṭa antena adṛṣṭā asya antasya samīkaraṇa samākhyānam upanayaḥ śiṣṭa tad jātīya rmma apagamāya nayatva samākhyānam nigamanam niṣṭhā gamana samākhyānam prasvasat prakāśa abhra antaḥ  arthaḥ anumānam pratyakṣa śiṣṭa saṃpratyayaḥ āpta āgamaḥ tadu viruddha upadeśaḥ caturthaḥ  vāda alaṃkāraḥ vāda adhiṣṭhāne samyak yuktibhiḥ vāda sabhāyām gambhīraḥ  nipuṇaḥ ca bhavati iti vāda alaṃkāra iti ucyate sa punar  ṣaḍvidhaḥ sva para samaya jña tā vākkaraṇa saṃpad vaiśaradyam pratibhānam sthairyam dākṣiṇyam ca pañcamaḥ  vāda nigrahaḥ kathā tyāgaḥ kathā sādaḥ kathā doṣaḥ ca kathā tyāgaḥ svāvāda doṣa abhyupagamaḥ para vāa guṇa abhyupagamaḥ ca kathā sādaḥ anya vastu pratisaraṇena vyāvṛttiḥ bāhya vastu vacanena mūla paratijñā parityāgaḥ krodha mada mānamrākṣa ādi pradarśanam ca yathā uktam sūtre kathā doṣaḥ saṃkṣepeṇa navavidhaḥ ākulam saṃrabdham agamakam amitam anarthakam akālam asthiram apradīptam apravaddham ca ṣaṣṭham vāda niḥsaraṇam guṇa doṣau vicārya vādāt niḥsarati akaraṇena vā prativāditya bhājana tām parṣadaḥ  vaiguṇyam ātmanaḥ  akauśalyam ca jñātvā vādam na karoti prativādini bhājana tām parṣadaḥ  guṇavat tvam ātmanaḥ kauśalyam ca jñātvā vādam karoti vāde bahu karā dharmāḥ samāsatas trayaḥ sva para samaya jña tā yayā sarvatra nipuṇaḥ  vādam karoti vaiśāradyam yena nipuṇaḥ samagra parṣadi vādam karoti pratimānam yena nipuṇaḥ sarvān   kaṭhinān praśnān vyākaroti api khalu sva hita sukha kāmena vādeṣu abhijñātum pravarttitavyam na paraiḥ vivādam kartum tad uktam bhagavatā mahāyānā bhidharmasutre bodhisattvena vīryam ārabhamāṇena kuśala pakṣa prayuktena pratipatti sārakeṇa dharma anudharma cāriṇā sarva sattva saṃgrāhakeṇa kṣipram anuttarām samyak  saṃbodhim abhisaṃbudhyatā dvādaśa sthāna dharmān samanupaśyatā na paraiḥ saha vivādaḥ kāryaḥ katame dvādaśa anuttara artha parama dharma deśanāyām saṃpratyayaḥ  durlabhaḥ prāśnikānām avavāda grāhakam cittam durlabham sabhyā guṇa doṣa vicārakāḥ ca durlabhā vāde prayuktānām ṣaṣ doṣa virahaḥ  durlabhaḥ katame ṣaḍ  asat pakṣa bhiniveśa doṣaḥ kusṛti vacana doṣaḥ akālika vāk karaṇa doṣaḥ kathā āsāda doṣaḥ pārupi avacata doṣaḥ citta āghāta doṣaḥ ca vāde saṃrambha abhāva u durlabhaḥ vāde para citta anurakṣaṇam durlabham vāde anurakṣaṇe api citta samādhi durlabhaḥ vāde cittasya nika arsa para utkarṣa kāma tā durlabhā nikarṣa para utkarṣayoḥ api cittasya asaṃkleśaḥ  durlabhaḥ saṃkliṣṭe tu citte sparśa vihāraḥ  durlabhaḥ asparśa vihāre tu kuśala dharma bhāvanā durlabhā nirantaram kuśala dharme abhāvite tu asama ahicittasya kṣipram samādhi lābhaḥ samāhita cittasya vā kṣipram vimokṣa lābhaḥ  durlabhaḥ abhisandhi viniścayaḥ katamaḥ uktāt anyaḥ  arthaḥ nāma pada vyañjana kāyānām channasya abhisandheḥ anya artha abhivyañjane vipariṇāmaḥ yathā uktam sūtre mātaram pitaram hatvā rājānam dvau bahu śrutau rāṣṭram sa anucaram hatvā naraḥ  viśuddha ucyate apicā uktam sūtre aśraddhaḥ  akṛtajñaḥ ca sandhi  chedī ca yaḥ  naraḥ hata avakāśaḥ  vāntāśaḥ sa vai uttama puruṣaḥ punar ca uktam sūtre asāre sāra matayaḥ  viparyāse ca susthitāḥ kleśena ca su saṃkliṣṭā labhante bodhim uttamām api ca uktam sūtre bodhisattvaḥ  mahāsattvaḥ pañcabhiḥ dharmaiḥ samanvāgataḥ  dāna pāra mitāyām kṣipram paripūrim labhate katame pañca mātsarya dharma tām anuvṛṃhayati dānena ca parikhidyate yācanakam ca dveṣṭi na kiṃcid  kadācid  dadāti dūre ca bhavati dānasya punar ca uktam sūtre bodhisattvaḥ  mahāsattvaḥ pañca dharma samanvāgataḥ  brahmacārī bhavati parameṇa viśuddhena brahmacaryeṇa samanvāgataḥ katame pañca na anyatra maithunyāt maithunasya niḥsaraṇam paryeṣate maithuna prahāṇena upekṣakaḥ  bhavati utpannam ca maithuna rogam adhivāsayati maithuna pratipakṣeṇa ca dharmeṇa uttrasyati abhīkṣṇam ca dvaya dvayam samāpadyate kim upādāya idam śāstram abhidharma samuccaya iti nāma labhate saṃkṣepataḥ tribhiḥ arthaiḥ sametya uccayatām upādāya samantāt uccaya tām upādāya samyak uccayatām ca upādāya
